  <div class="p-summary" data-fill-with="abstract">
   <h2 class="no-num no-toc no-ref heading settled" id="abstract"><span class="content">Abstract</span></h2>
   <p>Converting CSSOM value strings into meaningfully typed JavaScript representations and back can incur a significant performance overhead. This specification exposes CSS values as typed JavaScript objects to facilitate their performant manipulation.</p>
  </div>
  <h2 class="no-num no-toc no-ref heading settled" id="status"><span class="content">Status of this document</span></h2>
  <div data-fill-with="status">
   <p> <em>This section describes the status of this document at the time of
  its publication. Other documents may supersede this document. A list of
  current W3C publications and the latest revision of this technical report
  can be found in the <a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/">W3C technical reports
  index at https://www.w3.org/TR/.</a></em> </p>
   <p> Publication as a Working Draft does not imply endorsement by the W3C
  Membership. This is a draft document and may be updated, replaced or
  obsoleted by other documents at any time. It is inappropriate to cite this
  document as other than work in progress. </p>
   <p> <a href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues">GitHub Issues</a> are preferred for discussion of this specification.
  When filing an issue, please put the text “css-typed-om” in the title,
  preferably like this:
  “[css-typed-om] <i>…summary of comment…</i>”.
  All issues and comments are <a href="https://lists.w3.org/Archives/Public/public-houdini-archive/">archived</a>. </p>
   <p> This document was published by the <a href="https://www.w3.org/Style/CSS/members">CSS Working Group</a> and the <a href="https://www.w3.org/2001/tag/">Technical Architecture Group</a>. </p>

    operating under the <a href="https://www.w3.org/Consortium/Patent-Policy-20040205/">5 February 2004 W3C Patent Policy</a>.
    W3C maintains a <a href="https://www.w3.org/2004/01/pp-impl/32061/status" rel="disclosure">public list of any patent disclosures (CSS)</a> and a <a href="https://www.w3.org/2001/tag/disclosures" rel="disclosure">public list of any patent disclosures (Technical Architecture Group)</a> made in connection with the deliverables of each group;
    these pages also include instructions for disclosing a patent.
    An individual who has actual knowledge of a patent
    which the individual believes contains <a href="https://www.w3.org/Consortium/Patent-Policy-20040205/#def-essential">Essential Claim(s)</a> must disclose the information
    in accordance with <a href="https://www.w3.org/Consortium/Patent-Policy-20040205/#sec-Disclosure">section 6 of the W3C Patent Policy</a>. </p>

  <main>
   <h2 class="heading settled" data-level="1" id="intro"><span class="secno">1. </span><span class="content">Introduction</span><a class="self-link" href="#intro"></a></h2>
   <p>Converting CSSOM value strings into meaningfully typed JavaScript representations and
back can incur a significant performance overhead. This specification exposes CSS values
as typed JavaScript objects to facilitate their performant manipulation.</p>
   <p>The API exposed by this specification is designed for performance rather than ergonomics.
Some particular considerations:</p>
   <ul>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>retrieved JavaScript representations of CSS values are not mutable - instead updates
    must explicitly be set using the API.</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>objects are organized for consistency rather than ease of access. For example, even
    though lengths are often numeric pixel values, a declared <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-1">CSSNumericValue</a></code> can’t be
    treated as a number without first explicitly casting it to a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-1">CSSUnitValue</a></code>, as calc
    expressions and keywords are also valid lengths.</p>
   </ul>
   <h2 class="heading settled" data-level="2" id="stylevalue-objects"><span class="secno">2. </span><span class="content"><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-1">CSSStyleValue</a></code> objects</span><a class="self-link" href="#stylevalue-objects"></a></h2>
<pre class="idl highlight def"><span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="cssstylevalue"><code>CSSStyleValue</code></dfn> {
    <dfn class="kt dfn-paneled" data-dfn-for="CSSStyleValue" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-lt="stringification behavior" data-noexport="" id="CSSStyleValue-stringification-behavior">stringifier</dfn>;
    <span class="kt">static</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-2">CSSStyleValue</a>? <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="method" href="#dom-cssstylevalue-parse" id="ref-for-dom-cssstylevalue-parse-1">parse</a>(<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSStyleValue/parse(property, cssText)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssstylevalue-parse-property-csstext-property"><code>property</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssstylevalue-parse-property-csstext-property"></a></dfn>, <a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSStyleValue/parse(property, cssText)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssstylevalue-parse-property-csstext-csstext"><code>cssText</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssstylevalue-parse-property-csstext-csstext"></a></dfn>);
    <span class="kt">static</span> <span class="kt">sequence</span>&lt;<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-3">CSSStyleValue</a>>? <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="method" href="#dom-cssstylevalue-parseall" id="ref-for-dom-cssstylevalue-parseall-1">parseAll</a>(<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSStyleValue/parseAll(property, cssText)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssstylevalue-parseall-property-csstext-property"><code>property</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssstylevalue-parseall-property-csstext-property"></a></dfn>, <a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSStyleValue/parseAll(property, cssText)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssstylevalue-parseall-property-csstext-csstext"><code>cssText</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssstylevalue-parseall-property-csstext-csstext"></a></dfn>);
};
</pre>
   <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-4">CSSStyleValue</a></code> objects are the base class of all CSS Values accessible via the Typed OM API.
Values that can’t yet be directly supported by a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-5">CSSStyleValue</a></code> subclass
are also represented as <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-6">CSSStyleValue</a></code> objects.</p>
   <p>The <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#CSSStyleValue-stringification-behavior" id="ref-for-CSSStyleValue-stringification-behavior-1">stringification behavior</a> of <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-7">CSSStyleValue</a></code> objects is to
return a normalized representation
(see <a href="#stylevalue-normalization">§5 CSSStyleValue normalization</a>)
of the value the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-8">CSSStyleValue</a></code> object represents.</p>
   <p>The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSStyleValue" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" data-lt="parse(property, cssText)" id="dom-cssstylevalue-parse"><code>parse(DOMString <var>property</var>, DOMString <var>cssText</var>)</code></dfn>,
when invoked, must <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#parse-a-cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-parse-a-cssstylevalue-1">parse a CSSStyleValue</a> with property <var>property</var>, cssText <var>cssText</var>,
and parseMultiple set to false.</p>
   <p>The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSStyleValue" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" data-lt="parseAll(property, cssText)" id="dom-cssstylevalue-parseall"><code>parseAll(DOMString <var>property</var>, DOMString <var>cssText</var>)</code></dfn>,
when invoked, must <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#parse-a-cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-parse-a-cssstylevalue-2">parse a CSSStyleValue</a> with property <var>property</var>, cssText <var>cssText</var>,
and parseMultiple set to true.</p>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="parse a CSSStyleValue">
     To <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-noexport="" id="parse-a-cssstylevalue">parse a CSSStyleValue</dfn> given a <var>property</var>, <var>cssText</var>, and a <var>parseMultiple</var> flag, run these steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Attempt to parse <var>property</var> as an <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#typedef-ident">&lt;ident></a>.
If this fails, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#syntaxerror">SyntaxError</a></code> and exit this algorithm.
Otherwise, let <var>property</var> be the parsed result.
If <var>property</var> does not start with two dashes (U+002D HYPHEN),
let <var>property</var> be <var>property</var> <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#ascii-lowercase">ASCII lowercased</a>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>property</var> is not a <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-supported-property-names">supported property name</a>, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code> and exit this algorithm.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Attempt to <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-syntax-3/#css-parse-something-according-to-a-css-grammar">parse</a> <var>cssText</var> according to <var>property</var>’s grammar.
If this fails, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#syntaxerror">SyntaxError</a></code> and exit this algorithm.
Otherwise,
let <var>value</var> be the parsed result.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>property</var> is a <a data-link-type="dfn">list-valued property</a>, and <var>parseMultiple</var> is true,
subdivide <var>value</var> into a list of <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-9">CSSStyleValue</a></code> objects,
each representing one <a data-link-type="dfn">list-valued property iteration</a>,
and let <var>value</var> be the result. Return <var>value</var> as a sequence of <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-10">CSSStyleValue</a></code> objects.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>property</var> is a <a data-link-type="dfn">list-valued property</a>, and <var>parseMultiple</var> is false
subdivide <var>value</var> into a list of <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-11">CSSStyleValue</a></code> objects,
each representing one <a data-link-type="dfn">list-valued property iteration</a>,
and let <var>value</var> be the first entry in this list.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>return a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-12">CSSStyleValue</a></code> representing <var>value</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="issue no-marker" id="issue-14d5b436"><a class="self-link" href="#issue-14d5b436"></a><a class="marker" href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues/305" style="text-transform:none">w3c/css-houdini-drafts/305</a><a href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues/305">When doing CSSStyleValue.parse(), what should throw vs return null?</a></div>
   <h2 class="heading settled" data-level="3" id="the-stylepropertymap"><span class="secno">3. </span><span class="content">The <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#stylepropertymap" id="ref-for-stylepropertymap-1">StylePropertyMap</a></code></span><a class="self-link" href="#the-stylepropertymap"></a></h2>
<pre class="idl highlight def"><span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="stylepropertymapreadonly"><code>StylePropertyMapReadOnly</code></dfn> {
    <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-13">CSSStyleValue</a>? <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="StylePropertyMapReadOnly" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" data-lt="get(property)" id="dom-stylepropertymapreadonly-get"><code>get</code></dfn>(<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="StylePropertyMapReadOnly/get(property)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-stylepropertymapreadonly-get-property-property"><code>property</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-stylepropertymapreadonly-get-property-property"></a></dfn>);
    <span class="kt">sequence</span>&lt;<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-14">CSSStyleValue</a>> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="StylePropertyMapReadOnly" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" data-lt="getAll(property)" id="dom-stylepropertymapreadonly-getall"><code>getAll</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-stylepropertymapreadonly-getall"></a></dfn>(<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="StylePropertyMapReadOnly/getAll(property)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-stylepropertymapreadonly-getall-property-property"><code>property</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-stylepropertymapreadonly-getall-property-property"></a></dfn>);
    <a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-boolean"><span class="kt">boolean</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="StylePropertyMapReadOnly" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" data-lt="has(property)" id="dom-stylepropertymapreadonly-has"><code>has</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-stylepropertymapreadonly-has"></a></dfn>(<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="StylePropertyMapReadOnly/has(property)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-stylepropertymapreadonly-has-property-property"><code>property</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-stylepropertymapreadonly-has-property-property"></a></dfn>);
    <span class="kt">iterable</span>&lt;<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a>, (<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-15">CSSStyleValue</a> <span class="kt">or</span> <span class="kt">sequence</span>&lt;<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-16">CSSStyleValue</a>>)>;
    <span class="kt">sequence</span>&lt;<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a>> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="StylePropertyMapReadOnly" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" data-lt="getProperties()" id="dom-stylepropertymapreadonly-getproperties"><code>getProperties</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-stylepropertymapreadonly-getproperties"></a></dfn>();
    <dfn class="kt" data-dfn-for="StylePropertyMapReadOnly" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-lt="stringification behavior" data-noexport="" id="StylePropertyMapReadOnly-stringification-behavior">stringifier<a class="self-link" href="#StylePropertyMapReadOnly-stringification-behavior"></a></dfn>;
};

<span class="kt">callback</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="callback" data-export="" id="callbackdef-updatefunction"><code>UpdateFunction</code></dfn> = <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-17">CSSStyleValue</a> (<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-18">CSSStyleValue</a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="UpdateFunction" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-updatefunction-oldvalue"><code>oldValue</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-updatefunction-oldvalue"></a></dfn>);

<span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="stylepropertymap"><code>StylePropertyMap</code></dfn> : <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#stylepropertymapreadonly" id="ref-for-stylepropertymapreadonly-1">StylePropertyMapReadOnly</a> {
    <span class="kt">void</span> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="StylePropertyMap" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" data-lt="append(property, ...values)|append(property)" id="dom-stylepropertymap-append"><code>append</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-stylepropertymap-append"></a></dfn>(<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="StylePropertyMap/append(property, ...values)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-stylepropertymap-append-property-values-property"><code>property</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-stylepropertymap-append-property-values-property"></a></dfn>, (<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-19">CSSStyleValue</a> <span class="kt">or</span> <a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a>)... <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="StylePropertyMap/append(property, ...values)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-stylepropertymap-append-property-values-values"><code>values</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-stylepropertymap-append-property-values-values"></a></dfn>);
    <span class="kt">void</span> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="StylePropertyMap" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" data-lt="delete(property)" id="dom-stylepropertymap-delete"><code>delete</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-stylepropertymap-delete"></a></dfn>(<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="StylePropertyMap/delete(property)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-stylepropertymap-delete-property-property"><code>property</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-stylepropertymap-delete-property-property"></a></dfn>);
    <span class="kt">void</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="StylePropertyMap" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" data-lt="set(property, ...values)|set(property)" id="dom-stylepropertymap-set"><code>set</code></dfn>(<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="StylePropertyMap/set(property, ...values)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-stylepropertymap-set-property-values-property"><code>property</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-stylepropertymap-set-property-values-property"></a></dfn>, (<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-20">CSSStyleValue</a> <span class="kt">or</span> <a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a>)... <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="StylePropertyMap/set(property, ...values)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-stylepropertymap-set-property-values-values"><code>values</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-stylepropertymap-set-property-values-values"></a></dfn>);
    <span class="kt">void</span> <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="method" href="#dom-stylepropertymap-update" id="ref-for-dom-stylepropertymap-update-1">update</a>(<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="StylePropertyMap/update(property, updateFunction)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-stylepropertymap-update-property-updatefunction-property"><code>property</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-stylepropertymap-update-property-updatefunction-property"></a></dfn>, <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#callbackdef-updatefunction" id="ref-for-callbackdef-updatefunction-1">UpdateFunction</a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="StylePropertyMap/update(property, updateFunction)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-stylepropertymap-update-property-updatefunction-updatefunction"><code>updateFunction</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-stylepropertymap-update-property-updatefunction-updatefunction"></a></dfn>);
};
</pre>
   <p>A <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#stylepropertymapreadonly" id="ref-for-stylepropertymapreadonly-2">StylePropertyMapReadOnly</a></code> object has an associated <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-noexport="" id="property-model">property model</dfn>,
which is a list of property - sequence&lt;<code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-21">CSSStyleValue</a></code>> pairs. This list
is initialized differently depending on where the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-22">CSSStyleValue</a></code> is used
(see <a href="#computed-stylepropertymapreadonly-objects">§3.1 Computed StylePropertyMapReadOnly objects</a>, <a href="#declared-stylepropertymap-objects">§3.2 Declared StylePropertyMap objects</a>, and <a href="#inline-stylepropertymap-objects">§3.3 Inline StylePropertyMap objects</a>).</p>
   <div class="note" role="note">
     The sequence of <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-23">CSSStyleValue</a></code>s associated with a property do
not represent multiple successive definitions of that property’s value.
Instead, sequences represent values associated with list-valued properties. 
    <p>This approach allows single-valued properties to become list-valued in the
future without breaking code that relies on calling <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-stylepropertymapreadonly-get" id="ref-for-dom-stylepropertymapreadonly-get-1">get()</a></code> and/or <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-stylepropertymap-set" id="ref-for-dom-stylepropertymap-set-1">set()</a></code> for those properties.</p>
   </div>
   <p>The <dfn class="idl-code" data-dfn-for="StylePropertyMap" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" data-lt="append(DOMString property, (CSSStyleValue or DOMString)... values)" id="dom-stylepropertymap-append-domstring-property-cssstylevalue-or-domstring-values"><code>append(DOMString <var>property</var>,
(CSSStyleValue or DOMString)... <var>values</var>)</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-stylepropertymap-append-domstring-property-cssstylevalue-or-domstring-values"></a></dfn> method, when invoked, must <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#append-to-a-stylepropertymap" id="ref-for-append-to-a-stylepropertymap-1">append to a StylePropertyMap</a> with property <var>property</var> and values <var>values</var>.</p>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="append to a StylePropertyMap">
     To <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-noexport="" id="append-to-a-stylepropertymap">append to a StylePropertyMap</dfn> given a <var>property</var> and a list of <var>values</var>, run these steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>property</var> does not start with two dashes (U+002D HYPHEN),
let <var>property</var> be <var>property</var> <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#ascii-lowercase">ASCII lowercased</a>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>property</var> is not a <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-supported-property-names">supported property name</a>, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code> and exit this algorithm.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>property</var> is not a <a data-link-type="dfn">list-valued property</a>, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code> and exit this algorithm.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#stylepropertymap" id="ref-for-stylepropertymap-2">StylePropertyMap</a></code>’s <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#property-model" id="ref-for-property-model-1">property model</a> contains an entry for <var>property</var>,
let <var>entry</var> be that entry.
Otherwise, create a new entry for <var>property</var> with an empty list,
add it to the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#property-model" id="ref-for-property-model-2">property model</a>,
and let <var>entry</var> be the newly-created entry.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Let <var>values to append</var> be the empty list.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>For each <var>value</var> in <var>values</var> if the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#algorithm-that-coerces-value-into-an-appropriate-type-for-a-given-property" id="ref-for-algorithm-that-coerces-value-into-an-appropriate-type-for-a-given-property-1">algorithm that coerces value into an appropriate type for a given property</a> does not throw an error, append the returned object to <var>values to append</var>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Append <var>values to append</var> to the end of <var>entry</var>’s list.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="algorithm that coerces value into an appropriate type for a given property">
     This section describes the <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-noexport="" id="algorithm-that-coerces-value-into-an-appropriate-type-for-a-given-property">algorithm that coerces value into an appropriate type for a given property</dfn>, or fails and throws a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code>: 
    <dl>
     <dt data-md="">If <var>value</var> is a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-24">CSSStyleValue</a></code>,
     <dd data-md="">
      <p>If <var>value</var> does not match the grammar of a <a data-link-type="dfn">list-valued property iteration</a> of <var>property</var>, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code> and exit this algorithm.
Otherwise, return the <var>value</var>.</p>
     <dt data-md="">If <var>value</var> is a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString">DOMString</a></code>,
     <dd data-md="">
      <p><a data-link-type="dfn" href="#parse-a-cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-parse-a-cssstylevalue-3">Parse a CSSStyleValue</a> with property <var>property</var> and value <var>value</var> and return the resulting <var>value</var>.
If the result is null, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code> and exit this algorithm.
Otherwise, append each <a data-link-type="dfn">list-valued property iteration</a> in the result to a <var>values to append</var> object
and return <var>values to append</var>.</p>
    </dl>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="get a value from a StylePropertyMap">
     To <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-noexport="" id="get-a-value-from-a-stylepropertymap">get a value from a StylePropertyMap</dfn>, run these steps: 
    <div class="issue no-marker" id="issue-9acd40f1"><a class="self-link" href="#issue-9acd40f1"></a><a class="marker" href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues/148" style="text-transform:none">w3c/css-houdini-drafts/148</a><a href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues/148">[css-typed-om] add detailed descriptions of the rest of the methods on StylePropertyMap</a></div>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="set a value on a StylePropertyMap">
     To <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-noexport="" id="set-a-value-on-a-stylepropertymap">set a value on a StylePropertyMap</dfn>, run these steps: 
    <div class="issue no-marker" id="issue-9acd40f10"><a class="self-link" href="#issue-9acd40f10"></a><a class="marker" href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues/148" style="text-transform:none">w3c/css-houdini-drafts/148</a><a href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues/148">[css-typed-om] add detailed descriptions of the rest of the methods on StylePropertyMap</a></div>
   </div>
   <p>The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="StylePropertyMap" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" data-lt="update(property, updateFunction)" id="dom-stylepropertymap-update"><code>update(DOMString <var>property</var>,
UpdateFunction <var>updateFunction</var>)</code></dfn> method, when invoked, must <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#update-a-value-in-a-stylepropertymap" id="ref-for-update-a-value-in-a-stylepropertymap-1">update a value in a StylePropertyMap</a> with property name <var>property</var>, update function <var>updateFunction</var>, and property
map set to the object this method was invoked on .</p>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="update a value in a StylePropertyMap">
     To <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-noexport="" id="update-a-value-in-a-stylepropertymap">update a value in a StylePropertyMap</dfn> given a <var>property
    name</var>, <var>update function</var>, and <var>property map</var>, run these
    steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Let <var>old value</var> be the result of running the algorithm to <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#get-a-value-from-a-stylepropertymap" id="ref-for-get-a-value-from-a-stylepropertymap-1">get a value from a StylePropertyMap</a> with property name <var>property
name</var> and property map <var>property map</var>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Let <var>new value</var> be the return value given by <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#invoke-a-callback-function">invoking</a> the callback <var>update function</var> with a single input of <var>old value</var>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Run the algorithm to <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#set-a-value-on-a-stylepropertymap" id="ref-for-set-a-value-on-a-stylepropertymap-1">set a value on a StylePropertyMap</a> with property name <var>property name</var>,
value <var>new value</var>, and property map <var>property map</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <p>The <dfn class="idl-code" data-dfn-for="StylePropertyMap" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" id="dom-stylepropertymap-getproperties"><code>getProperties()</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-stylepropertymap-getproperties"></a></dfn> method returns all of the properties listed in
the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#property-model" id="ref-for-property-model-3">property model</a>. This list of properties is sorted in the following manner:</p>
   <ul>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>normal properties are sorted alphabetically.</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>custom properties are sorted by increasing code point order.</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>custom properties are sorted after normal properties.</p>
   </ul>
   <p><a data-link-type="dfn" href="#computed-stylepropertymap" id="ref-for-computed-stylepropertymap-1">computed StylePropertyMap</a>, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#declared-stylepropertymap" id="ref-for-declared-stylepropertymap-1">declared StylePropertyMap</a> and <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#inline-stylepropertymap" id="ref-for-inline-stylepropertymap-1">inline StylePropertyMap</a> are all live objects: the attributes and methods on these objects must operate on the actual underlying data, not a snapshot of the data.</p>
   <div class="issue no-marker" id="issue-4510b51a"><a class="self-link" href="#issue-4510b51a"></a><a class="marker" href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues/148" style="text-transform:none">w3c/css-houdini-drafts/148</a><a href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues/148">[css-typed-om] add detailed descriptions of the rest of the methods on StylePropertyMap</a></div>
   <div class="issue no-marker" id="issue-51d93ecd"><a class="self-link" href="#issue-51d93ecd"></a><a class="marker" href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues/268" style="text-transform:none">w3c/css-houdini-drafts/268</a><a href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues/268">[css-typed-om] Stringification behavior</a></div>
   <div class="issue no-marker" id="issue-c98669fe"><a class="self-link" href="#issue-c98669fe"></a><a class="marker" href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues/276" style="text-transform:none">w3c/css-houdini-drafts/276</a><a href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues/276">[css-typed-om] Describe how the StylePropertyMaps should interact with custom properties</a></div>
   <div class="issue no-marker" id="issue-ffbd95fd"><a class="self-link" href="#issue-ffbd95fd"></a><a class="marker" href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues/309" style="text-transform:none">w3c/css-houdini-drafts/309</a><a href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues/309">[css-typed-om] Should StyleMap be case sensitive?</a></div>
   <div class="issue no-marker" id="issue-d2a7ccbe"><a class="self-link" href="#issue-d2a7ccbe"></a><a class="marker" href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues/310" style="text-transform:none">w3c/css-houdini-drafts/310</a><a href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues/310">[css-typed-om]  Consider using properties in addition to .get/.set</a></div>
   <h3 class="heading settled" data-level="3.1" id="computed-stylepropertymapreadonly-objects"><span class="secno">3.1. </span><span class="content">Computed <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#stylepropertymapreadonly" id="ref-for-stylepropertymapreadonly-3">StylePropertyMapReadOnly</a></code> objects</span><a class="self-link" href="#computed-stylepropertymapreadonly-objects"></a></h3>
<pre class="idl highlight def"><span class="kt">partial</span> <span class="kt">interface</span> <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/window-object.html#window">Window</a> {
    <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#stylepropertymapreadonly" id="ref-for-stylepropertymapreadonly-4">StylePropertyMapReadOnly</a> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="Window" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" data-lt="getComputedStyleMap(element, pseudoElt)|getComputedStyleMap(element)" id="dom-window-getcomputedstylemap"><code>getComputedStyleMap</code></dfn>(<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#element">Element</a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="Window/getComputedStyleMap(element, pseudoElt), Window/getComputedStyleMap(element)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-window-getcomputedstylemap-element-pseudoelt-element"><code>element</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-window-getcomputedstylemap-element-pseudoelt-element"></a></dfn>, <span class="kt">optional</span> <a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a>? <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="Window/getComputedStyleMap(element, pseudoElt), Window/getComputedStyleMap(element)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-window-getcomputedstylemap-element-pseudoelt-pseudoelt"><code>pseudoElt</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-window-getcomputedstylemap-element-pseudoelt-pseudoelt"></a></dfn>);
};
</pre>
   <div class="issue no-marker" id="issue-c510b0ad"><a class="self-link" href="#issue-c510b0ad"></a><a class="marker" href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues/350" style="text-transform:none">w3c/css-houdini-drafts/350</a><a href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues/350">[all] Move Houdini APIs to `window.CSS`</a></div>
   <p><dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-noexport="" id="computed-stylepropertymap">Computed StylePropertyMap</dfn> objects represent the computed style of an <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#element">Element</a></code> or pseudo element, and are accessed by calling the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-window-getcomputedstylemap" id="ref-for-dom-window-getcomputedstylemap-1">getComputedStyleMap()</a></code> method.</p>
   <p>When constructed, the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#property-model" id="ref-for-property-model-4">property model</a> for <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#computed-stylepropertymap" id="ref-for-computed-stylepropertymap-2">computed StylePropertyMap</a> objects is initialized to contain an entry for every valid CSS property supported by the User Agent.</p>
   <p class="note" role="note"><span>Note:</span> The StylePropertyMap returned by getComputedStyleMap represents computed style,
            not resolved style. In this regard it provides different values than those
            in objects returned by getComputedStyle.</p>
   <h3 class="heading settled" data-level="3.2" id="declared-stylepropertymap-objects"><span class="secno">3.2. </span><span class="content">Declared <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#stylepropertymap" id="ref-for-stylepropertymap-3">StylePropertyMap</a></code> objects</span><a class="self-link" href="#declared-stylepropertymap-objects"></a></h3>
<pre class="idl highlight def"><span class="kt">partial</span> <span class="kt">interface</span> <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/cssom-1/#cssstylerule">CSSStyleRule</a> {
    [<a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="extended-attribute" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#SameObject">SameObject</a>] <span class="kt">readonly</span> <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#stylepropertymap" id="ref-for-stylepropertymap-4">StylePropertyMap</a> <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="attribute" data-readonly="" data-type="StylePropertyMap" href="#dom-cssstylerule-stylemap" id="ref-for-dom-cssstylerule-stylemap-1">styleMap</a>;
};
</pre>
   <p><dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-noexport="" id="declared-stylepropertymap">Declared StylePropertyMap</dfn> objects represent style property-value pairs embedded
in a style rule, and are accessed via the <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSStyleRule" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" id="dom-cssstylerule-stylemap"><code>styleMap</code></dfn> attribute of <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/cssom-1/#cssstylerule">CSSStyleRule</a></code> objects.</p>
   <p>When constructed, the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#property-model" id="ref-for-property-model-5">property model</a> for <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#declared-stylepropertymap" id="ref-for-declared-stylepropertymap-2">declared StylePropertyMap</a> objects is initialized to contain
an entry for each property that is paired with at least one valid value inside the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/cssom-1/#cssstylerule">CSSStyleRule</a></code> that the object represents. The value for a given property is
the last valid value provided by the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/cssom-1/#cssstylerule">CSSStyleRule</a></code> object.</p>
   <h3 class="heading settled" data-level="3.3" id="inline-stylepropertymap-objects"><span class="secno">3.3. </span><span class="content">Inline <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#stylepropertymap" id="ref-for-stylepropertymap-5">StylePropertyMap</a></code> objects</span><a class="self-link" href="#inline-stylepropertymap-objects"></a></h3>
<pre class="idl highlight def"><span class="kt">partial</span> <span class="kt">interface</span> <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#element">Element</a> {
    [<a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="extended-attribute" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#SameObject">SameObject</a>] <span class="kt">readonly</span> <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#stylepropertymap" id="ref-for-stylepropertymap-6">StylePropertyMap</a> <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="attribute" data-readonly="" data-type="StylePropertyMap" href="#dom-element-stylemap" id="ref-for-dom-element-stylemap-1">styleMap</a>;
};
</pre>
   <p><dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-noexport="" id="inline-stylepropertymap">Inline StylePropertyMap</dfn> objects represent inline style declarations attached
directly to <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#element">Element</a></code>s. They are accessed via the <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="Element" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" id="dom-element-stylemap"><code>styleMap</code></dfn> attribute of <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#element">Element</a></code> objects.</p>
   <p>When constructed, the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#property-model" id="ref-for-property-model-6">property model</a> for <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#inline-stylepropertymap" id="ref-for-inline-stylepropertymap-2">inline StylePropertyMap</a> objects
is initialized to contain an
entry for each property that is paired with at least one valid value in the string
representing the style attribute for the Element that the object is associated with.
The value for a given property is the last valid value provided in the string.</p>
   <h2 class="heading settled" data-level="4" id="stylevalue-subclasses"><span class="secno">4. </span><span class="content"><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-25">CSSStyleValue</a></code> subclasses</span><a class="self-link" href="#stylevalue-subclasses"></a></h2>
   <h3 class="heading settled" data-level="4.1" id="unparsedvalue-objects"><span class="secno">4.1. </span><span class="content"><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunparsedvalue" id="ref-for-cssunparsedvalue-1">CSSUnparsedValue</a></code> objects</span><a class="self-link" href="#unparsedvalue-objects"></a></h3>
<pre class="idl highlight def">[<dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSUnparsedValue" data-dfn-type="constructor" data-export="" data-lt="CSSUnparsedValue(members)|CSSUnparsedValue()" id="dom-cssunparsedvalue-cssunparsedvalue"><code>Constructor</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssunparsedvalue-cssunparsedvalue"></a></dfn>((<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a> <span class="kt">or</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssvariablereferencevalue" id="ref-for-cssvariablereferencevalue-1">CSSVariableReferenceValue</a>)... <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSUnparsedValue/CSSUnparsedValue(members)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssunparsedvalue-cssunparsedvalue-members-members"><code>members</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssunparsedvalue-cssunparsedvalue-members-members"></a></dfn>)]
<span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="cssunparsedvalue"><code>CSSUnparsedValue</code></dfn> : <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-26">CSSStyleValue</a> {
    <span class="kt">iterable</span>&lt;(<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a> <span class="kt">or</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssvariablereferencevalue" id="ref-for-cssvariablereferencevalue-2">CSSVariableReferenceValue</a>)>;
    <span class="kt">readonly</span> <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-unsigned-long"><span class="kt">unsigned</span> <span class="kt">long</span></a> <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="attribute" data-readonly="" data-type="unsigned long" href="#dom-cssunparsedvalue-length" id="ref-for-dom-cssunparsedvalue-length-1">length</a>;
    <span class="kt">getter</span> (<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a> <span class="kt">or</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssvariablereferencevalue" id="ref-for-cssvariablereferencevalue-3">CSSVariableReferenceValue</a>) (<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-unsigned-long"><span class="kt">unsigned</span> <span class="kt">long</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSUnparsedValue/__getter__(index)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssunparsedvalue-__getter__-index-index"><code>index</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssunparsedvalue-__getter__-index-index"></a></dfn>);
};

<span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="cssvariablereferencevalue"><code>CSSVariableReferenceValue</code></dfn> {
    <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSVariableReferenceValue" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" data-type="DOMString" id="dom-cssvariablereferencevalue-variable"><code>variable</code></dfn>;
    <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssunparsedvalue" id="ref-for-cssunparsedvalue-2">CSSUnparsedValue</a>? <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSVariableReferenceValue" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" data-type="CSSUnparsedValue?" id="dom-cssvariablereferencevalue-fallback"><code>fallback</code></dfn>;
};
</pre>
   <div class="issue no-marker" id="issue-be6f6723"><a class="self-link" href="#issue-be6f6723"></a><a class="marker" href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues/239" style="text-transform:none">w3c/css-houdini-drafts/239</a><a href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues/239">[css-typed-om]: There's no nice way to represent CSSUnparsedValue as a "list-plus" style object.</a></div>
   <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunparsedvalue" id="ref-for-cssunparsedvalue-3">CSSUnparsedValue</a></code> objects represent values that reference custom properties.
They represent a list of string fragments and variable references.</p>
   <p>They have a <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSUnparsedValue" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" id="dom-cssunparsedvalue-tokens-slot"><code>[[tokens]]</code></dfn> internal slot,
which is a <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list">list</a> of alternating <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString">DOMString</a></code> and <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssvariablereferencevalue" id="ref-for-cssvariablereferencevalue-4">CSSVariableReferenceValue</a></code> objects.
This list is the object’s <a data-link-type="dfn">values to iterate over</a>.</p>
   <p>The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSUnparsedValue" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" id="dom-cssunparsedvalue-length"><code>length</code></dfn> attribute indicates how many string fragments and variable references are contained within the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunparsedvalue" id="ref-for-cssunparsedvalue-4">CSSUnparsedValue</a></code>.</p>
   <p>The <dfn data-dfn-for="CSSUnparsedValue" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-noexport="" id="cssunparsedvalue-indexed-getter">indexed getter<a class="self-link" href="#cssunparsedvalue-indexed-getter"></a></dfn> retrieves the string fragment or variable reference at the provided index.</p>
   <h3 class="heading settled" data-level="4.2" id="keywordvalue-objects"><span class="secno">4.2. </span><span class="content"><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csskeywordvalue" id="ref-for-csskeywordvalue-1">CSSKeywordValue</a></code> objects</span><a class="self-link" href="#keywordvalue-objects"></a></h3>
   <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csskeywordvalue" id="ref-for-csskeywordvalue-2">CSSKeywordValue</a></code> objects represent CSS keywords and other <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-syntax-3/#identifier">identifiers</a>.</p>
<pre class="idl highlight def">[<a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="constructor" href="#dom-csskeywordvalue-csskeywordvalue" id="ref-for-dom-csskeywordvalue-csskeywordvalue-1">Constructor</a>(<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSKeywordValue/CSSKeywordValue(value)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-csskeywordvalue-csskeywordvalue-value-value"><code>value</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-csskeywordvalue-csskeywordvalue-value-value"></a></dfn>)]
<span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="csskeywordvalue"><code>CSSKeywordValue</code></dfn> : <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-27">CSSStyleValue</a> {
    <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSKeywordValue" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" data-type="DOMString" id="dom-csskeywordvalue-value"><code>value</code></dfn>;
    <a class="kt" data-link-type="dfn" href="#csskeywordvalue-stringification-behavior" id="ref-for-csskeywordvalue-stringification-behavior-1">stringifier</a>;
};
</pre>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSKeywordValue(|value|)">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSKeywordValue" data-dfn-type="constructor" data-export="" id="dom-csskeywordvalue-csskeywordvalue"><code>CSSKeywordValue(<var>value</var>)</code></dfn> constructor must,
    when called,
    perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csskeywordvalue" id="ref-for-csskeywordvalue-3">CSSKeywordValue</a></code> with its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csskeywordvalue-value" id="ref-for-dom-csskeywordvalue-value-1">value</a></code> internal slot
set to <var>value</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSKeywordValue stringification behavior">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-for="CSSKeywordValue" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-noexport="" id="csskeywordvalue-stringification-behavior">stringification behavior</dfn> of a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csskeywordvalue" id="ref-for-csskeywordvalue-4">CSSKeywordValue</a></code> <var>this</var> is: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Let <var>token</var> be an <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-syntax-3/#typedef-ident-token">&lt;ident-token></a> with its value set to <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csskeywordvalue-value" id="ref-for-dom-csskeywordvalue-value-2">value</a></code> internal slot.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return the serialization of <var>token</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <p>Any place that accepts a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csskeywordvalue" id="ref-for-csskeywordvalue-5">CSSKeywordValue</a></code> also accepts a raw <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString">DOMString</a></code>,
by using the following typedef and algorithm:</p>
<pre class="idl highlight def"><span class="kt">typedef</span> (<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a> <span class="kt">or</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#csskeywordvalue" id="ref-for-csskeywordvalue-6">CSSKeywordValue</a>) <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-type="typedef" data-export="" id="typedefdef-csskeywordish"><code>CSSKeywordish</code><a class="self-link" href="#typedefdef-csskeywordish"></a></dfn>;
</pre>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="rectify a keywordish value">
     To <dfn data-dfn-type="dfn" data-export="" id="rectify-a-keywordish-value">rectify a keywordish value<a class="self-link" href="#rectify-a-keywordish-value"></a></dfn> <var>val</var>,
    perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>val</var> is a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csskeywordvalue" id="ref-for-csskeywordvalue-7">CSSKeywordValue</a></code>,
return <var>val</var>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>val</var> is a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString">DOMString</a></code>,
return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csskeywordvalue" id="ref-for-csskeywordvalue-8">CSSKeywordValue</a></code> with its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csskeywordvalue-value" id="ref-for-dom-csskeywordvalue-value-3">value</a></code> internal slot
set to <var>val</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <h3 class="heading settled" data-level="4.3" id="numeric-objects"><span class="secno">4.3. </span><span class="content">Numeric Values:</span><a class="self-link" href="#numeric-objects"></a></h3>
   <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-2">CSSNumericValue</a></code> objects represent CSS values that are numeric in nature
(<a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#number-value">&lt;number></a>s, <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#percentage-value">&lt;percentage></a>s, <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#typedef-dimension">&lt;dimension></a>s).</p>
   <ul>
    <li data-md="">
     <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-2">CSSUnitValue</a></code> objects represent values that contain a single unit type
(for example "42px").</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathvalue" id="ref-for-cssmathvalue-1">CSSMathValue</a></code> objects represent math expressions,
which can contain more than one value/unit
(for example "calc(56em + 10%)").</p>
   </ul>
   <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-3">CSSNumericValue</a></code> objects are not range-restricted.
Any valid numeric value can be represented by a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-4">CSSNumericValue</a></code>,
and that value will not be clamped, rounded, or rejected
when set on a <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#declared-stylepropertymap" id="ref-for-declared-stylepropertymap-3">declared StylePropertyMap</a> or <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#inline-stylepropertymap" id="ref-for-inline-stylepropertymap-3">inline StylePropertyMap</a>.
Instead, clamping and/or rounding will occur during computation of style.</p>
   <div class="example" id="example-3ed0ca8c">
    <a class="self-link" href="#example-3ed0ca8c"></a> The following code is valid 
<pre class="lang-js highlight">myElement<span class="p">.</span>styleMap<span class="p">.</span>set<span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">"opacity"</span><span class="p">,</span> CSS<span class="p">.</span>number<span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">3</span><span class="p">));</span>
myElement<span class="p">.</span>styleMap<span class="p">.</span>set<span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">"z-index"</span><span class="p">,</span> CSS<span class="p">.</span>number<span class="p">(</span><span class="mf">15.4</span><span class="p">));</span>

console<span class="p">.</span>log<span class="p">(</span>myElement<span class="p">.</span>styleMap<span class="p">.</span>get<span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">"opacity"</span><span class="p">).</span>value<span class="p">);</span> <span class="c1">// 3</span>
<span class="c1"></span>console<span class="p">.</span>log<span class="p">(</span>myElement<span class="p">.</span>styleMap<span class="p">.</span>get<span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">"z-index"</span><span class="p">).</span>value<span class="p">);</span> <span class="c1">// 15.4</span>
<span class="c1"></span>
<span class="kd">var</span> computedStyle <span class="o">=</span> getComputedStyleMap<span class="p">(</span>myElement<span class="p">);</span>
<span class="kd">var</span> opacity <span class="o">=</span> computedStyle<span class="p">.</span>get<span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">"opacity"</span><span class="p">);</span>
<span class="kd">var</span> zIndex <span class="o">=</span> computedStyle<span class="p">.</span>get<span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">"z-index"</span><span class="p">);</span>
</pre>
    <p>After execution, the value of <code>opacity</code> is <code>1</code> (<a class="property" data-link-type="propdesc" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-color-4/#propdef-opacity">opacity</a> is range-restricted),
    and the value of <code>zIndex</code> is <code>15</code> (<a class="property" data-link-type="propdesc" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-positioning/#propdef-z-index">z-index</a> is rounded to an integer value).</p>
   </div>
   <p class="note" role="note"><span>Note:</span> "Numeric values" which incorporate variable references
will instead be represented as <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunparsedvalue" id="ref-for-cssunparsedvalue-5">CSSUnparsedValue</a></code> objects,
and keywords as <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csskeywordvalue" id="ref-for-csskeywordvalue-9">CSSKeywordValue</a></code> objects.</p>
   <p>Any place that accepts a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-5">CSSNumericValue</a></code> also accepts a raw <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-double">double</a></code>,
by using the following typedef and algorithm:</p>
<pre class="idl highlight def"><span class="kt">typedef</span> (<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-double"><span class="kt">double</span></a> <span class="kt">or</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-6">CSSNumericValue</a>) <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="typedef" data-export="" id="typedefdef-cssnumberish"><code>CSSNumberish</code></dfn>;
</pre>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="rectify a numberish value">
     To <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-export="" data-lt="rectify a numberish value | rectifying a numberish value" id="rectify-a-numberish-value">rectify a numberish value</dfn> <var>num</var>,
    perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>num</var> is a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-7">CSSNumericValue</a></code>,
return <var>num</var>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>num</var> is a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-double">double</a></code>,
return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-3">CSSUnitValue</a></code> with its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-value-1">value</a></code> internal slot set to <var>num</var> and its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-unit" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-unit-1">unit</a></code> internal slot set to "number".</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <h4 class="heading settled" data-level="4.3.1" id="numeric-value"><span class="secno">4.3.1. </span><span class="content">Common Numeric Operations, and the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-8">CSSNumericValue</a></code> Superclass</span><a class="self-link" href="#numeric-value"></a></h4>
   <p>All numeric CSS values
(<a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#number-value">&lt;number></a>s, <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#percentage-value">&lt;percentage></a>s, and <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#typedef-dimension">&lt;dimension></a>s)
are represented by subclasses of the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-9">CSSNumericValue</a></code> interface.</p>
<pre class="idl highlight def"><span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="cssnumericvalue"><code>CSSNumericValue</code></dfn> : <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-28">CSSStyleValue</a> {
    <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-10">CSSNumericValue</a> <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="method" href="#dom-cssnumericvalue-add" id="ref-for-dom-cssnumericvalue-add-1">add</a>(<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#typedefdef-cssnumberish" id="ref-for-typedefdef-cssnumberish-1">CSSNumberish</a>... <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSNumericValue/add(...values)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssnumericvalue-add-values-values"><code>values</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssnumericvalue-add-values-values"></a></dfn>);
    <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-11">CSSNumericValue</a> <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="method" href="#dom-cssnumericvalue-sub" id="ref-for-dom-cssnumericvalue-sub-1">sub</a>(<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#typedefdef-cssnumberish" id="ref-for-typedefdef-cssnumberish-2">CSSNumberish</a>... <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSNumericValue/sub(...values)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssnumericvalue-sub-values-values"><code>values</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssnumericvalue-sub-values-values"></a></dfn>);
    <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-12">CSSNumericValue</a> <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="method" href="#dom-cssnumericvalue-mul" id="ref-for-dom-cssnumericvalue-mul-1">mul</a>(<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#typedefdef-cssnumberish" id="ref-for-typedefdef-cssnumberish-3">CSSNumberish</a>... <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSNumericValue/mul(...values)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssnumericvalue-mul-values-values"><code>values</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssnumericvalue-mul-values-values"></a></dfn>);
    <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-13">CSSNumericValue</a> <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="method" href="#dom-cssnumericvalue-div" id="ref-for-dom-cssnumericvalue-div-1">div</a>(<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#typedefdef-cssnumberish" id="ref-for-typedefdef-cssnumberish-4">CSSNumberish</a>... <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSNumericValue/div(...values)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssnumericvalue-div-values-values"><code>values</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssnumericvalue-div-values-values"></a></dfn>);
    <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-14">CSSNumericValue</a> <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="method" href="#dom-cssnumericvalue-min" id="ref-for-dom-cssnumericvalue-min-1">min</a>(<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#typedefdef-cssnumberish" id="ref-for-typedefdef-cssnumberish-5">CSSNumberish</a>... <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSNumericValue/min(...values)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssnumericvalue-min-values-values"><code>values</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssnumericvalue-min-values-values"></a></dfn>);
    <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-15">CSSNumericValue</a> <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="method" href="#dom-cssnumericvalue-max" id="ref-for-dom-cssnumericvalue-max-1">max</a>(<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#typedefdef-cssnumberish" id="ref-for-typedefdef-cssnumberish-6">CSSNumberish</a>... <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSNumericValue/max(...values)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssnumericvalue-max-values-values"><code>values</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssnumericvalue-max-values-values"></a></dfn>);

    <a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-boolean"><span class="kt">boolean</span></a> <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="method" href="#dom-cssnumericvalue-equals" id="ref-for-dom-cssnumericvalue-equals-1">equals</a>(<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#typedefdef-cssnumberish" id="ref-for-typedefdef-cssnumberish-7">CSSNumberish</a>... <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSNumericValue/equals(...value)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssnumericvalue-equals-value-value"><code>value</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssnumericvalue-equals-value-value"></a></dfn>);

    <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-16">CSSNumericValue</a> <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="method" href="#dom-cssnumericvalue-to" id="ref-for-dom-cssnumericvalue-to-1">to</a>(<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSNumericValue/to(unit)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssnumericvalue-to-unit-unit"><code>unit</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssnumericvalue-to-unit-unit"></a></dfn>);
    <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssmathsum" id="ref-for-cssmathsum-1">CSSMathSum</a> <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="method" href="#dom-cssnumericvalue-tosum" id="ref-for-dom-cssnumericvalue-tosum-1">toSum</a>(<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a>... <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSNumericValue/toSum(...units)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssnumericvalue-tosum-units-units"><code>units</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssnumericvalue-tosum-units-units"></a></dfn>);
    // ??? type();

    <span class="kt">static</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-17">CSSNumericValue</a> <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="method" href="#dom-cssnumericvalue-parse" id="ref-for-dom-cssnumericvalue-parse-1">parse</a>(<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSNumericValue/parse(cssText)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssnumericvalue-parse-csstext-csstext"><code>cssText</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssnumericvalue-parse-csstext-csstext"></a></dfn>);
};
</pre>
   <p class="issue" id="issue-db0e4ae9"><a class="self-link" href="#issue-db0e4ae9"></a> Figure out how we want to represent the type of an expression in JS,
and define the type() method accordingly.</p>
   <p>The methods on the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-18">CSSNumericValue</a></code> superclass
represent operations that all numeric values can perform.</p>
   <p>The following are the arithmetic operations you can perform on dimensions:</p>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSNumericValue.add()">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSNumericValue" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" id="dom-cssnumericvalue-add"><code>add(...<var>values</var>)</code></dfn> method,
    when called on a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-19">CSSNumericValue</a></code> <var>this</var>,
    must perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Replace each <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> of <var>values</var> with the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#rectify-a-numberish-value" id="ref-for-rectify-a-numberish-value-1">rectifying a numberish value</a> for the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>this</var> is a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathsum" id="ref-for-cssmathsum-2">CSSMathSum</a></code> object, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-prepend">prepend</a> the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">items</a> in <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathsum-values" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathsum-values-1">values</a></code> internal slot
to <var>values</var>.
Otherwise,
prepend <var>this</var> to <var>values</var>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If all of the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">items</a> in <var>values</var> are <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-4">CSSUnitValue</a></code>s
and have the same <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-unit" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-unit-2">unit</a></code>,
return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-5">CSSUnitValue</a></code> whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-unit" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-unit-3">unit</a></code> internal slot is set to <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-unit" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-unit-4">unit</a></code> internal slot,
and <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-value-2">value</a></code> internal slot is set to the sum of
the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-value-3">value</a></code> internal slots
of the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">items</a> in <var>values</var>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Let <var>type</var> be the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#add-two-types" id="ref-for-add-two-types-1">adding</a> the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-type-1">types</a> of every <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> in <var>values</var>.
If <var>type</var> is failure, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathsum" id="ref-for-cssmathsum-3">CSSMathSum</a></code> object
whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathsum-values" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathsum-values-2">values</a></code> internal slot
is set to <var>values</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSNumericValue.sub()">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSNumericValue" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" id="dom-cssnumericvalue-sub"><code>sub(...<var>values</var>)</code></dfn> method,
    when called on a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-20">CSSNumericValue</a></code> <var>this</var>,
    must perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Replace each <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> of <var>values</var> with the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#rectify-a-numberish-value" id="ref-for-rectify-a-numberish-value-2">rectifying a numberish value</a> for the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a>,
then <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssmath-negate" id="ref-for-cssmath-negate-1">negating</a> the value.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return the result of calling the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssnumericvalue-add" id="ref-for-dom-cssnumericvalue-add-2">add()</a></code> internal algorithm
with <var>this</var> and <var>values</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="negate">
     To <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-for="CSSMath" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-noexport="" id="cssmath-negate">negate</dfn> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-21">CSSNumericValue</a></code> <var>this</var>: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>this</var> is a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathnegate" id="ref-for-cssmathnegate-1">CSSMathNegate</a></code> object,
return <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathnegate-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathnegate-value-1">value</a></code> internal slot.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>this</var> is a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-6">CSSUnitValue</a></code> object,
return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-7">CSSUnitValue</a></code> with the same <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-unit" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-unit-5">unit</a></code> internal slot as <var>this</var>,
and a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-value-4">value</a></code> internal slot set to the negation of <var>this</var>’s.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Otherwise,
return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathnegate" id="ref-for-cssmathnegate-2">CSSMathNegate</a></code> object
whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathnegate-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathnegate-value-2">value</a></code> internal slot
is set to <var>this</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSNumericValue.mul()">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSNumericValue" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" id="dom-cssnumericvalue-mul"><code>mul(...<var>values</var>)</code></dfn> method,
    when called on a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-22">CSSNumericValue</a></code> <var>this</var>,
    must perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Replace each <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> of <var>values</var> with the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#rectify-a-numberish-value" id="ref-for-rectify-a-numberish-value-3">rectifying a numberish value</a> for the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>this</var> is a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathproduct" id="ref-for-cssmathproduct-1">CSSMathProduct</a></code> object, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-prepend">prepend</a> the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">items</a> in <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathproduct-values" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathproduct-values-1">values</a></code> internal slot
to <var>values</var>.
Otherwise,
prepend <var>this</var> to <var>values</var>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Let <var>type</var> be the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-multiply-two-types" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-multiply-two-types-1">multiplying</a> the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-type-2">types</a> of every <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> in <var>values</var>.
If <var>type</var> is failure, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathproduct" id="ref-for-cssmathproduct-2">CSSMathProduct</a></code> object
whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathproduct-values" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathproduct-values-2">values</a></code> internal slot
is set to <var>values</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSNumericValue.div()">
