     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSNumericValue" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" id="dom-cssnumericvalue-div"><code>div(...<var>values</var>)</code></dfn> method,
    when called on a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-23">CSSNumericValue</a></code> <var>this</var>,
    must perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Replace each <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> of <var>values</var> with the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#rectify-a-numberish-value" id="ref-for-rectify-a-numberish-value-4">rectifying a numberish value</a> for the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a>,
then <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssmath-invert" id="ref-for-cssmath-invert-1">inverting</a> the value.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return the result of calling the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssnumericvalue-mul" id="ref-for-dom-cssnumericvalue-mul-2">mul()</a></code> internal algorithm
with <var>this</var> and <var>values</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="invert">
     To <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-for="CSSMath" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-noexport="" id="cssmath-invert">invert</dfn> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-24">CSSNumericValue</a></code> <var>this</var>: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>this</var> is a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathinvert" id="ref-for-cssmathinvert-1">CSSMathInvert</a></code> object,
return <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathinvert-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathinvert-value-1">value</a></code> internal slot.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Otherwise,
return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathinvert" id="ref-for-cssmathinvert-2">CSSMathInvert</a></code> object
whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathinvert-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathinvert-value-2">value</a></code> internal slot
is set to <var>this</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSNumericValue.min()">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSNumericValue" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" id="dom-cssnumericvalue-min"><code>min(...<var>values</var>)</code></dfn> method,
    when called on a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-25">CSSNumericValue</a></code> <var>this</var>,
    must perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Replace each <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> of <var>values</var> with the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#rectify-a-numberish-value" id="ref-for-rectify-a-numberish-value-5">rectifying a numberish value</a> for the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>this</var> is a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathmin" id="ref-for-cssmathmin-1">CSSMathMin</a></code> object, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-prepend">prepend</a> the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">items</a> in <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathmin-values" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathmin-values-1">values</a></code> internal slot
to <var>values</var>.
Otherwise,
prepend <var>this</var> to <var>values</var>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Let <var>type</var> be the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#add-two-types" id="ref-for-add-two-types-2">adding</a> the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-type-3">types</a> of every <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> in <var>values</var>.
If <var>type</var> is failure, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathmin" id="ref-for-cssmathmin-2">CSSMathMin</a></code> object
whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathmin-values" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathmin-values-2">values</a></code> internal slot
is set to <var>values</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSNumericValue.max()">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSNumericValue" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" id="dom-cssnumericvalue-max"><code>max(...<var>values</var>)</code></dfn> method,
    when called on a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-26">CSSNumericValue</a></code> <var>this</var>,
    must perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Replace each <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> of <var>values</var> with the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#rectify-a-numberish-value" id="ref-for-rectify-a-numberish-value-6">rectifying a numberish value</a> for the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>this</var> is a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathmax" id="ref-for-cssmathmax-1">CSSMathMax</a></code> object, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-prepend">prepend</a> the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">items</a> in <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathmax-values" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathmax-values-1">values</a></code> internal slot
to <var>values</var>.
Otherwise,
prepend <var>this</var> to <var>values</var>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Let <var>type</var> be the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#add-two-types" id="ref-for-add-two-types-3">adding</a> the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-type-4">types</a> of every <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> in <var>values</var>.
If <var>type</var> is failure, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathmax" id="ref-for-cssmathmax-2">CSSMathMax</a></code> object
whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathmax-values" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathmax-values-2">values</a></code> internal slot
is set to <var>values</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSNumericValue.equals(value)">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSNumericValue" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" id="dom-cssnumericvalue-equals"><code>equals(...<var>values</var>)</code></dfn> method,
    when called on a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-27">CSSNumericValue</a></code> <var>this</var>,
    must perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Replace each <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> of <var>values</var> with the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#rectify-a-numberish-value" id="ref-for-rectify-a-numberish-value-7">rectifying a numberish value</a> for the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Let <var>thisAndValues</var> be <var>this</var> prepended to <var>values</var>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If all <var>item</var>s of <var>thisAndValues</var> do not belong to the same class return false. Example: all items in <var>thisAndValues</var> must be <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-8">CSSUnitValue</a></code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If all <var>item</var>s in <var>thisAndValues</var> are {{CSSUnitValue}}s and have the same <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-unit" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-unit-6">unit</a></code> and <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-value-5">value</a></code> return true.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If all <var>item</var>s in <var>thisAndValues</var> are <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathvalue" id="ref-for-cssmathvalue-2">CSSMathValue</a></code>s :</p>
      <ol>
       <li data-md="">
        <p>If <var>thisAndValues</var> are all either <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathsum" id="ref-for-cssmathsum-4">CSSMathSum</a></code>, <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathproduct" id="ref-for-cssmathproduct-3">CSSMathProduct</a></code>, <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathmin" id="ref-for-cssmathmin-3">CSSMathMin</a></code> or <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathmax" id="ref-for-cssmathmax-3">CSSMathMax</a></code>, iterate over the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericarray" id="ref-for-cssnumericarray-1">CSSNumericArray</a></code>s on <var>thisAndValues</var>,</p>
        <ol>
         <li data-md="">
          <p>For each <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-28">CSSNumericValue</a></code> in each of the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericarray" id="ref-for-cssnumericarray-2">CSSNumericArray</a></code>s go back to step 1 to check that the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-9">CSSUnitValue</a></code>s on all items in <var>thisAndValue</var> are equal.</p>
        </ol>
       <li data-md="">
        <p>If <var>this</var> and <var>value</var> are both either <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathnegate" id="ref-for-cssmathnegate-3">CSSMathNegate</a></code> or <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathinvert" id="ref-for-cssmathinvert-3">CSSMathInvert</a></code>:</p>
        <ol>
         <li data-md="">
          <p>Go back to step 1 to check that the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-10">CSSUnitValue</a></code> on all items in <var>thisAndValue</var> are equal.</p>
        </ol>
      </ol>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSNumericValue.to()">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSNumericValue" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" id="dom-cssnumericvalue-to"><code>to(<var>unit</var>)</code></dfn> method converts an existing <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-29">CSSNumericValue</a></code> <var>this</var> into another one with the specified <var>unit</var>,
    if possible.
    When called, it must perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Let <var>type</var> be the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#create-a-type" id="ref-for-create-a-type-1">creating a type</a> from <var>unit</var>.
If <var>type</var> is failure, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#syntaxerror">SyntaxError</a></code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Let <var>sum</var> be the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#create-a-sum-value" id="ref-for-create-a-sum-value-1">creating a sum value</a> from <var>this</var>.
If <var>sum</var> is failure, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>sum</var> has more than one <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a>, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code>.
Otherwise, let <var>item</var> be the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#create-a-cssunitvalue-from-a-sum-value-item" id="ref-for-create-a-cssunitvalue-from-a-sum-value-item-1">creating a CSSUnitValue</a> from the sole <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> in <var>sum</var>,
then <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#convert-a-cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-convert-a-cssunitvalue-1">converting</a> it to <var>unit</var>.
If <var>item</var> is failure, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return <var>item</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="create a CSSUnitValue from a sum value item">
     When asked to <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-export="" id="create-a-cssunitvalue-from-a-sum-value-item">create a CSSUnitValue from a sum value item</dfn> <var>item</var>,
    perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>item</var> has more than one <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-entry">entry</a> in its <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#sum-value-unit-map" id="ref-for-sum-value-unit-map-1">unit map</a>,
return failure.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>item</var> has no <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-entry">entries</a> in its <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#sum-value-unit-map" id="ref-for-sum-value-unit-map-2">unit map</a>,
return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-11">CSSUnitValue</a></code> whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-unit" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-unit-7">unit</a></code> internal slot
is set to "number",
and whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-value-6">value</a></code> internal slot
is set to <var>item</var>’s <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#sum-value-value" id="ref-for-sum-value-value-1">value</a>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Otherwise, <var>item</var> has a single <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-entry">entry</a> in its <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#sum-value-unit-map" id="ref-for-sum-value-unit-map-3">unit map</a>.
If that <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-entry">entry’s</a> <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-value">value</a> is anything other than <code>1</code>,
return failure.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Otherwise, return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-12">CSSUnitValue</a></code> whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-unit" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-unit-8">unit</a></code> internal slot
is set to that <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-entry">entry’s</a> <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-key">key</a>,
and whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-value-7">value</a></code> internal slot
is set to <var>item</var>’s <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#sum-value-value" id="ref-for-sum-value-value-2">value</a>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSNumericValue.toSum()">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSNumericValue" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" id="dom-cssnumericvalue-tosum"><code>toSum(...<var>units</var>)</code></dfn> method converts an existing <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-30">CSSNumericValue</a></code> <var>this</var> into a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathsum" id="ref-for-cssmathsum-5">CSSMathSum</a></code> of only <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-13">CSSUnitValue</a></code>s with the specified units,
    if possible.
    (It’s like <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssnumericvalue-to" id="ref-for-dom-cssnumericvalue-to-2">to()</a></code>,
    but allows the result to have multiple units in it.)
    If called without any units,
    it just simplifies <var>this</var> into a minimal sum of <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-14">CSSUnitValue</a></code>s. 
    <p>When called, it must perform the following steps:</p>
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p><a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-iterate">For each</a> <var>unit</var> in <var>units</var>,
if the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#create-a-type" id="ref-for-create-a-type-2">creating a type</a> from <var>unit</var> is failure, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#syntaxerror">SyntaxError</a></code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Let <var>sum</var> be the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#create-a-sum-value" id="ref-for-create-a-sum-value-2">creating a sum value</a> from <var>this</var>.
If <var>sum</var> is failure, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Let <var>values</var> be the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#create-a-cssunitvalue-from-a-sum-value-item" id="ref-for-create-a-cssunitvalue-from-a-sum-value-item-2">creating a CSSUnitValue</a> <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-iterate">for each</a> <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> in <var>sum</var>.
If any <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> of <var>values</var> is failure, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>units</var> is <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-empty">empty</a>,
sort <var>values</var> in <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#code-point">code point</a> order according to the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-unit" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-unit-9">unit</a></code> internal slot of its <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">items</a>,
then return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathsum" id="ref-for-cssmathsum-6">CSSMathSum</a></code> object
whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathsum-values" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathsum-values-3">values</a></code> internal slot is set to <var>values</var>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Otherwise,
let <var>result</var> initially be an empty <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list">list</a>. <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-iterate">For each</a> <var>unit</var> in <var>units</var>:</p>
      <ol>
       <li data-md="">
        <p>Let <var>temp</var> initially be a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-15">CSSUnitValue</a></code> whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-unit" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-unit-10">unit</a></code> internal slot
is set to <var>unit</var> and whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-value-8">value</a></code> internal slot
is set to <code>0</code>.</p>
       <li data-md="">
        <p><a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-iterate">For each</a> <var>value</var> in <var>values</var>:</p>
        <ol>
         <li data-md="">
          <p>Let <var>value unit</var> be <var>value</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-unit" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-unit-11">unit</a></code> internal slot.</p>
         <li data-md="">
          <p>If <var>value unit</var> is a <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#compatible-units">compatible unit</a> with <var>unit</var>,
then:</p>
          <p>1.<a data-link-type="dfn" href="#convert-a-cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-convert-a-cssunitvalue-2">convert</a> <var>value</var> to <var>unit</var>.</p>
          <ol start="2">
           <li data-md="">
            <p>Increment <var>temp</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-value-9">value</a></code> internal slot
by the value of <var>value</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-value-10">value</a></code> internal slot.</p>
           <li data-md="">
            <p><a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-remove">Remove</a> <var>value</var> from <var>values</var>.</p>
          </ol>
        </ol>
       <li data-md="">
        <p><a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-append">Append</a> <var>temp</var> to <var>result</var>.</p>
      </ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>values</var> is not <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-empty">empty</a>, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code>. <span class="note"><var>this</var> had units that you didn’t ask for.</span></p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathsum" id="ref-for-cssmathsum-7">CSSMathSum</a></code> object
whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathsum-values" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathsum-values-4">values</a></code> internal slot
is set to <var>result</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="sum value">
     A <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-noexport="" id="sum-value">sum value</dfn> is an abstract representation of a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-31">CSSNumericValue</a></code> as a sum of numbers with (possibly complex) units.
    Not all <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-32">CSSNumericValue</a></code>s can be expressed as a <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#sum-value" id="ref-for-sum-value-1">sum value</a>. 
    <p>A <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#sum-value" id="ref-for-sum-value-2">sum value</a> is a <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list">list</a>.
    Each entry in the list is a <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#tuple">tuple</a> of a <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-for="sum value" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-noexport="" id="sum-value-value">value</dfn>,
    which is a number,
    and a <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-for="sum value" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-noexport="" id="sum-value-unit-map">unit map</dfn>,
    which is a <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#ordered-map">map</a> of units (strings) to powers (integers).</p>
    <div class="example" id="example-d129033b">
     <a class="self-link" href="#example-d129033b"></a> Here are a few examples of CSS values,
        and their equivalent <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#sum-value" id="ref-for-sum-value-3">sum values</a>: 
     <ul>
      <li data-md="">
       <p><span class="css">1px</span> becomes <code>«(1, «["px" → 1]»)»</code></p>
      <li data-md="">
       <p><span class="css">calc(1px + 1in)</span> becomes <code>«(97, «["px" → 1]»)»</code> (because <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#in">in</a> and <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#px">px</a> are <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#compatible-units">compatible units</a>,
and <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#px">px</a> is the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#canonical-unit">canonical unit</a> for them)</p>
      <li data-md="">
       <p><span class="css">calc(1px + 2em)</span> becomes <code>«(1, «["px" → 1]»), (2, «["em" → 1]»)»</code></p>
      <li data-md="">
       <p><span class="css">calc(1px + 2%)</span> becomes <code>«(1, «["px" → 1]»), (2, «["percent" → 1]»)»</code> (percentages are allowed to add to other units,
but aren’t resolved into another unit,
like they are in a <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-type-5">type</a>)</p>
      <li data-md="">
       <p><span class="css">calc(1px * 2em)</span> becomes <code>«(2, «["em" → 1, "px" → 1]»)»</code></p>
      <li data-md="">
       <p><span class="css">calc(1px + 1deg)</span> can’t be represented as a <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#sum-value" id="ref-for-sum-value-4">sum value</a> because it’s an invalid computation</p>
      <li data-md="">
       <p><span class="css">calc(1px * 1deg)</span> becomes <code>«(2, «["deg" → 1, "px" → 1]»)»</code></p>
     </ul>
    </div>
    <p>To <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-lt="create a sum value|creating a sum value" data-noexport="" id="create-a-sum-value">create a sum value</dfn> from a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-33">CSSNumericValue</a></code> <var>this</var>,
    the steps differ based on <var>this</var>’s class:</p>
    <dl class="switch">
     <dt data-md=""><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-16">CSSUnitValue</a></code>
     <dd data-md="">
      <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="sum value from CSSUnitValue">
       <ol>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>Let <var>unit</var> be the value of <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-unit" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-unit-12">unit</a></code> internal slot,
and <var>value</var> be the value of <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-value-11">value</a></code> internal slot.</p>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>If <var>unit</var> is a member of a set of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#compatible-units">compatible units</a>,
and is not the set’s <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#canonical-unit">canonical unit</a>,
multiply <var>value</var> by the conversion ratio between <var>unit</var> and the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#canonical-unit">canonical unit</a>,
and change <var>unit</var> to the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#canonical-unit">canonical unit</a>.</p>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>If <var>unit</var> is <code>"number"</code>,
return «(<var>value</var>, «[ ]»)».</p>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>Otherwise, return <code>«(<var>value</var>, «[<var>unit</var> → 1]»)»</code>.</p>
       </ol>
      </div>
     <dt data-md=""><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathsum" id="ref-for-cssmathsum-8">CSSMathSum</a></code>
     <dd data-md="">
      <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="sum value from CSSMathSum">
       <ol>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>Let <var>values</var> initially be an empty list.</p>
        <li data-md="">
         <p><a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-iterate">For each</a> <var>item</var> in <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathsum-values" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathsum-values-5">values</a></code> internal slot:</p>
         <ol>
          <li data-md="">
           <p>Let <var>value</var> be the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#create-a-sum-value" id="ref-for-create-a-sum-value-3">creating a sum value</a> from <var>item</var>.
If <var>value</var> is failure,
return failure.</p>
          <li data-md="">
           <p><a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-iterate">For each</a> <var>subvalue</var> of <var>value</var>:</p>
           <ol>
            <li data-md="">
             <p>If <var>values</var> already contains an <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> with the same <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#sum-value-unit-map" id="ref-for-sum-value-unit-map-4">unit map</a> as <var>subvalue</var>,
increment that <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a>’s <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#sum-value-value" id="ref-for-sum-value-value-3">value</a> by the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#sum-value-value" id="ref-for-sum-value-value-4">value</a> of <var>subvalue</var>.</p>
            <li data-md="">
             <p>Otherwise, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-append">append</a> <var>subvalue</var> to <var>values</var>.</p>
           </ol>
         </ol>
        <li data-md="">
         <p><a data-link-type="dfn" href="#create-a-type-from-a-unit-map" id="ref-for-create-a-type-from-a-unit-map-1">Create a type</a> from the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#sum-value-unit-map" id="ref-for-sum-value-unit-map-5">unit map</a> of each <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> of <var>values</var>,
and <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#add-two-types" id="ref-for-add-two-types-4">add</a> all the types together.
If the result is failure,
return failure.</p>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>Return <var>values</var>.</p>
       </ol>
      </div>
     <dt data-md=""><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathnegate" id="ref-for-cssmathnegate-4">CSSMathNegate</a></code>
     <dd data-md="">
      <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="sum value from CSSMathNegate">
       <ol>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>Let <var>values</var> be the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#create-a-sum-value" id="ref-for-create-a-sum-value-4">creating a sum value</a> from <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathnegate-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathnegate-value-3">value</a></code> internal slot.</p>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>If <var>values</var> is failure,
return failure.</p>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>Negate the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#sum-value-value" id="ref-for-sum-value-value-5">value</a> of each <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> of <var>values</var>.</p>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>Return <var>values</var>.</p>
       </ol>
      </div>
     <dt data-md=""><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathproduct" id="ref-for-cssmathproduct-4">CSSMathProduct</a></code>
     <dd data-md="">
      <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="sum value from CSSMathProduct">
       <ol>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>Let <var>values</var> initially be the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#sum-value" id="ref-for-sum-value-5">sum value</a> «(1, «[ ]»)».
(I.e. what you’d get from <span class="css">1</span>.)</p>
        <li data-md="">
         <p><a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-iterate">For each</a> <var>item</var> in <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathproduct-values" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathproduct-values-3">values</a></code> internal slot:</p>
         <ol>
          <li data-md="">
           <p>Let <var>new values</var> be the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#create-a-sum-value" id="ref-for-create-a-sum-value-5">creating a sum value</a> from <var>item</var>.
Let <var>temp</var> initially be an empty <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list">list</a>.</p>
          <li data-md="">
           <p>If <var>new values</var> is failure,
return failure.</p>
          <li data-md="">
           <p><a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-iterate">For each</a> <var>item1</var> in <var>values</var>:</p>
           <ol>
            <li data-md="">
             <p><a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-iterate">For each</a> <var>item2</var> in <var>new values</var>:</p>
             <ol>
              <li data-md="">
               <p>Let <var>item</var> be a <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#tuple">tuple</a> with its <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#sum-value-value" id="ref-for-sum-value-value-6">value</a> set to the product of the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#sum-value-value" id="ref-for-sum-value-value-7">values</a> of <var>item1</var> and <var>item2</var>,
and its <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#sum-value-unit-map" id="ref-for-sum-value-unit-map-6">unit map</a> set to the union of the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#sum-value-unit-map" id="ref-for-sum-value-unit-map-7">unit maps</a> of <var>item1</var> and <var>item2</var>,
with all <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-entry">entries</a> with a zero value removed.</p>
              <li data-md="">
               <p>Append <var>item</var> to <var>temp</var>.</p>
             </ol>
           </ol>
          <li data-md="">
           <p>Set <var>values</var> to <var>temp</var>.</p>
         </ol>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>Return <var>values</var>.</p>
       </ol>
      </div>
     <dt data-md=""><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathinvert" id="ref-for-cssmathinvert-4">CSSMathInvert</a></code>
     <dd data-md="">
      <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="sum value from CSSMathInvert">
       <ol>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>Let <var>values</var> be the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#create-a-sum-value" id="ref-for-create-a-sum-value-6">creating a sum value</a> from <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathinvert-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathinvert-value-3">value</a></code> internal slot.</p>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>If <var>values</var> is failure,
return failure.</p>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>If the length of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#sum-value-value" id="ref-for-sum-value-value-8">values</a> is more than one,
return failure.</p>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>Invert (find the reciprocal of) the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#sum-value-value" id="ref-for-sum-value-value-9">value</a> of the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> in <var>values</var>,
and negate the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-value">value</a> of each <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-entry">entry</a> in its <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#sum-value-unit-map" id="ref-for-sum-value-unit-map-8">unit map</a>.</p>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>Return <var>values</var>.</p>
       </ol>
      </div>
     <dt data-md=""><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathmin" id="ref-for-cssmathmin-4">CSSMathMin</a></code>
     <dd data-md="">
      <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="sum value from CSSMathMin">
       <ol>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>Let <var>args</var> be the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#create-a-sum-value" id="ref-for-create-a-sum-value-7">creating a sum value</a> <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-iterate">for each</a> <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> in <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathmin-values" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathmin-values-3">values</a></code> internal slot.</p>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>If any <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> of <var>args</var> is failure,
or has a length greater than one,
return failure.</p>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>If not all of the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#sum-value-unit-map" id="ref-for-sum-value-unit-map-9">unit maps</a> among the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">items</a> of <var>args</var> are identical,
return failure.</p>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>Return the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> of <var>args</var> whose sole <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> has the smallest <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#sum-value-value" id="ref-for-sum-value-value-10">value</a>.</p>
       </ol>
      </div>
     <dt data-md=""><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathmax" id="ref-for-cssmathmax-4">CSSMathMax</a></code>
     <dd data-md="">
      <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="sum value from CSSMathMax">
       <ol>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>Let <var>args</var> be the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#create-a-sum-value" id="ref-for-create-a-sum-value-8">creating a sum value</a> <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-iterate">for each</a> <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> in <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathmax-values" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathmax-values-3">values</a></code> internal slot.</p>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>If any <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> of <var>args</var> is failure,
or has a length greater than one,
return failure.</p>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>If not all of the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#sum-value-unit-map" id="ref-for-sum-value-unit-map-10">unit maps</a> among the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">items</a> of <var>args</var> are identical,
return failure.</p>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>Return the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> of <var>args</var> whose sole <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> has the largest <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#sum-value-value" id="ref-for-sum-value-value-11">value</a>.</p>
       </ol>
      </div>
    </dl>
    <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="create a type from a unit map">
      To <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-noexport="" id="create-a-type-from-a-unit-map">create a type from a unit map</dfn> <var>unit map</var>: 
     <ol>
      <li data-md="">
       <p>Let <var>types</var> be an initially empty <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list">list</a>.</p>
      <li data-md="">
       <p><a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-iterate">For each</a> <var>unit</var> → <var>power</var> in <var>unit map</var>:</p>
       <ol>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>Let <var>type</var> be the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#create-a-type" id="ref-for-create-a-type-3">creating a type</a> from <var>unit</var>.</p>
        <li data-md="">
         <p>Set <var>type</var>’s sole <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-value">value</a> to <var>power</var>.</p>
        <li data-md="">
         <p><a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-append">Append</a> <var>type</var> to <var>types</var>.</p>
       </ol>
      <li data-md="">
       <p>Return the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-multiply-two-types" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-multiply-two-types-2">multiplying</a> all the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">items</a> of <var>types</var>.</p>
     </ol>
    </div>
   </div>
   <p>The <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssnumericvalue-parse" id="ref-for-dom-cssnumericvalue-parse-2">parse()</a></code> method allows a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-34">CSSNumericValue</a></code> to be constructed directly from a string containing CSS.
Note that this is a static method,
existing directly on the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-35">CSSNumericValue</a></code> interface object,
rather than on <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-36">CSSNumericValue</a></code> instances.</p>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSNumericValue.parse(cssText)">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSNumericValue" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" id="dom-cssnumericvalue-parse"><code>parse(<var>cssText</var>)</code></dfn> method,
    when called,
    must perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p><a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-syntax-3/#parse-a-component-value">Parse a component value</a> from <var>cssText</var> and let <var>result</var> be the result.
If <var>result</var> is a syntax error, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#syntaxerror">SyntaxError</a></code> and abort this algorithm.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>result</var> is not a <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-syntax-3/#typedef-number-token">&lt;number-token></a>, <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-syntax-3/#typedef-percentage-token">&lt;percentage-token></a>, <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-syntax-3/#typedef-dimension-token">&lt;dimension-token></a>,
or a <a class="production css" data-link-type="function" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#funcdef-calc">&lt;calc()></a>, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#syntaxerror">SyntaxError</a></code> and abort this algorithm.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p><a data-link-type="dfn" href="#normalize-a-numeric-value" id="ref-for-normalize-a-numeric-value-1">Normalize a numeric value</a> <var>result</var>,
and return the result.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <h4 class="heading settled" data-level="4.3.2" id="numeric-typing"><span class="secno">4.3.2. </span><span class="content">Numeric Value Typing</span><a class="self-link" href="#numeric-typing"></a></h4>
   <p>Each <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-37">CSSNumericValue</a></code> has an associated <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-for="CSSNumericValue" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-noexport="" id="cssnumericvalue-type">type</dfn>,
which is a <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#ordered-map">map</a> of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-base-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-base-type-1">base types</a> to integers,
and an associated <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-percent-hint" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-percent-hint-1">percent hint</a>.
The <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-for="CSSNumericValue" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-lt="base type" data-noexport="" id="cssnumericvalue-base-type">base types</dfn> are
"length",
"angle",
"time",
"frequency",
"resolution",
"flex",
and "percent".
The ordering of a <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-type-6">type</a>’s entries always matches this <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-base-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-base-type-2">base type</a> ordering.
The <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-for="CSSNumericValue" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-noexport="" id="cssnumericvalue-percent-hint">percent hint</dfn> is either null or a <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-base-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-base-type-3">base type</a> other than "percent".</p>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="create a type">
     To <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-lt="create a type|creating a type" data-noexport="" id="create-a-type">create a type</dfn> from a string <var>unit</var>,
    follow the appropriate branch of the following: 
    <dl class="switch">
     <dt data-md=""><var>unit</var> is "number"
     <dd data-md="">
      <p>Return «[ ]» (empty map)</p>
     <dt data-md=""><var>unit</var> is "percent"
     <dd data-md="">
      <p>Return «[ "percent" → 1 ]»</p>
     <dt data-md=""><var>unit</var> is a <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#length-value" title="Expands to: em | vb | ch | cm | vh | vi | vw | ex | in | ic | pt | px | lh | pc | rem | rlh | vmax | advance measure | vmin | mm | cap | q">&lt;length></a> unit
     <dd data-md="">
      <p>Return «[ "length" → 1 ]»</p>
     <dt data-md=""><var>unit</var> is an <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#angle-value" title="Expands to: turn | rad | grad | deg">&lt;angle></a> unit
     <dd data-md="">
      <p>Return «[ "angle" → 1 ]»</p>
     <dt data-md=""><var>unit</var> is a <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#time-value" title="Expands to: s | ms">&lt;time></a> unit
     <dd data-md="">
      <p>Return «[ "time" → 1 ]»</p>
     <dt data-md=""><var>unit</var> is a <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#frequency-value" title="Expands to: hz | khz">&lt;frequency></a> unit
     <dd data-md="">
      <p>Return «[ "frequency" → 1 ]»</p>
     <dt data-md=""><var>unit</var> is a <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#resolution-value" title="Expands to: dppx | x | dpcm | dpi">&lt;resolution></a> unit
     <dd data-md="">
      <p>Return «[ "resolution" → 1 ]»</p>
     <dt data-md=""><var>unit</var> is a <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-grid-1/#typedef-flex" title="Expands to: fr">&lt;flex></a> unit
     <dd data-md="">
      <p>Return «[ "flex" → 1 ]»</p>
     <dt data-md="">anything else
     <dd data-md="">
      <p>Return failure.</p>
    </dl>
    <p>In all cases, the associated <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-percent-hint" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-percent-hint-2">percent hint</a> is null.</p>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="add two types">
     To <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-local-lt="add | addition" data-noexport="" id="add-two-types">add two types</dfn> <var>type1</var> and <var>type2</var>,
    perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Replace <var>type1</var> with a fresh copy of <var>type1</var>,
and <var>type2</var> with a fresh copy of <var>type2</var>.
Let <var>finalType</var> be a new <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-type-7">type</a> with an initially empty <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#ordered-map">ordered map</a> and an initially null <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-percent-hint" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-percent-hint-3">percent hint</a>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <dl class="switch">
       <dt data-md="">If both <var>type1</var> and <var>type2</var> have non-null <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-percent-hint" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-percent-hint-4">percent hints</a> with different values
       <dd data-md="">
        <p>The types can’t be added.
Return failure.</p>
       <dt data-md="">If <var>type1</var> has a non-null <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-percent-hint" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-percent-hint-5">percent hint</a> <var>hint</var> and <var>type2</var> doesn’t
       <dd data-md="">
        <p><a data-link-type="dfn" href="#apply-the-percent-hint" id="ref-for-apply-the-percent-hint-1">Apply the percent hint</a> <var>hint</var> to <var>type2</var>.</p>
        <p>Vice versa if <var>type2</var> has a non-null <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-percent-hint" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-percent-hint-6">percent hint</a> and <var>type1</var> doesn’t.</p>
       <dt data-md="">Otherwise
       <dd data-md="">
        <p>Continue to the next step.</p>
      </dl>
     <li data-md="">
      <dl class="switch">
       <dt data-md="">If all the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-entry">entries</a> of <var>type1</var> with non-zero values
are <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-exists">contained</a> in <var>type2</var> with the same value,
and vice-versa
       <dd data-md="">
        <p>Copy all of <var>type1</var>’s <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-entry">entries</a> to <var>finalType</var>,
and then copy all of <var>type2</var>’s <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-entry">entries</a> to <var>finalType</var> that <var>finalType</var> doesn’t already <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-exists">contain</a>.
Set <var>finalType</var>’s <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-percent-hint" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-percent-hint-7">percent hint</a> to <var>type1</var>’s <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-percent-hint" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-percent-hint-8">percent hint</a>.
Return <var>finalType</var>.</p>
       <dt data-md="">If <var>type1</var> and/or <var>type2</var> <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-exists">contain</a> "percent" with a non-zero value,
and <var>type1</var> and/or <var>type2</var> <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-exists">contain</a> a key <em>other than</em> "percent" with a non-zero value
       <dd data-md="">
        <p>For each <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-base-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-base-type-4">base type</a> other than "percent" <var>hint</var>:</p>
        <ol>
         <li data-md="">
          <p>Provisionally <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#apply-the-percent-hint" id="ref-for-apply-the-percent-hint-2">apply the percent hint</a> <var>hint</var> to both <var>type1</var> and <var>type2</var>.</p>
         <li data-md="">
          <p>If, afterwards, all the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-entry">entries</a> of <var>type1</var> with non-zero values
are <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-exists">contained</a> in <var>type2</var> with the same value,
and vice versa,
then copy all of <var>type1</var>’s <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-entry">entries</a> to <var>finalType</var>,
and then copy all of <var>type2</var>’s <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-entry">entries</a> to <var>finalType</var> that <var>finalType</var> doesn’t already <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-exists">contain</a>.
Set <var>finalType</var>’s <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-percent-hint" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-percent-hint-9">percent hint</a> to <var>hint</var>.
Return <var>finalType</var>.</p>
         <li data-md="">
          <p>Otherwise, revert <var>type1</var> and <var>type2</var> to their state at the start of this loop.</p>
        </ol>
        <p>If the loop finishes without returning <var>finalType</var>,
then the types can’t be added.
Return failure.</p>
        <p class="note" role="note"><span>Note:</span> You can shortcut this in some cases
by just checking the sum of all the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-value">values</a> of <var>type1</var> vs <var>type2</var>.
If the sums are different,
the types can’t be added.</p>
       <dt data-md="">Otherwise
       <dd data-md="">
        <p>The types can’t be added.
Return failure.</p>
      </dl>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="apply the percent hint">
     To <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-noexport="" id="apply-the-percent-hint">apply the percent hint</dfn> <var>hint</var> to a <var>type</var>,
    perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>type</var> doesn’t <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-exists">contain</a> <var>hint</var>, set <var>type</var>[<var>hint</var>] to 0.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>type</var> <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-exists">contains</a> "percent", add <var>type</var>["percent"] to <var>type</var>[<var>hint</var>],
then set <var>type</var>["percent"] to 0.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Set <var>type</var>’s <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-percent-hint" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-percent-hint-10">percent hint</a> to <var>hint</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="multiply two types">
     To <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-for="CSSNumericValue" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-local-lt="multiply | multiplication" data-noexport="" id="cssnumericvalue-multiply-two-types">multiply two types</dfn> <var>type1</var> and <var>type2</var>,
    perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Replace <var>type1</var> with a fresh copy of <var>type1</var>,
and <var>type2</var> with a fresh copy of <var>type2</var>.
Let <var>finalType</var> be a new <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-type-8">type</a> with an initially empty <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#ordered-map">ordered map</a> and an initially null <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-percent-hint" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-percent-hint-11">percent hint</a>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If both <var>type1</var> and <var>type2</var> have non-null <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-percent-hint" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-percent-hint-12">percent hints</a> with different values,
the types can’t be multiplied.
Return failure.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>type1</var> has a non-null <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-percent-hint" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-percent-hint-13">percent hint</a> <var>hint</var> and <var>type2</var> doesn’t, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#apply-the-percent-hint" id="ref-for-apply-the-percent-hint-3">apply the percent hint</a> <var>hint</var> to <var>type2</var>.</p>
      <p>Vice versa if <var>type2</var> has a non-null <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-percent-hint" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-percent-hint-14">percent hint</a> and <var>type1</var> doesn’t.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Copy all of <var>type1</var>’s <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-entry">entries</a> to <var>finalType</var>,
then <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-iterate">for each</a> <var>baseType</var> → <var>power</var> of <var>type2</var>:</p>
      <ol>
       <li data-md="">
        <p>If <var>finalType</var>[<var>baseType</var>] <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-exists">exists</a>,
increment its value by <var>power</var>.</p>
       <li data-md="">
        <p>Otherwise, set <var>finalType</var>[<var>baseType</var>] to <var>power</var>.</p>
      </ol>
      <p>Set <var>finalType</var>’s <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-percent-hint" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-percent-hint-15">percent hint</a> to <var>type1</var>’s <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-percent-hint" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-percent-hint-16">percent hint</a>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return <var>finalType</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <p>A <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-type-9">type</a> is said to <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-for="CSSNumericValue" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-noexport="" id="cssnumericvalue-match">match</dfn> a CSS production in some circumstances:</p>
   <ul>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>A <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-type-10">type</a> matches <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#length-value" title="Expands to: em | vb | ch | cm | vh | vi | vw | ex | in | ic | pt | px | lh | pc | rem | rlh | vmax | advance measure | vmin | mm | cap | q">&lt;length></a> if its only non-zero <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-entry">entry</a> is «[ "length" → 1 ]»
and its <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-percent-hint" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-percent-hint-17">percent hint</a> is null.
Similarly for <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#angle-value" title="Expands to: turn | rad | grad | deg">&lt;angle></a>, <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#time-value" title="Expands to: s | ms">&lt;time></a>, <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#frequency-value" title="Expands to: hz | khz">&lt;frequency></a>, <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#resolution-value" title="Expands to: dppx | x | dpcm | dpi">&lt;resolution></a>, and <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-grid-1/#typedef-flex" title="Expands to: fr">&lt;flex></a>.</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>A <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-type-11">type</a> matches <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#percentage-value">&lt;percentage></a> if its only non-zero <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-entry">entry</a> is «[ "percent" → 1 ]».</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>A <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-type-12">type</a> matches <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#typedef-length-percentage">&lt;length-percentage></a> if its only non-zero <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-entry">entry</a> is either «[ "length" → 1 ]» or «[ "percentage" → 1 ]»
Same for <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#typedef-angle-percentage">&lt;angle-percentage></a>, <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#typedef-time-percentage">&lt;time-percentage></a>, etc.</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>A <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-type-13">type</a> matches <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#number-value">&lt;number></a> if it has no non-zero <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-entry">entries</a> and its <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-percent-hint" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-percent-hint-18">percent hint</a> is null.</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>A <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-type-14">type</a> matches <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#typedef-number-percentage">&lt;number-percentage></a> if it has no non-zero <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-entry">entries</a>,
or its only non-zero <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-entry">entry</a> is «[ "percentage" → 1 ]».</p>
   </ul>
   <p>Many specifications use ''[ <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#length-value" title="Expands to: em | vb | ch | cm | vh | vi | vw | ex | in | ic | pt | px | lh | pc | rem | rlh | vmax | advance measure | vmin | mm | cap | q">&lt;length></a> | <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#percentage-value">&lt;percentage></a> ]''
instead of ''<a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#typedef-length-percentage">&lt;length-percentage></a>'' in their grammar,
and specify in prose that the <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#length-value" title="Expands to: em | vb | ch | cm | vh | vi | vw | ex | in | ic | pt | px | lh | pc | rem | rlh | vmax | advance measure | vmin | mm | cap | q">&lt;length></a> and <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#percentage-value">&lt;percentage></a> can be combined.
For the purposes of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-match" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-match-1">matching</a>,
these cases should be treated as <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#typedef-length-percentage">&lt;length-percentage></a>.
Similarly for <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#typedef-angle-percentage">&lt;angle-percentage></a>, etc.</p>
   <p class="note" role="note"><span>Note:</span> <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-type-15">Types</a> form a semi-group under both addition
and a monoid under multiplication
(with the multiplicative identity being «[ ]» with a null <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-percent-hint" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-percent-hint-19">percent hint</a>),
meaning that they’re associative and commutative.
Thus the spec can, for example, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#add-two-types" id="ref-for-add-two-types-5">add</a> an unbounded number of types together unambiguously,
rather than having to manually <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#add-two-types" id="ref-for-add-two-types-6">add</a> them pair-wise.</p>
   <h4 class="heading settled" data-level="4.3.3" id="simple-numeric"><span class="secno">4.3.3. </span><span class="content">Value + Unit: <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-17">CSSUnitValue</a></code> objects</span><a class="self-link" href="#simple-numeric"></a></h4>
   <p>Numeric values that can be expressed as a single unit
(or a naked number or percentage)
are represented as <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-18">CSSUnitValue</a></code>s.</p>
   <div class="example" id="example-d97acb92">
    <a class="self-link" href="#example-d97acb92"></a> For example, the value <span class="css">5px</span> in a stylesheet
    will be represented by a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-19">CSSUnitValue</a></code> with its <code>value</code> attribute set to <code>5</code> and its <code>unit</code> attribute set to <code>"px"</code>. 
    <p>Similarly, the value <span class="css">10</span> in a stylesheet
    will be represented by a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-20">CSSUnitValue</a></code> with its <code>value</code> attribute set to <code>10</code> and its <code>unit</code> attribute set to <code>"number"</code>.</p>
   </div>
<pre class="idl highlight def">[<a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="constructor" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-cssunitvalue-1">Constructor</a>(<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-double"><span class="kt">double</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSUnitValue/CSSUnitValue(value, unit)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssunitvalue-cssunitvalue-value-unit-value"><code>value</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-cssunitvalue-value-unit-value"></a></dfn>, <a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSUnitValue/CSSUnitValue(value, unit)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssunitvalue-cssunitvalue-value-unit-unit"><code>unit</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-cssunitvalue-value-unit-unit"></a></dfn>)]
<span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="cssunitvalue"><code>CSSUnitValue</code></dfn> : <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-38">CSSNumericValue</a> {
    <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-double"><span class="kt">double</span></a> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSUnitValue" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" data-type="double" id="dom-cssunitvalue-value"><code>value</code></dfn>;
    <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a> <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="attribute" data-type="DOMString" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-unit" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-unit-13">unit</a>;
    <span class="kt">readonly</span> <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSUnitValue" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" data-readonly="" data-type="DOMString" id="dom-cssunitvalue-type"><code>type</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-type"></a></dfn>;
};
</pre>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSUnitValue constructor(value, unit)">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSUnitValue" data-dfn-type="constructor" data-export="" id="dom-cssunitvalue-cssunitvalue"><code>CSSUnitValue(<var>value</var>, <var>unit</var>)</code></dfn> constructor must,
    when called,
    perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#create-a-type" id="ref-for-create-a-type-4">creating a type</a> from <var>unit</var> returns failure, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#syntaxerror">SyntaxError</a></code> and abort this algorithm.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-21">CSSUnitValue</a></code> with its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-value-12">value</a></code> internal slot set to <var>value</var> and its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-unit" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-unit-14">unit</a></code> set to <var>unit</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSUnitValue.unit">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSUnitValue" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" id="dom-cssunitvalue-unit"><code>unit</code></dfn> attribute of a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-22">CSSUnitValue</a></code> <var>this</var> must,
    on setting a value <var>unit</var>,
    perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#create-a-type" id="ref-for-create-a-type-5">creating a type</a> from <var>unit</var> returns failure,, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Otherwise,
set <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-unit" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-unit-15">unit</a></code> internal slot to <var>unit</var>.</p>
    </ol>
    <p>On reading,
    it must return the value of <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-unit" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-unit-16">unit</a></code> internal slot.</p>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="[=type=] of a {{CSSUnitValue}}"> The <dfn data-dfn-type="dfn" data-noexport="" id="type-of-a-cssunitvalue"><a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-type-16">type</a> of a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-23">CSSUnitValue</a></code><a class="self-link" href="#type-of-a-cssunitvalue"></a></dfn> is the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#create-a-type" id="ref-for-create-a-type-6">creating a type</a> from its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-unit" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-unit-17">unit</a></code> internal slot. </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="create a CSSUnitValue from a string">
     To <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-export="" id="create-a-cssunitvalue-from-a-string">create a CSSUnitValue from a string</dfn> <var>str</var>,
    return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-24">CSSUnitValue</a></code> object
    with its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-value-13">value</a></code> internal slot
    set to the numeric portion of <var>str</var> parsed into a number,
    and its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-unit" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-unit-18">unit</a></code> internal slot
    set to the unit portion of <var>str</var>,
    or "number" or "percent" if <var>str</var> is a plain number or percent. 
    <div class="example" id="example-49853360"><a class="self-link" href="#example-49853360"></a> For example, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#create-a-cssunitvalue-from-a-string" id="ref-for-create-a-cssunitvalue-from-a-string-1">creating a CSSUnitValue</a> from <span class="css">5px</span> creates an object equivalent to <code>new CSSUnitValue(5, "px")</code>. </div>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="convert a CSSUnitValue">
     To <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-export="" id="convert-a-cssunitvalue">convert a CSSUnitValue</dfn> <var>this</var> to a unit <var>unit</var>,
    perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Let <var>old unit</var> be the value of <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-unit" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-unit-19">unit</a></code> internal slot,
and <var>old value</var> be the value of <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-value-14">value</a></code> internal slot.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>old unit</var> and <var>unit</var> are not <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#compatible-units">compatible units</a>,
return failure.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-25">CSSUnitValue</a></code> whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-unit" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-unit-20">unit</a></code> internal slot
is set to <var>unit</var>,
and whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-value-15">value</a></code> internal slot
is set to <var>old value</var> multiplied by
the conversation ratio between <var>old unit</var> and <var>unit</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <h4 class="heading settled" data-level="4.3.4" id="complex-numeric"><span class="secno">4.3.4. </span><span class="content">Complex Numeric Values: <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathvalue" id="ref-for-cssmathvalue-3">CSSMathValue</a></code> objects</span><a class="self-link" href="#complex-numeric"></a></h4>
   <p>Numeric values that are more complicated than a single value+unit
are represented by a tree of <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathvalue" id="ref-for-cssmathvalue-4">CSSMathValue</a></code> subclasses,
eventually terminating in <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-26">CSSUnitValue</a></code> objects at the leaf nodes.
The <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#funcdef-calc">calc()</a>, <span class="css">min()</span>, and <span class="css">max()</span> functions in CSS
are represented in this way.</p>
   <div class="example" id="example-daada808">
    <a class="self-link" href="#example-daada808"></a> For example,
    the CSS value <span class="css">calc(1em + 5px)</span> will be represented by a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathsum" id="ref-for-cssmathsum-9">CSSMathSum</a></code> like <code>CSSMathSum(CSS.em(1), CSS.px(5))</code>. 
    <p>A more complex expression,
    like <span class="css">calc(1em + 5px * 2)</span>,
    will be represented by a nested structure
    like <code>CSSMathSum(CSS.em(1), CSSMathProduct(CSS.px(5), 2))</code>.</p>
   </div>
<pre class="idl highlight def"><span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="cssmathvalue"><code>CSSMathValue</code></dfn> : <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-39">CSSNumericValue</a> {
    <span class="kt">readonly</span> <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#enumdef-cssmathoperator" id="ref-for-enumdef-cssmathoperator-1">CSSMathOperator</a> <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="attribute" data-readonly="" data-type="CSSMathOperator" href="#dom-cssmathvalue-operator" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathvalue-operator-1">operator</a>;
    <span class="kt">readonly</span> <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMathValue" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" data-readonly="" data-type="DOMString" id="dom-cssmathvalue-type"><code>type</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssmathvalue-type"></a></dfn>;
};

[<a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="constructor" href="#dom-cssmathsum-cssmathsum" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathsum-cssmathsum-1">Constructor</a>(<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#typedefdef-cssnumberish" id="ref-for-typedefdef-cssnumberish-8">CSSNumberish</a>... <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMathSum/CSSMathSum(args)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssmathsum-cssmathsum-args-args"><code>args</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssmathsum-cssmathsum-args-args"></a></dfn>)]
<span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="cssmathsum"><code>CSSMathSum</code></dfn> : <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssmathvalue" id="ref-for-cssmathvalue-5">CSSMathValue</a> {
    <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericarray" id="ref-for-cssnumericarray-3">CSSNumericArray</a> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMathSum" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" data-type="CSSNumericArray" id="dom-cssmathsum-values"><code>values</code></dfn>;
};

[<a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="constructor" href="#dom-cssmathproduct-cssmathproduct" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathproduct-cssmathproduct-1">Constructor</a>(<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#typedefdef-cssnumberish" id="ref-for-typedefdef-cssnumberish-9">CSSNumberish</a>... <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMathProduct/CSSMathProduct(args)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssmathproduct-cssmathproduct-args-args"><code>args</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssmathproduct-cssmathproduct-args-args"></a></dfn>)]
<span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="cssmathproduct"><code>CSSMathProduct</code></dfn> : <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssmathvalue" id="ref-for-cssmathvalue-6">CSSMathValue</a> {
    <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericarray" id="ref-for-cssnumericarray-4">CSSNumericArray</a> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMathProduct" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" data-type="CSSNumericArray" id="dom-cssmathproduct-values"><code>values</code></dfn>;
};

[<a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="constructor" href="#dom-cssmathnegate-cssmathnegate" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathnegate-cssmathnegate-1">Constructor</a>(<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#typedefdef-cssnumberish" id="ref-for-typedefdef-cssnumberish-10">CSSNumberish</a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMathNegate/CSSMathNegate(arg)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssmathnegate-cssmathnegate-arg-arg"><code>arg</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssmathnegate-cssmathnegate-arg-arg"></a></dfn>)]
<span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="cssmathnegate"><code>CSSMathNegate</code></dfn> : <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssmathvalue" id="ref-for-cssmathvalue-7">CSSMathValue</a> {
    <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-40">CSSNumericValue</a> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMathNegate" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" data-type="CSSNumericValue" id="dom-cssmathnegate-value"><code>value</code></dfn>;
};
