[<a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="constructor" href="#dom-cssmathinvert-cssmathinvert" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathinvert-cssmathinvert-1">Constructor</a>(<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#typedefdef-cssnumberish" id="ref-for-typedefdef-cssnumberish-11">CSSNumberish</a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMathInvert/CSSMathInvert(arg)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssmathinvert-cssmathinvert-arg-arg"><code>arg</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssmathinvert-cssmathinvert-arg-arg"></a></dfn>)]
<span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="cssmathinvert"><code>CSSMathInvert</code></dfn> : <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssmathvalue" id="ref-for-cssmathvalue-8">CSSMathValue</a> {
    <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-41">CSSNumericValue</a> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMathInvert" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" data-type="CSSNumericValue" id="dom-cssmathinvert-value"><code>value</code></dfn>;
};

[<a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="constructor" href="#dom-cssmathmin-cssmathmin" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathmin-cssmathmin-1">Constructor</a>(<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#typedefdef-cssnumberish" id="ref-for-typedefdef-cssnumberish-12">CSSNumberish</a>... <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMathMin/CSSMathMin(args)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssmathmin-cssmathmin-args-args"><code>args</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssmathmin-cssmathmin-args-args"></a></dfn>)]
<span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="cssmathmin"><code>CSSMathMin</code></dfn> : <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssmathvalue" id="ref-for-cssmathvalue-9">CSSMathValue</a> {
    <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericarray" id="ref-for-cssnumericarray-5">CSSNumericArray</a> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMathMin" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" data-type="CSSNumericArray" id="dom-cssmathmin-values"><code>values</code></dfn>;
};

[<a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="constructor" href="#dom-cssmathmax-cssmathmax" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathmax-cssmathmax-1">Constructor</a>(<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#typedefdef-cssnumberish" id="ref-for-typedefdef-cssnumberish-13">CSSNumberish</a>... <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMathMax/CSSMathMax(args)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssmathmax-cssmathmax-args-args"><code>args</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssmathmax-cssmathmax-args-args"></a></dfn>)]
<span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="cssmathmax"><code>CSSMathMax</code></dfn> : <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssmathvalue" id="ref-for-cssmathvalue-10">CSSMathValue</a> {
    <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericarray" id="ref-for-cssnumericarray-6">CSSNumericArray</a> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMathMax" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" data-type="CSSNumericArray" id="dom-cssmathmax-values"><code>values</code></dfn>;
};

<span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="cssnumericarray"><code>CSSNumericArray</code></dfn> {}; // See issue below

<span class="kt">enum</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="enum" data-export="" id="enumdef-cssmathoperator"><code>CSSMathOperator</code></dfn> {
    <dfn class="s idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMathOperator" data-dfn-type="enum-value" data-export="" data-lt="&quot;sum&quot;|sum" id="dom-cssmathoperator-sum"><code>"sum"</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssmathoperator-sum"></a></dfn>,
    <dfn class="s idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMathOperator" data-dfn-type="enum-value" data-export="" data-lt="&quot;product&quot;|product" id="dom-cssmathoperator-product"><code>"product"</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssmathoperator-product"></a></dfn>,
    <dfn class="s idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMathOperator" data-dfn-type="enum-value" data-export="" data-lt="&quot;negate&quot;|negate" id="dom-cssmathoperator-negate"><code>"negate"</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssmathoperator-negate"></a></dfn>,
    <dfn class="s idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMathOperator" data-dfn-type="enum-value" data-export="" data-lt="&quot;invert&quot;|invert" id="dom-cssmathoperator-invert"><code>"invert"</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssmathoperator-invert"></a></dfn>,
    <dfn class="s idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMathOperator" data-dfn-type="enum-value" data-export="" data-lt="&quot;min&quot;|min" id="dom-cssmathoperator-min"><code>"min"</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssmathoperator-min"></a></dfn>,
    <dfn class="s idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMathOperator" data-dfn-type="enum-value" data-export="" data-lt="&quot;max&quot;|max" id="dom-cssmathoperator-max"><code>"max"</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssmathoperator-max"></a></dfn>,
};
</pre>
   <p class="issue" id="issue-e95dded6"><a class="self-link" href="#issue-e95dded6"></a> <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericarray" id="ref-for-cssnumericarray-7">CSSNumericArray</a></code> will be an Array-like
restricted to containing CSSNumericValue objects.
This is dependent on <a href="https://github.com/heycam/webidl/issues/345">WebIDL#345</a> getting resolved properly.</p>
   <p class="note" role="note"><span>Note:</span> CSSMathValue, being a pure superclass,
cannot be directly constructed.
It exists solely to host the common attributes
of all the "math" operations.</p>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSMathValue.operator">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMathValue, CSSMathSum, CSSMathProduct, CSSMathMin, CSSMathMax, CSSMathNegate, CSSMathInvert" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" id="dom-cssmathvalue-operator"><code>operator</code></dfn> attribute
    of a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathvalue" id="ref-for-cssmathvalue-11">CSSMathValue</a></code> <var>this</var> must,
    on getting,
    return the following string,
    depending on the interface of <var>this</var>: 
    <dl class="switch">
     <dt data-md=""><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathsum" id="ref-for-cssmathsum-10">CSSMathSum</a></code>
     <dd data-md="">
      <p><code>"sum"</code></p>
     <dt data-md=""><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathproduct" id="ref-for-cssmathproduct-5">CSSMathProduct</a></code>
     <dd data-md="">
      <p><code>"product"</code></p>
     <dt data-md=""><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathmin" id="ref-for-cssmathmin-5">CSSMathMin</a></code>
     <dd data-md="">
      <p><code>"min"</code></p>
     <dt data-md=""><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathmax" id="ref-for-cssmathmax-5">CSSMathMax</a></code>
     <dd data-md="">
      <p><code>"max"</code></p>
     <dt data-md=""><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathnegate" id="ref-for-cssmathnegate-5">CSSMathNegate</a></code>
     <dd data-md="">
      <p><code>"negate"</code></p>
     <dt data-md=""><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathinvert" id="ref-for-cssmathinvert-5">CSSMathInvert</a></code>
     <dd data-md="">
      <p><code>"invert"</code></p>
    </dl>
    <p class="note" role="note"><span>Note:</span> These are all instances of the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#enumdef-cssmathoperator" id="ref-for-enumdef-cssmathoperator-2">CSSMathOperator</a></code> enum.</p>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSMathSum(...args)">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMathSum" data-dfn-type="constructor" data-export="" id="dom-cssmathsum-cssmathsum"><code>CSSMathSum(...<var>args</var>)</code></dfn> constructor must,
    when called,
    perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Replace each <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a> of <var>args</var> with the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#rectify-a-numberish-value" id="ref-for-rectify-a-numberish-value-8">rectifying a numberish value</a> for the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">item</a>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>args</var> <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-is-empty">is empty</a>, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#syntaxerror">SyntaxError</a></code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Let <var>type</var> be the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#add-two-types" id="ref-for-add-two-types-7">adding</a> the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-type-17">types</a> of all the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">items</a> of <var>args</var>.
If <var>type</var> is failure, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathsum" id="ref-for-cssmathsum-11">CSSMathSum</a></code> whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathsum-values" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathsum-values-6">values</a></code> internal slot
is set to <var>args</var>.</p>
    </ol>
    <p>The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMathMin" data-dfn-type="constructor" data-export="" id="dom-cssmathmin-cssmathmin"><code>CSSMathMin(...<var>args</var>)</code></dfn> and <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMathMax" data-dfn-type="constructor" data-export="" id="dom-cssmathmax-cssmathmax"><code>CSSMathMax(...<var>args</var>)</code></dfn> constructors
    are defined identically to the above,
    except that in the last step
    they return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathmin" id="ref-for-cssmathmin-6">CSSMathMin</a></code> or <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathmax" id="ref-for-cssmathmax-6">CSSMathMax</a></code> object,
    respectively.</p>
    <p>The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMathProduct" data-dfn-type="constructor" data-export="" id="dom-cssmathproduct-cssmathproduct"><code>CSSMathProduct(...<var>args</var>)</code></dfn> constructor
    is defined identically to the above,
    except that in step 3 it <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-multiply-two-types" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-multiply-two-types-3">multiplies</a> the types instead of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#add-two-types" id="ref-for-add-two-types-8">adding</a>,
    and in the last step
    it returns a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathproduct" id="ref-for-cssmathproduct-6">CSSMathProduct</a></code>.</p>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSMathNegate(arg)">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMathNegate" data-dfn-type="constructor" data-export="" id="dom-cssmathnegate-cssmathnegate"><code>CSSMathNegate(<var>arg</var>)</code></dfn> constructor must,
    when called,
    perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Replace <var>arg</var> with the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#rectify-a-numberish-value" id="ref-for-rectify-a-numberish-value-9">rectifying a numberish value</a> for <var>arg</var>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathnegate" id="ref-for-cssmathnegate-6">CSSMathNegate</a></code> whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathnegate-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathnegate-value-4">value</a></code> internal slot
is set to <var>arg</var>.</p>
    </ol>
    <p>The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMathInvert" data-dfn-type="constructor" data-export="" id="dom-cssmathinvert-cssmathinvert"><code>CSSMathInvert(<var>arg</var>)</code></dfn> constructor
    is defined identically to the above,
    except that in the last step
    it returns a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathinvert" id="ref-for-cssmathinvert-6">CSSMathInvert</a></code> object.</p>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="[=type=] of a CSSMathValue">
     The <dfn data-dfn-type="dfn" data-noexport="" id="type-of-a-cssmathvalue"><a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-type-18">type</a> of a CSSMathValue<a class="self-link" href="#type-of-a-cssmathvalue"></a></dfn> depends on its class: 
    <dl class="switch">
     <dt data-md=""><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathsum" id="ref-for-cssmathsum-12">CSSMathSum</a></code>
     <dt data-md=""><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathmin" id="ref-for-cssmathmin-7">CSSMathMin</a></code>
     <dt data-md=""><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathmax" id="ref-for-cssmathmax-7">CSSMathMax</a></code>
     <dd data-md="">
      <p>The <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-type-19">type</a> is the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#add-two-types" id="ref-for-add-two-types-9">adding</a> the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-type-20">types</a> of each of the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">items</a> in its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathsum-values" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathsum-values-7">values</a></code> internal slot.</p>
     <dt data-md=""><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathproduct" id="ref-for-cssmathproduct-7">CSSMathProduct</a></code>
     <dd data-md="">
      <p>The <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-type-21">type</a> is the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-multiply-two-types" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-multiply-two-types-4">multiplying</a> the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-type-22">types</a> of each of the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-item">items</a> in its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathproduct-values" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathproduct-values-4">values</a></code> internal slot.</p>
     <dt data-md=""><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathnegate" id="ref-for-cssmathnegate-7">CSSMathNegate</a></code>
     <dt data-md=""><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathinvert" id="ref-for-cssmathinvert-7">CSSMathInvert</a></code>
     <dd data-md="">
      <p>The <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-type-23">type</a> is the same as the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssnumericvalue-type" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-type-24">type</a> of its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathnegate-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathnegate-value-5">value</a></code> internal slot,
but with all <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#map-value">values</a> negated.</p>
    </dl>
   </div>
   <h4 class="heading settled" data-level="4.3.5" id="numeric-factory"><span class="secno">4.3.5. </span><span class="content">Numeric Factory Functions</span><a class="self-link" href="#numeric-factory"></a></h4>
   <p>The following factory functions can be used
to create new numeric values much less verbosely
than using the constructors directly.</p>
<pre class="idl highlight def"><span class="kt">partial</span> <span class="kt">namespace</span> <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="namespace">CSS</a> {

    <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-57">CSSUnitValue</a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSS" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" data-lt="dpi(value)" id="dom-css-dpi"><code>dpi</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-css-dpi"></a></dfn>(<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-double"><span class="kt">double</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSS/dpi(value)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-css-dpi-value-value"><code>value</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-css-dpi-value-value"></a></dfn>);
    <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-58">CSSUnitValue</a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSS" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" data-lt="dpcm(value)" id="dom-css-dpcm"><code>dpcm</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-css-dpcm"></a></dfn>(<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-double"><span class="kt">double</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSS/dpcm(value)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-css-dpcm-value-value"><code>value</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-css-dpcm-value-value"></a></dfn>);
    <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-59">CSSUnitValue</a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSS" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" data-lt="dppx(value)" id="dom-css-dppx"><code>dppx</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-css-dppx"></a></dfn>(<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-double"><span class="kt">double</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSS/dppx(value)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-css-dppx-value-value"><code>value</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-css-dppx-value-value"></a></dfn>);

    // &lt;flex>
    <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-60">CSSUnitValue</a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSS" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" data-lt="fr(value)" id="dom-css-fr"><code>fr</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-css-fr"></a></dfn>(<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-double"><span class="kt">double</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSS/fr(value)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-css-fr-value-value"><code>value</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-css-fr-value-value"></a></dfn>);
};
</pre>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSS.numeric">
     All of the above methods must,
    when called with a double <var>value</var>,
    return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-61">CSSUnitValue</a></code> whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-value-16">value</a></code> internal slot
    is set to <var>value</var> and whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-unit" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-unit-21">unit</a></code> internal slot
    is set to the name of the method as defined here. 
    <p class="note" role="note"><span>Note:</span> The unit used does not depend on the <em>current</em> name of the function,
    if it’s stored in another variable; <code>let foo = CSS.px; let val = foo(5);</code> does not return a <code>{value: 5, unit: "foo"}</code> <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-62">CSSUnitValue</a></code>.
    The above talk about names is just a shorthand
    to avoid defining the unit individually for all ~20 functions.</p>
   </div>
   <div class="example" id="example-9b45edcf">
    <a class="self-link" href="#example-9b45edcf"></a> For example, rather than creating a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csspositionvalue" id="ref-for-csspositionvalue-1">CSSPositionValue</a></code> with code like: 
<pre class="lang-js highlight"><span class="kd">let</span> pos <span class="o">=</span> <span class="k">new</span> CSSPositionValue<span class="p">(</span>
    <span class="k">new</span> CSSUnitValue<span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">5</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s2">"px"</span><span class="p">),</span>
    <span class="k">new</span> CSSUnitValue<span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">10</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s2">"px"</span><span class="p">));</span>
</pre>
    <p>One can instead write:</p>
<pre class="lang-js highlight"><span class="kd">let</span> pos <span class="o">=</span> <span class="k">new</span> CSSPositionValue<span class="p">(</span>CSS<span class="p">.</span>px<span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">5</span><span class="p">),</span> CSS<span class="p">.</span>px<span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">10</span><span class="p">));</span>
</pre>
   </div>
   <h3 class="heading settled" data-level="4.4" id="transformvalue-objects"><span class="secno">4.4. </span><span class="content"><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csstransformvalue" id="ref-for-csstransformvalue-1">CSSTransformValue</a></code> objects</span><a class="self-link" href="#transformvalue-objects"></a></h3>
   <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csstransformvalue" id="ref-for-csstransformvalue-2">CSSTransformValue</a></code> objects represent <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#typedef-transform-list">&lt;transform-list></a> values,
used by the <a class="property" data-link-type="propdesc" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#propdef-transform">transform</a> property.
They "contain" one or more <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csstransformcomponent" id="ref-for-csstransformcomponent-1">CSSTransformComponent</a></code>s,
which represent individual <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#typedef-transform-function">&lt;transform-function></a> values.</p>
<pre class="idl highlight def">[<a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="constructor" href="#dom-csstransformvalue-csstransformvalue" id="ref-for-dom-csstransformvalue-csstransformvalue-1">Constructor</a>(<span class="kt">optional</span> <span class="kt">sequence</span>&lt;<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#csstransformcomponent" id="ref-for-csstransformcomponent-2">CSSTransformComponent</a>> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSTransformValue/CSSTransformValue(transforms)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-csstransformvalue-csstransformvalue-transforms-transforms"><code>transforms</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-csstransformvalue-csstransformvalue-transforms-transforms"></a></dfn>)]
<span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="csstransformvalue"><code>CSSTransformValue</code></dfn> : <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-29">CSSStyleValue</a> {
    /*arraylike&lt;CSSTransformComponent>;*/
    <span class="kt">readonly</span> <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-boolean"><span class="kt">boolean</span></a> <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="attribute" data-readonly="" data-type="boolean" href="#dom-csstransformvalue-is2d" id="ref-for-dom-csstransformvalue-is2d-1">is2D</a>;
    <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/geometry-1/#dom-dommatrix">DOMMatrix</a> <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="method" href="#dom-csstransformvalue-tomatrix" id="ref-for-dom-csstransformvalue-tomatrix-1">toMatrix</a>();
};
</pre>
   <p class="issue" id="issue-74739362"><a class="self-link" href="#issue-74739362"></a> Assuming the resolution of <a href="https://github.com/heycam/webidl/issues/345">WebIDL#345</a> produces an "arraylike" declaration.</p>
   <p>A <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csstransformvalue" id="ref-for-csstransformvalue-3">CSSTransformValue</a></code>’s <a data-link-type="dfn">values to iterate over</a> is a <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list">list</a> of <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csstransformcomponent" id="ref-for-csstransformcomponent-3">CSSTransformComponent</a></code>s.</p>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSTransformValue(|transforms|)">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSTransformValue" data-dfn-type="constructor" data-export="" id="dom-csstransformvalue-csstransformvalue"><code>CSSTransformValue(<var>transforms</var>)</code></dfn> constructor must,
    when called,
    perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csstransformvalue" id="ref-for-csstransformvalue-4">CSSTransformValue</a></code> whose <a data-link-type="dfn">values to iterate over</a> is <var>transforms</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSTransformValue.is2D"> The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSTransformValue" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" id="dom-csstransformvalue-is2d"><code>is2D</code></dfn> attribute of a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csstransformvalue" id="ref-for-csstransformvalue-5">CSSTransformValue</a></code> <var>this</var> must,
    on getting,
    return <code>true</code> if, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-iterate">for each</a> <var>func</var> in <var>this</var>’s <a data-link-type="dfn">values to iterate over</a>,
    the <var>func</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d" id="ref-for-dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d-1">is2D</a></code> attribute would return <code>true</code>;
    otherwise,
    the attribute returns <code>false</code>. </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSTransformValue.toMatrix()">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSTransformValue" data-dfn-type="method" data-export="" id="dom-csstransformvalue-tomatrix"><code>toMatrix()</code></dfn> method of a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csstransformvalue" id="ref-for-csstransformvalue-6">CSSTransformValue</a></code> <var>this</var> must,
    when called,
    perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Let <var>matrix</var> be a 4x4 matrix,
initially set to the identity matrix.
Let <var>is2D</var> be a boolean initially set to <code>true</code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p><a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list-iterate">For each</a> <var>func</var> in <var>this</var>’s <a data-link-type="dfn">values to iterate over</a>:</p>
      <ol>
       <li data-md="">
        <p>Let <var>funcMatrix</var> be <var>func</var>’s equivalent 4x4 transform matrix,
as defined in <a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#mathematical-description">CSS Transforms 1 §21 Mathematical Description of Transform Functions</a>.</p>
        <p>As the entries of such a matrix are defined relative to the <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#px">px</a> unit,
if any <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#length-value" title="Expands to: em | vb | ch | cm | vh | vi | vw | ex | in | ic | pt | px | lh | pc | rem | rlh | vmax | advance measure | vmin | mm | cap | q">&lt;length></a>s in <var>func</var> involved in generating the matrix
are not <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#compatible-units">compatible units</a> with <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#px">px</a>, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code>.</p>
       <li data-md="">
        <p>Set <var>matrix</var> to the result of multiplying <var>matrix</var> and <var>funcMatrix</var>.</p>
       <li data-md="">
        <p>If <var>func</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d" id="ref-for-dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d-2">is2D</a></code> internal slot is <code>false</code>,
set <var>is2D</var> to <code>false</code>.</p>
      </ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/geometry-1/#dom-dommatrix">DOMMatrix</a></code> representing <var>matrix</var>,
and with its internal <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://drafts.fxtf.org/geometry-1/#matrix-is-2d">is 2D</a> flag set to <var>is2D</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
<pre class="idl highlight def"><span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="csstransformcomponent"><code>CSSTransformComponent</code></dfn> {
    <dfn class="kt" data-dfn-for="CSSTransformComponent" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-lt="stringification behavior" data-noexport="" id="CSSTransformComponent-stringification-behavior">stringifier<a class="self-link" href="#CSSTransformComponent-stringification-behavior"></a></dfn>;
    <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-boolean"><span class="kt">boolean</span></a> <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="attribute" data-type="boolean" href="#dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d" id="ref-for-dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d-3">is2D</a>;
};

[<a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="constructor" href="#dom-csstranslation-csstranslation" id="ref-for-dom-csstranslation-csstranslation-1">Constructor</a>(<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-42">CSSNumericValue</a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSTranslation/CSSTranslation(x, y, z)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-csstranslation-csstranslation-x-y-z-x"><code>x</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-csstranslation-csstranslation-x-y-z-x"></a></dfn>, <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-43">CSSNumericValue</a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSTranslation/CSSTranslation(x, y, z)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-csstranslation-csstranslation-x-y-z-y"><code>y</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-csstranslation-csstranslation-x-y-z-y"></a></dfn>, <span class="kt">optional</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-44">CSSNumericValue</a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSTranslation/CSSTranslation(x, y, z)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-csstranslation-csstranslation-x-y-z-z"><code>z</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-csstranslation-csstranslation-x-y-z-z"></a></dfn>)]
<span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="csstranslation"><code>CSSTranslation</code></dfn> : <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#csstransformcomponent" id="ref-for-csstransformcomponent-4">CSSTransformComponent</a> {
    <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-45">CSSNumericValue</a> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSTranslation" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" data-type="CSSNumericValue" id="dom-csstranslation-x"><code>x</code></dfn>;
    <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-46">CSSNumericValue</a> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSTranslation" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" data-type="CSSNumericValue" id="dom-csstranslation-y"><code>y</code></dfn>;
    <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-47">CSSNumericValue</a> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSTranslation" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" data-type="CSSNumericValue" id="dom-csstranslation-z"><code>z</code></dfn>;
};

[<a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="constructor" href="#dom-cssrotation-cssrotation" id="ref-for-dom-cssrotation-cssrotation-1">Constructor</a>(<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-48">CSSNumericValue</a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSRotation/CSSRotation(angle)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssrotation-cssrotation-angle-angle"><code>angle</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssrotation-cssrotation-angle-angle"></a></dfn>),
 <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="constructor" href="#dom-cssrotation-cssrotation-x-y-z-angle" id="ref-for-dom-cssrotation-cssrotation-x-y-z-angle-1">Constructor</a>(<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#typedefdef-cssnumberish" id="ref-for-typedefdef-cssnumberish-14">CSSNumberish</a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSRotation/CSSRotation(x, y, z, angle)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssrotation-cssrotation-x-y-z-angle-x"><code>x</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssrotation-cssrotation-x-y-z-angle-x"></a></dfn>, <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#typedefdef-cssnumberish" id="ref-for-typedefdef-cssnumberish-15">CSSNumberish</a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSRotation/CSSRotation(x, y, z, angle)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssrotation-cssrotation-x-y-z-angle-y"><code>y</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssrotation-cssrotation-x-y-z-angle-y"></a></dfn>, <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#typedefdef-cssnumberish" id="ref-for-typedefdef-cssnumberish-16">CSSNumberish</a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSRotation/CSSRotation(x, y, z, angle)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssrotation-cssrotation-x-y-z-angle-z"><code>z</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssrotation-cssrotation-x-y-z-angle-z"></a></dfn>, <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-49">CSSNumericValue</a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSRotation/CSSRotation(x, y, z, angle)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssrotation-cssrotation-x-y-z-angle-angle"><code>angle</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssrotation-cssrotation-x-y-z-angle-angle"></a></dfn>)]
<span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="cssrotation"><code>CSSRotation</code></dfn> : <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#csstransformcomponent" id="ref-for-csstransformcomponent-5">CSSTransformComponent</a> {
    <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#typedefdef-cssnumberish" id="ref-for-typedefdef-cssnumberish-17">CSSNumberish</a> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSRotation" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" data-type="CSSNumberish" id="dom-cssrotation-x"><code>x</code></dfn>;
    <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#typedefdef-cssnumberish" id="ref-for-typedefdef-cssnumberish-18">CSSNumberish</a> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSRotation" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" data-type="CSSNumberish" id="dom-cssrotation-y"><code>y</code></dfn>;
    <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#typedefdef-cssnumberish" id="ref-for-typedefdef-cssnumberish-19">CSSNumberish</a> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSRotation" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" data-type="CSSNumberish" id="dom-cssrotation-z"><code>z</code></dfn>;
    <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-50">CSSNumericValue</a> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSRotation" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" data-type="CSSNumericValue" id="dom-cssrotation-angle"><code>angle</code></dfn>;
};

[<a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="constructor" href="#dom-cssscale-cssscale" id="ref-for-dom-cssscale-cssscale-1">Constructor</a>(<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#typedefdef-cssnumberish" id="ref-for-typedefdef-cssnumberish-20">CSSNumberish</a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSScale/CSSScale(x, y, z)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssscale-cssscale-x-y-z-x"><code>x</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssscale-cssscale-x-y-z-x"></a></dfn>, <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#typedefdef-cssnumberish" id="ref-for-typedefdef-cssnumberish-21">CSSNumberish</a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSScale/CSSScale(x, y, z)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssscale-cssscale-x-y-z-y"><code>y</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssscale-cssscale-x-y-z-y"></a></dfn>, <span class="kt">optional</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#typedefdef-cssnumberish" id="ref-for-typedefdef-cssnumberish-22">CSSNumberish</a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSScale/CSSScale(x, y, z)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssscale-cssscale-x-y-z-z"><code>z</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssscale-cssscale-x-y-z-z"></a></dfn>)]
<span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="cssscale"><code>CSSScale</code></dfn> : <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#csstransformcomponent" id="ref-for-csstransformcomponent-6">CSSTransformComponent</a> {

[<a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="constructor" href="#dom-cssperspective-cssperspective" id="ref-for-dom-cssperspective-cssperspective-1">Constructor</a>(<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-55">CSSNumericValue</a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSPerspective/CSSPerspective(length)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssperspective-cssperspective-length-length"><code>length</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssperspective-cssperspective-length-length"></a></dfn>)]

[<a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="constructor" href="#dom-cssmatrixcomponent-cssmatrixcomponent" id="ref-for-dom-cssmatrixcomponent-cssmatrixcomponent-1">Constructor</a>(<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/geometry-1/#dom-dommatrixreadonly">DOMMatrixReadOnly</a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMatrixComponent/CSSMatrixComponent(matrix, options)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssmatrixcomponent-cssmatrixcomponent-matrix-options-matrix"><code>matrix</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssmatrixcomponent-cssmatrixcomponent-matrix-options-matrix"></a></dfn>, <span class="kt">optional</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#dictdef-cssmatrixcomponentoptions" id="ref-for-dictdef-cssmatrixcomponentoptions-1">CSSMatrixComponentOptions</a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMatrixComponent/CSSMatrixComponent(matrix, options)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssmatrixcomponent-cssmatrixcomponent-matrix-options-options"><code>options</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssmatrixcomponent-cssmatrixcomponent-matrix-options-options"></a></dfn>)]
<span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="cssmatrixcomponent"><code>CSSMatrixComponent</code></dfn> : <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#csstransformcomponent" id="ref-for-csstransformcomponent-9">CSSTransformComponent</a> {
    <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/geometry-1/#dom-dommatrix">DOMMatrix</a> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMatrixComponent" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" data-type="DOMMatrix" id="dom-cssmatrixcomponent-matrix"><code>matrix</code></dfn>;
};

<span class="kt">dictionary</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="dictionary" data-export="" id="dictdef-cssmatrixcomponentoptions"><code>CSSMatrixComponentOptions</code></dfn> {
    <a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-boolean"><span class="kt">boolean</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMatrixComponentOptions" data-dfn-type="dict-member" data-export="" data-type="boolean " id="dom-cssmatrixcomponentoptions-is2d"><code>is2D</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssmatrixcomponentoptions-is2d"></a></dfn>;
};
</pre>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSTransformComponent.is2D">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSTransformComponent" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" id="dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d"><code>is2D</code></dfn> attribute
    indicates whether the transform is 2D or 3D.
    When it’s <code>true</code>,
    the attributes of the transform that are relevant to 3D transforms
    (such as the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstranslation-z" id="ref-for-dom-csstranslation-z-1">CSSTranslation.z</a></code> attribute)
    simply have no effect on the transform they represent. 
    <p class="note" role="note"><span>Note:</span> This affects the serialization of the object,
    and concepts such as the object’s "equivalent 4x4 matrix".</p>
   </div>
   <details class="note">
    <summary><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d" id="ref-for-dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d-4">is2D</a></code> Design Considerations</summary>
    <p>For legacy reasons,
    2D and 3D transforms are distinct,
    even if they have identical effects;
    a <span class="css">translateZ(0px)</span> has observable effects on a page,
    even tho it’s defined to be an identity transform,
    as the UA activates some 3D-based optimizations for the element.</p>
    <p>There were several possible ways to reflect this—<wbr>nullable 3D-related attributes,
    separate 2D and 3D interfaces,
    etc—<wbr>but we chose the current design
    (an author-flippable switch that dictates the behavior)
    because it allows authors to,
    in most circumstances,
    operate on transforms without having to care whether they’re 2D or 3D,
    but also prevents "accidentally" flipping a 2D transform into becoming 3D.</p>
   </details>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSTranslation()">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSTranslation" data-dfn-type="constructor" data-export="" id="dom-csstranslation-csstranslation"><code>CSSTranslation(<var>x</var>, <var>y</var>, <var>z</var>)</code></dfn> constructor must,
    when invoked,
    perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>x</var>, <var>y</var>, or <var>z</var> (if passed)
don’t match <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#typedef-length-percentage">&lt;length-percentage></a>, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Let <var>this</var> be a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csstranslation" id="ref-for-csstranslation-1">CSSTranslation</a></code> object,
with its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstranslation-x" id="ref-for-dom-csstranslation-x-1">x</a></code> and <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstranslation-y" id="ref-for-dom-csstranslation-y-1">y</a></code> internal slots
set to <var>x</var> and <var>y</var>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>z</var> was passed,
set <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstranslation-z" id="ref-for-dom-csstranslation-z-2">z</a></code> internal slot
to <var>z</var>,
and set <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d" id="ref-for-dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d-5">is2D</a></code> internal slot
to <code>false</code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>z</var> was not passed,
set <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstranslation-z" id="ref-for-dom-csstranslation-z-3">z</a></code> internal slot
to <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#create-a-cssunitvalue-from-a-string" id="ref-for-create-a-cssunitvalue-from-a-string-2">new unit value</a> of <span class="css">0px</span>,
and set <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d" id="ref-for-dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d-6">is2D</a></code> internal slot
to <code>true</code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return <var>this</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSRotation(angle)">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSRotation" data-dfn-type="constructor" data-export="" id="dom-cssrotation-cssrotation"><code>CSSRotation(<var>angle</var>)</code></dfn> constructor must,
    when invoked,
    perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>angle</var> doesn’t match <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#angle-value" title="Expands to: turn | rad | grad | deg">&lt;angle></a>, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssrotation" id="ref-for-cssrotation-1">CSSRotation</a></code> with its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssrotation-angle" id="ref-for-dom-cssrotation-angle-1">angle</a></code> internal slot
set to <var>angle</var>,
its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssrotation-x" id="ref-for-dom-cssrotation-x-1">x</a></code> and <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssrotation-y" id="ref-for-dom-cssrotation-y-1">y</a></code> internal slots
set to <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#create-a-cssunitvalue-from-a-string" id="ref-for-create-a-cssunitvalue-from-a-string-3">new unit values</a> of <span class="css">0</span>,
its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssrotation-z" id="ref-for-dom-cssrotation-z-1">z</a></code> internal slot
set to a <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#create-a-cssunitvalue-from-a-string" id="ref-for-create-a-cssunitvalue-from-a-string-4">new unit value</a> of <span class="css">1</span>,
and its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d" id="ref-for-dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d-7">is2D</a></code> internal slot set to <code>true</code>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSRotation(x, y, z, angle)">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSRotation" data-dfn-type="constructor" data-export="" id="dom-cssrotation-cssrotation-x-y-z-angle"><code>CSSRotation(<var>x</var>, <var>y</var>, <var>z</var>, <var>angle</var>)</code></dfn> constructor must,
    when invoked,
    perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>angle</var> doesn’t match <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#angle-value" title="Expands to: turn | rad | grad | deg">&lt;angle></a>, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Let <var>x</var>, <var>y</var>, and <var>z</var> be replaced by the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#rectify-a-numberish-value" id="ref-for-rectify-a-numberish-value-10">rectifying a numberish value</a>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>x</var>, <var>y</var>, or <var>z</var> don’t match <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#number-value">&lt;number></a>, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssrotation" id="ref-for-cssrotation-2">CSSRotation</a></code> with its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssrotation-angle" id="ref-for-dom-cssrotation-angle-2">angle</a></code> internal slot
set to <var>angle</var>,
its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssrotation-x" id="ref-for-dom-cssrotation-x-2">x</a></code>, <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssrotation-y" id="ref-for-dom-cssrotation-y-2">y</a></code>, <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssrotation-z" id="ref-for-dom-cssrotation-z-2">z</a></code> internal slots set to <var>x</var>, <var>y</var>, and <var>z</var>,
and its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d" id="ref-for-dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d-8">is2D</a></code> internal slot set to <code>false</code>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSScale()">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSScale" data-dfn-type="constructor" data-export="" id="dom-cssscale-cssscale"><code>CSSScale(<var>x</var>, <var>y</var>, <var>z</var>)</code></dfn> constructor must,

    perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Let <var>x</var>, <var>y</var>, and <var>z</var> (if passed)
be replaced by the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#rectify-a-numberish-value" id="ref-for-rectify-a-numberish-value-11">rectifying a numberish value</a>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>x</var>, <var>y</var>, or <var>z</var> (if passed)
don’t match <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#number-value">&lt;number></a>, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Let <var>this</var> be a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssscale" id="ref-for-cssscale-1">CSSScale</a></code> object,
with its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssscale-x" id="ref-for-dom-cssscale-x-1">x</a></code> and <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssscale-y" id="ref-for-dom-cssscale-y-1">y</a></code> internal slots

     <li data-md="">

     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>z</var> was not passed,
set <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssscale-z" id="ref-for-dom-cssscale-z-2">z</a></code> internal slot
to a <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#create-a-cssunitvalue-from-a-string" id="ref-for-create-a-cssunitvalue-from-a-string-5">new unit value</a> of <span class="css">1</span>,
and set <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d" id="ref-for-dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d-10">is2D</a></code> internal slot to <code>true</code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return <var>this</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSSkew()">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSSkew" data-dfn-type="constructor" data-export="" id="dom-cssskew-cssskew"><code>CSSSkew(<var>ax</var>, <var>ay</var>)</code></dfn> constructor must,

    perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>ax</var> or <var>ay</var> do not match <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#angle-value" title="Expands to: turn | rad | grad | deg">&lt;angle></a>, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssskew" id="ref-for-cssskew-1">CSSSkew</a></code> object
with its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssskew-ax" id="ref-for-dom-cssskew-ax-1">ax</a></code> and <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssskew-ay" id="ref-for-dom-cssskew-ay-1">ay</a></code> internal slots
set to <var>ax</var> and <var>ay</var>,
and its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d" id="ref-for-dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d-11">is2D</a></code> internal slot set to <code>true</code>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSSkew.is2D">
     The <dfn class="idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSSkew" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" id="dom-cssskew-is2d"><code>is2D</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssskew-is2d"></a></dfn> attribute of a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssskew" id="ref-for-cssskew-2">CSSSkew</a></code> object must,
    on setting,
    do nothing. 
    <p class="note" role="note"><span>Note:</span> <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#funcdef-skew">skew()</a> functions always represent 2D transforms.</p>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSPerspective()">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSPerspective" data-dfn-type="constructor" data-export="" id="dom-cssperspective-cssperspective"><code>CSSPerspective(<var>length</var>)</code></dfn> constructor must,
    when invoked,
    perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>length</var> does not match <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#length-value" title="Expands to: em | vb | ch | cm | vh | vi | vw | ex | in | ic | pt | px | lh | pc | rem | rlh | vmax | advance measure | vmin | mm | cap | q">&lt;length></a>, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssperspective" id="ref-for-cssperspective-1">CSSPerspective</a></code> object
with its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssperspective-length" id="ref-for-dom-cssperspective-length-1">length</a></code> internal slot
set to <var>length</var>,
and its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d" id="ref-for-dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d-12">is2D</a></code> internal slot set to <code>false</code>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSPerspective.is2D">
     The <dfn class="idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSPerspective" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" id="dom-cssperspective-is2d"><code>is2D</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssperspective-is2d"></a></dfn> attribute of a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssperspective" id="ref-for-cssperspective-2">CSSPerspective</a></code> object must,
    on setting,
    do nothing. 
    <p class="note" role="note"><span>Note:</span> <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-transforms-2/#funcdef-perspective">perspective()</a> functions always represent 3D transforms.</p>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSMatrixComponent()">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSMatrixComponent" data-dfn-type="constructor" data-export="" id="dom-cssmatrixcomponent-cssmatrixcomponent"><code>CSSMatrixComponent(<var>matrix</var>, <var>options</var>)</code></dfn> constructor must,
    when invoked,
    perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Let <var>this</var> be a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmatrixcomponent" id="ref-for-cssmatrixcomponent-1">CSSMatrixComponent</a></code> object
with its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmatrixcomponent-matrix" id="ref-for-dom-cssmatrixcomponent-matrix-1">matrix</a></code> internal slot
set to <var>matrix</var>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>options</var> was passed
and has a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dictdef-cssmatrixcomponentoptions" id="ref-for-dictdef-cssmatrixcomponentoptions-2">CSSMatrixComponentOptions</a></code> field,
set <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstransformvalue-is2d" id="ref-for-dom-csstransformvalue-is2d-2">is2D</a></code> internal slot
to the value of that field.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Otherwise,
set <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstransformvalue-is2d" id="ref-for-dom-csstransformvalue-is2d-3">is2D</a></code> internal slot
to the value of <var>matrix</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/geometry-1/#dom-dommatrixreadonly-is2d">is2D</a></code> internal slot.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return <var>this</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="note" role="note">
     Each <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csstransformcomponent" id="ref-for-csstransformcomponent-10">CSSTransformComponent</a></code> can correspond to
    one of a number of underlying transform functions.
    For example, a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csstranslation" id="ref-for-csstranslation-2">CSSTranslation</a></code> with an x value of <span class="css">10px</span> and y &amp; z values of <span class="css">0px</span> could represent any of the following: 
    <ul>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>translate(10px)</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>translate(10px, 0)</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>translateX(10px)</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>translate3d(10px, 0, 0)</p>
    </ul>
    <p>When stringified, however,
    it will always print out either <span class="css">translate(10px, 0px)</span> or <span class="css">translate3d(10px, 0px, 0px)</span>,
    depending on whether its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d" id="ref-for-dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d-13">is2D</a></code> internal slot
    is <code>true</code> or <code>false</code>,
    respectively.</p>
   </div>
   <h3 class="heading settled" data-level="4.5" id="positionvalue-objects"><span class="secno">4.5. </span><span class="content"><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csspositionvalue" id="ref-for-csspositionvalue-2">CSSPositionValue</a></code> objects</span><a class="self-link" href="#positionvalue-objects"></a></h3>
   <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csspositionvalue" id="ref-for-csspositionvalue-3">CSSPositionValue</a></code> objects represent <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#typedef-position">&lt;position></a> values,
used by properties such as <a class="property" data-link-type="propdesc" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-images/#object-position">object-position</a>.</p>
<pre class="idl highlight def">[<a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="constructor" href="#dom-csspositionvalue-csspositionvalue" id="ref-for-dom-csspositionvalue-csspositionvalue-1">Constructor</a>(<a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-57">CSSNumericValue</a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSPositionValue/CSSPositionValue(x, y)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-csspositionvalue-csspositionvalue-x-y-x"><code>x</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-csspositionvalue-csspositionvalue-x-y-x"></a></dfn>, <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-58">CSSNumericValue</a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSPositionValue/CSSPositionValue(x, y)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-csspositionvalue-csspositionvalue-x-y-y"><code>y</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-csspositionvalue-csspositionvalue-x-y-y"></a></dfn>)]
<span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="csspositionvalue"><code>CSSPositionValue</code></dfn> : <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-30">CSSStyleValue</a> {
    <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-59">CSSNumericValue</a> <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="attribute" data-type="CSSNumericValue" href="#dom-csspositionvalue-x" id="ref-for-dom-csspositionvalue-x-1">x</a>;
    <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-60">CSSNumericValue</a> <a class="nv idl-code" data-link-type="attribute" data-type="CSSNumericValue" href="#dom-csspositionvalue-y" id="ref-for-dom-csspositionvalue-y-1">y</a>;
};
</pre>
   <p>The <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csspositionvalue-x" id="ref-for-dom-csspositionvalue-x-2">x</a></code> attribute expresses the offset from the left edge of the container. <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csspositionvalue-y" id="ref-for-dom-csspositionvalue-y-2">y</a></code> expressions the offset from the top edge of the container.</p>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSPositionValue(|x|, |y|)">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSPositionValue" data-dfn-type="constructor" data-export="" id="dom-csspositionvalue-csspositionvalue"><code>CSSPositionValue(<var>x</var>, <var>y</var>)</code></dfn> constructor must,
    when called,
    perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>x</var> or <var>y</var> doesn’t match <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#typedef-length-percentage">&lt;length-percentage></a>, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Otherwise, return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csspositionvalue" id="ref-for-csspositionvalue-4">CSSPositionValue</a></code> whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csspositionvalue-x" id="ref-for-dom-csspositionvalue-x-3">x</a></code> internal slot is set to <var>x</var>,
and whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csspositionvalue-y" id="ref-for-dom-csspositionvalue-y-3">y</a></code> internal slot is set to <var>y</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="CSSPositionValue.x">
     The <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSPositionValue" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" id="dom-csspositionvalue-x"><code>x</code></dfn> and <dfn class="dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSPositionValue" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" id="dom-csspositionvalue-y"><code>y</code></dfn> attribute of a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csspositionvalue" id="ref-for-csspositionvalue-5">CSSPositionValue</a></code> <var>this</var> must,
    on setting a value <var>value</var>,
    perform the following steps: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>value</var> doesn’t match <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#typedef-length-percentage">&lt;length-percentage></a>, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#dfn-throw">throw</a> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#exceptiondef-typeerror">TypeError</a></code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Otherwise, set <var>this</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csspositionvalue-x" id="ref-for-dom-csspositionvalue-x-4">x</a></code> or <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csspositionvalue-y" id="ref-for-dom-csspositionvalue-y-4">y</a></code> internal slot,
as appropriate,
to <var>value</var>.</p>
    </ol>
    <p>On reading, the attributes must return the value of the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csspositionvalue-x" id="ref-for-dom-csspositionvalue-x-5">x</a></code> or <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csspositionvalue-y" id="ref-for-dom-csspositionvalue-y-5">y</a></code> internal slot,
        as appropriate.</p>
   </div>
   <div class="example" id="example-20dff8ec">
    <a class="self-link" href="#example-20dff8ec"></a> <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#typedef-position">&lt;position></a> values accept a complicated combination of keywords and values,
    but in the Typed OM are always simplified to just two offsets.
    For example, the following style sheet: 
<pre class="lang-css highlight"><span class="nt">.example </span><span class="p">{</span>
    <span class="k">object-position</span><span class="p">:</span> center bottom <span class="m">10</span><span class="l">px</span><span class="p">;</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre>
    <p>Will produce the following behavior:</p>
<pre class="lang-javascript highlight"><span class="kd">let</span> map <span class="o">=</span> document<span class="p">.</span>querySelector<span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">'.example'</span><span class="p">).</span>styleMap<span class="p">;</span>

map<span class="p">.</span>get<span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">'object-position'</span><span class="p">).</span>x<span class="p">;</span>
<span class="c1">// CSS.percent(50)</span>
<span class="c1"></span>
map<span class="p">.</span>get<span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">'object-position'</span><span class="p">).</span>y<span class="p">;</span>
<span class="c1">// CSSMathSum(CSS.percent(100), CSS.px(-10))</span>
</pre>
   </div>
   <h3 class="heading settled" data-level="4.6" id="resourcevalue-objects"><span class="secno">4.6. </span><span class="content"><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssresourcevalue" id="ref-for-cssresourcevalue-1">CSSResourceValue</a></code> objects</span><a class="self-link" href="#resourcevalue-objects"></a></h3>
<pre class="idl highlight def"><span class="kt">enum</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="enum" data-export="" id="enumdef-cssresourcestate"><code>CSSResourceState</code></dfn> {<dfn class="s idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSResourceState" data-dfn-type="enum-value" data-export="" data-lt="&quot;unloaded&quot;|unloaded" id="dom-cssresourcestate-unloaded"><code>"unloaded"</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssresourcestate-unloaded"></a></dfn>, <dfn class="s idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSResourceState" data-dfn-type="enum-value" data-export="" data-lt="&quot;loading&quot;|loading" id="dom-cssresourcestate-loading"><code>"loading"</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssresourcestate-loading"></a></dfn>, <dfn class="s idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSResourceState" data-dfn-type="enum-value" data-export="" data-lt="&quot;loaded&quot;|loaded" id="dom-cssresourcestate-loaded"><code>"loaded"</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssresourcestate-loaded"></a></dfn>, <dfn class="s idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSResourceState" data-dfn-type="enum-value" data-export="" data-lt="&quot;error&quot;|error" id="dom-cssresourcestate-error"><code>"error"</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssresourcestate-error"></a></dfn>};

<span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="cssresourcevalue"><code>CSSResourceValue</code></dfn> : <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-31">CSSStyleValue</a> {
    <span class="kt">readonly</span> <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#enumdef-cssresourcestate" id="ref-for-enumdef-cssresourcestate-1">CSSResourceState</a> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSResourceValue" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" data-readonly="" data-type="CSSResourceState" id="dom-cssresourcevalue-state"><code>state</code></dfn>;
};

</pre>
   <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssresourcevalue" id="ref-for-cssresourcevalue-2">CSSResourceValue</a></code> objects represent CSS values that may require an asynchronous network fetch
before being usable.</p>
   <p>A <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssresourcevalue" id="ref-for-cssresourcevalue-3">CSSResourceValue</a></code> is in one of the following states, as reflected in the value of the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssresourcevalue-state" id="ref-for-dom-cssresourcevalue-state-1">state</a></code> attribute:</p>
   <dl>
    <dt data-md="">"unloaded"
    <dd data-md="">
     <p>The resource is not ready and is not actively being fetched</p>
    <dt data-md="">"loading"
    <dd data-md="">
     <p>The resource is not ready, but is in the process of being fetched</p>
    <dt data-md="">"loaded"
    <dd data-md="">
     <p>The resource is ready for rendering</p>
    <dt data-md="">"error"
    <dd data-md="">
     <p>The resource can’t be fetched, or the fetched resource is invalid</p>
   </dl>
   <div class="example" id="example-d42ec2e6"><a class="self-link" href="#example-d42ec2e6"></a> For example, images that match the <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#url-value">&lt;url></a> production can be used immediately, but will not result
in a visual change until the image data is fetched. <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssresourcevalue" id="ref-for-cssresourcevalue-4">CSSResourceValue</a></code> objects represent this by
providing values that track loaded state via the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#enumdef-cssresourcestate" id="ref-for-enumdef-cssresourcestate-2">CSSResourceState</a></code> enum. </div>
   <div class="issue no-marker" id="issue-c8cb3cfb"><a class="self-link" href="#issue-c8cb3cfb"></a><a class="marker" href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues/186" style="text-transform:none">w3c/css-houdini-drafts/186</a><a href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues/186">[css-worklets] [css-typed-om] CSSResourceValues constructed within Worklets should have state "unloaded".</a></div>
   <h3 class="heading settled" data-level="4.7" id="imagevalue-objects"><span class="secno">4.7. </span><span class="content"><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssimagevalue" id="ref-for-cssimagevalue-1">CSSImageValue</a></code> objects</span><a class="self-link" href="#imagevalue-objects"></a></h3>
<pre class="idl highlight def"><span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="cssimagevalue"><code>CSSImageValue</code></dfn> : <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssresourcevalue" id="ref-for-cssresourcevalue-5">CSSResourceValue</a> {
    <span class="kt">readonly</span> <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-double"><span class="kt">double</span></a>? <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSImageValue" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" data-readonly="" data-type="double?" id="dom-cssimagevalue-intrinsicwidth"><code>intrinsicWidth</code></dfn>;
    <span class="kt">readonly</span> <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-double"><span class="kt">double</span></a>? <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSImageValue" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" data-readonly="" data-type="double?" id="dom-cssimagevalue-intrinsicheight"><code>intrinsicHeight</code></dfn>;
    <span class="kt">readonly</span> <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-double"><span class="kt">double</span></a>? <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSImageValue" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" data-readonly="" data-type="double?" id="dom-cssimagevalue-intrinsicratio"><code>intrinsicRatio</code></dfn>;
};

[<dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSURLImageValue" data-dfn-type="constructor" data-export="" data-lt="CSSURLImageValue(url)" id="dom-cssurlimagevalue-cssurlimagevalue"><code>Constructor</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssurlimagevalue-cssurlimagevalue"></a></dfn>(<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-USVString"><span class="kt">USVString</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSURLImageValue/CSSURLImageValue(url)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssurlimagevalue-cssurlimagevalue-url-url"><code>url</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssurlimagevalue-cssurlimagevalue-url-url"></a></dfn>)]
<span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="cssurlimagevalue"><code>CSSURLImageValue</code></dfn> : <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssimagevalue" id="ref-for-cssimagevalue-2">CSSImageValue</a> {
    <span class="kt">readonly</span> <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-USVString"><span class="kt">USVString</span></a> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSURLImageValue" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" data-readonly="" data-type="USVString" id="dom-cssurlimagevalue-url"><code>url</code></dfn>;
};

</pre>
   <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssimagevalue" id="ref-for-cssimagevalue-3">CSSImageValue</a></code> objects represent values for properties that take <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-images/#image-type">&lt;image></a> productions,
for example <a class="property" data-link-type="propdesc" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-background/#background-image">background-image</a>, <a class="property" data-link-type="propdesc" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-lists-3/#propdef-list-style-image">list-style-image</a>, and <a class="property" data-link-type="propdesc" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-background/#border-image-source">border-image-source</a>.</p>
   <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssimagevalue" id="ref-for-cssimagevalue-4">CSSImageValue</a></code> objects that do not require network data (for example linear and radial gradients)
are initialized with <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssresourcevalue-state" id="ref-for-dom-cssresourcevalue-state-2">state</a></code> "loaded".</p>
   <p>If the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssimagevalue" id="ref-for-cssimagevalue-5">CSSImageValue</a></code>'s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssresourcevalue-state" id="ref-for-dom-cssresourcevalue-state-3">state</a></code> is "loaded",
and the resource has an intrinsic width, height, or aspect ratio,
then <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssimagevalue-intrinsicwidth" id="ref-for-dom-cssimagevalue-intrinsicwidth-1">intrinsicWidth</a></code>, <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssimagevalue-intrinsicheight" id="ref-for-dom-cssimagevalue-intrinsicheight-1">intrinsicHeight</a></code>, and <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssimagevalue-intrinsicratio" id="ref-for-dom-cssimagevalue-intrinsicratio-1">intrinsicRatio</a></code> must reflect the resource’s corresponding value.
In all other cases, the attributes must be <code>null</code>.</p>
   <p class="issue" id="issue-645e7b87"><a class="self-link" href="#issue-645e7b87"></a> Does the loading lifecycle need to be described here?</p>
   <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssurlimagevalue" id="ref-for-cssurlimagevalue-1">CSSURLImageValue</a></code> objects represent <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssimagevalue" id="ref-for-cssimagevalue-6">CSSImageValue</a></code>s that match the <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#url-value">&lt;url></a> production. For these
objects, the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssurlimagevalue-url" id="ref-for-dom-cssurlimagevalue-url-1">url</a></code> attribute contains the URL that references the image.</p>
   <h3 class="heading settled" data-level="4.8" id="fontfacevalue-objects"><span class="secno">4.8. </span><span class="content"><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssfontfacevalue" id="ref-for-cssfontfacevalue-1">CSSFontFaceValue</a></code> objects</span><a class="self-link" href="#fontfacevalue-objects"></a></h3>
<pre class="idl highlight def">[<dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSFontFaceValue" data-dfn-type="constructor" data-export="" data-lt="CSSFontFaceValue(fontFamilyName)" id="dom-cssfontfacevalue-cssfontfacevalue"><code>Constructor</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssfontfacevalue-cssfontfacevalue"></a></dfn>(<a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a> <dfn class="nv idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSFontFaceValue/CSSFontFaceValue(fontFamilyName)" data-dfn-type="argument" data-export="" id="dom-cssfontfacevalue-cssfontfacevalue-fontfamilyname-fontfamilyname"><code>fontFamilyName</code><a class="self-link" href="#dom-cssfontfacevalue-cssfontfacevalue-fontfamilyname-fontfamilyname"></a></dfn>)]
<span class="kt">interface</span> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-type="interface" data-export="" id="cssfontfacevalue"><code>CSSFontFaceValue</code></dfn> : <a class="n" data-link-type="idl-name" href="#cssresourcevalue" id="ref-for-cssresourcevalue-6">CSSResourceValue</a> {
    <span class="kt">readonly</span> <span class="kt">attribute</span> <a class="n idl-code" data-link-type="interface" href="https://heycam.github.io/webidl/#idl-DOMString"><span class="kt">DOMString</span></a> <dfn class="nv dfn-paneled idl-code" data-dfn-for="CSSFontFaceValue" data-dfn-type="attribute" data-export="" data-readonly="" data-type="DOMString" id="dom-cssfontfacevalue-fontfamilyname"><code>fontFamilyName</code></dfn>;
};

</pre>
   <div class="issue no-marker" id="issue-ca05412c"><a class="self-link" href="#issue-ca05412c"></a><a class="marker" href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues/293" style="text-transform:none">w3c/css-houdini-drafts/293</a><a href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues/293">[CSS Typed OM] CSSFontFaceValue objects can't store source value</a></div>
   <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssfontfacevalue" id="ref-for-cssfontfacevalue-2">CSSFontFaceValue</a></code> objects are opaque representations of the contents of
@font-face rules. They are used to pass font information into <a data-link-type="dfn">paint image definition</a>s,
