via <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-variables-1/#custom-property">custom properties</a>.</p>
   <p>As font data may need to be fetched from a remote source, <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssfontfacevalue" id="ref-for-cssfontfacevalue-3">CSSFontFaceValue</a></code> is a subclass
of <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssresourcevalue" id="ref-for-cssresourcevalue-7">CSSResourceValue</a></code>.</p>
   <div class="issue no-marker" id="issue-0dc92981"><a class="self-link" href="#issue-0dc92981"></a><a class="marker" href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues/159" style="text-transform:none">w3c/css-houdini-drafts/159</a><a href="https://github.com/w3c/css-houdini-drafts/issues/159">[css-typed-om] Spec up ColorValue</a></div>
   <h2 class="heading settled" data-level="5" id="stylevalue-normalization"><span class="secno">5. </span><span class="content"><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-32">CSSStyleValue</a></code> normalization</span><a class="self-link" href="#stylevalue-normalization"></a></h2>
   <p>This section describes how Typed OM objects are constructed from CSS values.</p>
   <p>If a property’s grammar is more complex than one of the types listed here,
it produces a raw <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-33">CSSStyleValue</a></code>,
with a <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#CSSStyleValue-stringification-behavior" id="ref-for-CSSStyleValue-stringification-behavior-2">stringification behavior</a> that produces the CSSOM serialization of the property.</p>
   <p class="issue" id="issue-7d42ebb7"><a class="self-link" href="#issue-7d42ebb7"></a> Better to define a full table of properties and what types they normalize to.</p>
   <p class="issue" id="issue-085de778"><a class="self-link" href="#issue-085de778"></a> Per F2F, "CSSOM serialization" isn’t well-defined/interoperable enough.
We instead need to strictly define the serialization of every property.
This should be done according to CSSOM principlies, tho
(generally, shortest possible value).</p>
   <h3 class="heading settled" data-level="5.1" id="normalize-tokens"><span class="secno">5.1. </span><span class="content">Raw CSS tokens: properties with <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-variables-1/#funcdef-var">var()</a> references</span><a class="self-link" href="#normalize-tokens"></a></h3>
   <p>Regardless of what the property’s grammar is otherwise,
a property value with an un-substituted <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-variables-1/#funcdef-var">var()</a> reference
is represented as a <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#list">list</a> of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-syntax-3/#component-value">component values</a>,
which becomes a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunparsedvalue" id="ref-for-cssunparsedvalue-6">CSSUnparsedValue</a></code> in the Typed OM.</p>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="normalize a list of component values">
     To <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-export="" id="normalize-a-list-of-component-values">normalize a list of component values</dfn> from a <var>list</var>: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Replace all <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-variables-1/#funcdef-var">var()</a> references in <var>list</var> with <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssvariablereferencevalue" id="ref-for-cssvariablereferencevalue-5">CSSVariableReferenceValue</a></code> objects,
as described in <a href="#normalize-var">§5.2 var() References</a>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Replace each remaining maximal subsequence of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-syntax-3/#component-value">component values</a> in <var>list</var> with a single string of their concatenated serializations.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunparsedvalue" id="ref-for-cssunparsedvalue-7">CSSUnparsedValue</a></code> whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunparsedvalue-tokens-slot" id="ref-for-dom-cssunparsedvalue-tokens-slot-1">[[tokens]]</a></code> slot is set to <var>list</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="example" id="example-a92ed1a9">
    <a class="self-link" href="#example-a92ed1a9"></a> The string "calc(42px + var(--foo, 15em) + var(--bar, var(--far) + 15px))"
is converted into a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunparsedvalue" id="ref-for-cssunparsedvalue-8">CSSUnparsedValue</a></code> that contains a sequence with: 
    <ul>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>the string "calc(42px + "</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssvariablereferencevalue" id="ref-for-cssvariablereferencevalue-6">CSSVariableReferenceValue</a></code> with:</p>
      <ul>
       <li data-md="">
        <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssvariablereferencevalue-variable" id="ref-for-dom-cssvariablereferencevalue-variable-1">variable</a></code> "--foo"</p>
       <li data-md="">
        <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssvariablereferencevalue-fallback" id="ref-for-dom-cssvariablereferencevalue-fallback-1">fallback</a></code> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunparsedvalue" id="ref-for-cssunparsedvalue-9">CSSUnparsedValue</a></code> with a single-valued sequence containing " 15em"</p>
      </ul>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>the string " + "</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssvariablereferencevalue" id="ref-for-cssvariablereferencevalue-7">CSSVariableReferenceValue</a></code> with:</p>
      <ul>
       <li data-md="">
        <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssvariablereferencevalue-variable" id="ref-for-dom-cssvariablereferencevalue-variable-2">variable</a></code> "--bar"</p>
       <li data-md="">
        <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssvariablereferencevalue-fallback" id="ref-for-dom-cssvariablereferencevalue-fallback-2">fallback</a></code> a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunparsedvalue" id="ref-for-cssunparsedvalue-10">CSSUnparsedValue</a></code> with a sequence containing:</p>
        <ul>
         <li data-md="">
          <p>the string " "</p>
         <li data-md="">
          <p>a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssvariablereferencevalue" id="ref-for-cssvariablereferencevalue-8">CSSVariableReferenceValue</a></code> with</p>
          <ul>
           <li data-md="">
            <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssvariablereferencevalue-variable" id="ref-for-dom-cssvariablereferencevalue-variable-3">variable</a></code> "--far"</p>
           <li data-md="">
            <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssvariablereferencevalue-fallback" id="ref-for-dom-cssvariablereferencevalue-fallback-3">fallback</a></code> null</p>
          </ul>
         <li data-md="">
          <p>the string " + 15px"</p>
        </ul>
      </ul>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>the string ")"</p>
    </ul>
   </div>
   <h3 class="heading settled" data-level="5.2" id="normalize-var"><span class="secno">5.2. </span><span class="content"><a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-variables-1/#funcdef-var">var()</a> References</span><a class="self-link" href="#normalize-var"></a></h3>
   <p><a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-variables-1/#funcdef-var">var()</a> references become <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssvariablereferencevalue" id="ref-for-cssvariablereferencevalue-9">CSSVariableReferenceValue</a></code>s in the Typed OM.</p>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="normalize a var() reference">
     To <dfn data-dfn-type="dfn" data-export="" id="normalize-a-var-reference">normalize a <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-variables-1/#funcdef-var">var()</a> reference<a class="self-link" href="#normalize-a-var-reference"></a></dfn> <var>var</var>: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Let <var>object</var> be a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssvariablereferencevalue" id="ref-for-cssvariablereferencevalue-10">CSSVariableReferenceValue</a></code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Set <var>object</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssvariablereferencevalue-variable" id="ref-for-dom-cssvariablereferencevalue-variable-4">variable</a></code> internal slot
to the serialization of the <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#identifier-value">&lt;custom-ident></a> providing the variable name.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>var</var> has a fallback value,
set <var>object</var>’s <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssvariablereferencevalue-fallback" id="ref-for-dom-cssvariablereferencevalue-fallback-4">fallback</a></code> internal slot
to the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#normalize-a-list-of-component-values" id="ref-for-normalize-a-list-of-component-values-1">normalizing the fallback’s component values</a>.
Otherwise,
set it to <code>null</code>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return <var>object</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <h3 class="heading settled" data-level="5.3" id="normalize-ident"><span class="secno">5.3. </span><span class="content"><a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-syntax-3/#identifier">Identifier</a> Values</span><a class="self-link" href="#normalize-ident"></a></h3>
   <p>CSS <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-syntax-3/#identifier">identifiers</a> become <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csskeywordvalue" id="ref-for-csskeywordvalue-10">CSSKeywordValue</a></code>s in the Typed OM.</p>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="normalize an [=identifier=]">
     To <dfn data-dfn-type="dfn" data-export="" id="normalize-an-identifier">normalize an <a data-link-type="dfn" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-syntax-3/#identifier">identifier</a><a class="self-link" href="#normalize-an-identifier"></a></dfn> <var>ident</var>: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csskeywordvalue" id="ref-for-csskeywordvalue-11">CSSKeywordValue</a></code> with its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csskeywordvalue-value" id="ref-for-dom-csskeywordvalue-value-4">value</a></code> internal slot
set to the serialization of <var>ident</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <h3 class="heading settled" data-level="5.4" id="normalize-numeric"><span class="secno">5.4. </span><span class="content"><a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#number-value">&lt;number></a>, <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#percentage-value">&lt;percentage></a>, and <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#typedef-dimension">&lt;dimension></a> values</span><a class="self-link" href="#normalize-numeric"></a></h3>
   <p>CSS <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#number-value">&lt;number></a>, <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#percentage-value">&lt;percentage></a>, and <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#typedef-dimension">&lt;dimension></a> values become <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-61">CSSNumericValue</a></code>s in the Typed OM.</p>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="normalize a numeric value">
     To <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-export="" id="normalize-a-numeric-value">normalize a numeric value</dfn> <var>num</var>: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>num</var> is a <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#funcdef-calc">calc()</a>, <span class="css">min()</span>, or <span class="css">max()</span> expression, <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssmath-normalize-a-math-expression" id="ref-for-cssmath-normalize-a-math-expression-1">normalize a math expression</a> from <var>num</var> and return the result.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>num</var> is the unitless value <span class="css">0</span> and <var>num</var> is a <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#typedef-dimension">&lt;dimension></a>,
return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-63">CSSUnitValue</a></code> with its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-value-17">value</a></code> internal slot
set to 0,
and its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-unit" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-unit-22">unit</a></code> internal slot
set to "px".</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-64">CSSUnitValue</a></code> with its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-value-18">value</a></code> internal slot
set to the numeric value of <var>num</var>,
and its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-unit" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-unit-23">unit</a></code> internal slot
set to "number" if <var>num</var> is a <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#number-value">&lt;number></a>,
"percent" if <var>num</var> is a <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#percentage-value">&lt;percentage></a>,
and <var>num</var>’s unit if <var>num</var> is a <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#typedef-dimension">&lt;dimension></a>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="normalize a math expression">
     To <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-for="CSSMath" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-export="" data-local-lt="normalize" id="cssmath-normalize-a-math-expression">normalize a math expression</dfn> <var>num</var>: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>If <var>num</var> is a <span class="css">min()</span> or <span class="css">max()</span> expression:</p>
      <ol>
       <li data-md="">
        <p>Let <var>values</var> be the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#cssmath-normalize-a-math-expression" id="ref-for-cssmath-normalize-a-math-expression-2">normalizing</a> the arguments to the expression,
treating each argument as if it were the contents of a <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#funcdef-calc">calc()</a> expression.</p>
       <li data-md="">
        <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathmin" id="ref-for-cssmathmin-8">CSSMathMin</a></code> or <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathmax" id="ref-for-cssmathmax-8">CSSMathMax</a></code> object, respectively,
with its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathmin-values" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathmin-values-4">values</a></code> internal slot
set to <var>values</var>.</p>
      </ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p class="assertion">Assert: Otherwise, <var>num</var> is a <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#funcdef-calc">calc()</a>.</p>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Turn <var>num</var>’s argument
into an expression tree
using standard PEMDAS precedence rules,
with the following exceptions/clarification:</p>
      <ul>
       <li data-md="">
        <p>Treat subtraction as instead being addition,
with the RHS argument instead wrapped in a special "negate" node.</p>
       <li data-md="">
        <p>Treat division as instead being multiplication,
with the RHS argument instead wrapped in a special "invert" node.</p>
       <li data-md="">
        <p>Addition and multiplication are N-ary;
each node can have any number of arguments.</p>
       <li data-md="">
        <p>If an expression has only a single value in it,
and no operation,
treat it as an addition node with the single argument.</p>
      </ul>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Recursively transform the expression tree into objects,
as follows:</p>
      <dl class="switch">
       <dt data-md="">addition node
       <dd data-md="">
        <p>becomes a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathsum" id="ref-for-cssmathsum-13">CSSMathSum</a></code> object,
with its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathsum-values" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathsum-values-8">values</a></code> internal slot
set to its list of arguments</p>
       <dt data-md="">multiplication node
       <dd data-md="">
        <p>becomes a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathproduct" id="ref-for-cssmathproduct-8">CSSMathProduct</a></code> object,
with its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathproduct-values" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathproduct-values-5">values</a></code> internal slot
set to its list of arguments</p>
       <dt data-md="">negate node
       <dd data-md="">
        <p>becomes a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathnegate" id="ref-for-cssmathnegate-8">CSSMathNegate</a></code> object,
with its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathnegate-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathnegate-value-6">value</a></code> internal slot
set to its argument</p>
       <dt data-md="">invert node
       <dd data-md="">
        <p>becomes a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathinvert" id="ref-for-cssmathinvert-8">CSSMathInvert</a></code> object,
with its <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmathinvert-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssmathinvert-value-4">value</a></code> internal slot
set to its argument</p>
       <dt data-md="">leaf node
       <dd data-md="">
        <p>normalized as appropriate</p>
      </dl>
    </ol>
    <div class="example" id="example-3941d1a8">
     <a class="self-link" href="#example-3941d1a8"></a> For example, <span class="css">calc(1px - 2 * 3em)</span> produces the structure: 
<pre>CSSMathSum(
    CSS.px(1),
    CSSMathNegate(
        CSSMathProduct(
            2,
            CSS.em(3)
        )
    )
)
</pre>
    </div>
    <p class="note" role="note"><span>Note:</span> The value computation process may transform different units into identical ones,
    simplifying the resulting expression.
    For example, <span class="css">calc(1px + 2em)</span> as a specified value
    results in a <span style=";white-space:nowrap"><code>CSSMathSum(CSS.px(1), CSS.em(2))</code></span>,
    but as a computed value will give <span style=";white-space:nowrap"><code>CSS.px(33)</code></span> or similar
    (depending on the value of an <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#em">em</a> in that context).</p>
   </div>
   <h3 class="heading settled" data-level="5.5" id="transformvalue-normalization"><span class="secno">5.5. </span><span class="content"><a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#typedef-transform-list">&lt;transform-list></a> and <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#typedef-transform-function">&lt;transform-function></a> values</span><a class="self-link" href="#transformvalue-normalization"></a></h3>
   <p>CSS <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#typedef-transform-list">&lt;transform-list></a> values become <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csstransformvalue" id="ref-for-csstransformvalue-7">CSSTransformValue</a></code>s in the Typed OM,
while CSS <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#typedef-transform-function">&lt;transform-function></a> values become <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csstransformcomponent" id="ref-for-csstransformcomponent-11">CSSTransformComponent</a></code>s.</p>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="normalize a transform-list">
     To <dfn data-dfn-type="dfn" data-export="" id="normalize-a-transform-list">normalize a <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#typedef-transform-list">&lt;transform-list></a><a class="self-link" href="#normalize-a-transform-list"></a></dfn> <var>list</var>: 
    <ol>
     <li data-md="">
      <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csstransformvalue" id="ref-for-csstransformvalue-8">CSSTransformValue</a></code> whose <a data-link-type="dfn">values to iterate over</a> are the result of mapping the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#normalize-a-transform-function" id="ref-for-normalize-a-transform-function-1">normalize a &lt;transform-function></a> algorithm
over <var>list</var>.</p>
    </ol>
   </div>
   <div class="algorithm" data-algorithm="normalize a transform-function">
     To <dfn class="dfn-paneled" data-dfn-type="dfn" data-export="" id="normalize-a-transform-function">normalize a <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#typedef-transform-function">&lt;transform-function></a></dfn> <var>func</var>,
    perform the appropriate set of steps below,
    based on <var>func</var>: 
    <dl class="switch">
     <dt data-md=""><a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#funcdef-matrix">matrix()</a>
     <dt data-md=""><a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-transforms-2/#funcdef-matrix3d">matrix3d()</a>
     <dd data-md="">
      <ol>
       <li data-md="">
        <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmatrixcomponent" id="ref-for-cssmatrixcomponent-2">CSSMatrixComponent</a></code> object,
whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssmatrixcomponent-matrix" id="ref-for-dom-cssmatrixcomponent-matrix-2">matrix</a></code> internal slot
is set to a 4x4 matrix representing the same information
as <var>func</var>,
and whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d" id="ref-for-dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d-14">is2D</a></code> internal slot
is <code>true</code> if <var>func</var> is <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#funcdef-matrix">matrix()</a>,
and <code>false</code> otherwise.</p>
      </ol>
     <dt data-md=""><a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#funcdef-translate">translate()</a>
     <dt data-md=""><a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#funcdef-translatex">translateX()</a>
     <dt data-md=""><a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#funcdef-translatey">translateY()</a>
     <dt data-md=""><a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-transforms-2/#funcdef-translate3d">translate3d()</a>
     <dt data-md=""><a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-transforms-2/#funcdef-translatez">translateZ()</a>
     <dd data-md="">
      <ol>
       <li data-md="">
        <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csstranslation" id="ref-for-csstranslation-3">CSSTranslation</a></code> object,
whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstranslation-x" id="ref-for-dom-csstranslation-x-2">x</a></code>, <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstranslation-y" id="ref-for-dom-csstranslation-y-2">y</a></code>, and <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstranslation-z" id="ref-for-dom-csstranslation-z-4">z</a></code> internal slots
are set to the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#normalize-a-numeric-value" id="ref-for-normalize-a-numeric-value-2">normalization</a> of the specified x/y/z offsets,
or the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#normalize-a-numeric-value" id="ref-for-normalize-a-numeric-value-3">normalization</a> of <span class="css">0px</span> if not specified in <var>func</var>,
and whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d" id="ref-for-dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d-15">is2D</a></code> internal slot
is <code>true</code> if <var>func</var> is <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#funcdef-translate">translate()</a>, <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#funcdef-translatex">translateX()</a>, or <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#funcdef-translatey">translateY()</a>,
and <code>false</code> otherwise.</p>
      </ol>
     <dt data-md=""><a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#funcdef-scale">scale()</a>
     <dt data-md=""><a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#funcdef-scalex">scaleX()</a>
     <dt data-md=""><a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#funcdef-scaley">scaleY()</a>
     <dt data-md=""><a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-transforms-2/#funcdef-scale3d">scale3d()</a>
     <dt data-md=""><a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-transforms-2/#funcdef-scalez">scaleZ()</a>
     <dd data-md="">
      <ol>
       <li data-md="">
        <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssscale" id="ref-for-cssscale-2">CSSScale</a></code> object,
whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssscale-x" id="ref-for-dom-cssscale-x-2">x</a></code>, <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssscale-y" id="ref-for-dom-cssscale-y-2">y</a></code>, and <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssscale-z" id="ref-for-dom-cssscale-z-3">z</a></code> internal slots
are set to the specified x/y/z scales,
or to <span class="css">1</span> if not specified in <var>func</var> and whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d" id="ref-for-dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d-16">is2D</a></code> internal slot
is <code>true</code> if <var>func</var> is <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#funcdef-scale">scale()</a>, <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#funcdef-scalex">scaleX()</a>, or <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#funcdef-scaley">scaleY()</a>,
and <code>false</code> otherwise.</p>
      </ol>
     <dt data-md=""><a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#funcdef-rotate">rotate()</a>
     <dt data-md=""><a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-transforms-2/#funcdef-rotate3d">rotate3d()</a>
     <dt data-md=""><a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-transforms-2/#funcdef-rotatex">rotateX()</a>
     <dt data-md=""><a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-transforms-2/#funcdef-rotatey">rotateY()</a>
     <dt data-md=""><a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-transforms-2/#funcdef-rotatez">rotateZ()</a>
     <dd data-md="">
      <ol>
       <li data-md="">
        <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssrotation" id="ref-for-cssrotation-3">CSSRotation</a></code> object,
whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssrotation-angle" id="ref-for-dom-cssrotation-angle-3">angle</a></code> internal slot
is set to the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#normalize-a-numeric-value" id="ref-for-normalize-a-numeric-value-4">normalization</a> of the specified angle,
and whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssrotation-x" id="ref-for-dom-cssrotation-x-3">x</a></code>, <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssrotation-y" id="ref-for-dom-cssrotation-y-3">y</a></code>, and <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssrotation-z" id="ref-for-dom-cssrotation-z-3">z</a></code> internal slots
are set to the specified rotation axis coordinates,
or the implicit axis coordinates if not specified in <var>func</var> and whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d" id="ref-for-dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d-17">is2D</a></code> internal slot
is <code>true</code> if <var>func</var> is <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#funcdef-rotate">rotate()</a>,
and <code>false</code> otherwise.</p>
      </ol>
     <dt data-md=""><a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#funcdef-skew">skew()</a>
     <dt data-md=""><a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#funcdef-skewx">skewX()</a>
     <dt data-md=""><a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-transforms-1/#funcdef-skewy">skewY()</a>
     <dd data-md="">
      <ol>
       <li data-md="">
        <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssskew" id="ref-for-cssskew-3">CSSSkew</a></code> object,
whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssskew-ax" id="ref-for-dom-cssskew-ax-2">ax</a></code> and <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssskew-ay" id="ref-for-dom-cssskew-ay-2">ay</a></code> internal slots
are set to the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#normalize-a-numeric-value" id="ref-for-normalize-a-numeric-value-5">normalization</a> of the specified x and y angles,
or the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#normalize-a-numeric-value" id="ref-for-normalize-a-numeric-value-6">normalization</a> of <span class="css">0deg</span> if not specified in <var>func</var>,
and whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d" id="ref-for-dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d-18">is2D</a></code> internal slot
is <code>true</code>.</p>
      </ol>
     <dt data-md=""><a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-transforms-2/#funcdef-perspective">perspective()</a>
     <dd data-md="">
      <ol>
       <li data-md="">
        <p>Return a new <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssperspective" id="ref-for-cssperspective-3">CSSPerspective</a></code> object,
whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssperspective-length" id="ref-for-dom-cssperspective-length-2">length</a></code> internal slot
is set to the <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#normalize-a-numeric-value" id="ref-for-normalize-a-numeric-value-7">normalization</a> of the specified length
and whose <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d" id="ref-for-dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d-19">is2D</a></code> internal slot
is <code>false</code>.</p>
      </ol>
    </dl>
   </div>
   <h3 class="heading settled" data-level="5.6" id="positionvalue-normalization"><span class="secno">5.6. </span><span class="content"><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csspositionvalue" id="ref-for-csspositionvalue-6">CSSPositionValue</a></code> normalization</span><a class="self-link" href="#positionvalue-normalization"></a></h3>
   <p>If the provided value matches the <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#typedef-position">&lt;position></a> production, then a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csspositionvalue" id="ref-for-csspositionvalue-7">CSSPositionValue</a></code> is constructed
with <var>x</var> and <var>y</var> components determined via the following process. If this process, or
any sub-process referenced by this process fails, then normalization as a whole fails.</p>
   <ol>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>Initialize both <var>x</var> and <var>y</var> to a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-62">CSSNumericValue</a></code> value representing 50%.</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>If the provided value is a single keyword, length, percentage, or calc expression, then follow
    the procedure outlined in <a href="#from-single-keyword">§5.6.1 Determining x or y from a single value</a> with <var>value</var> given
    by the provided value and a horizontal <var>bias</var>.</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>Otherwise, if the provided value consists of a combination of two keywords, then:</p>
     <ol>
      <li data-md="">
       <p>follow the procedure outlined in <a href="#from-single-keyword">§5.6.1 Determining x or y from a single value</a> with <var>value</var> given by the
    first keyword and an auto <var>bias</var>.</p>
      <li data-md="">
       <p>if <var>bias</var> is horizontal, set it to vertical. Otherwise, set it to horizontal.</p>
      <li data-md="">
       <p>follow the procedure again with <var>value</var> given by the second keyword, using the existing <var>bias</var>.</p>
     </ol>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>Otherwise, if the provided value consists of a combination of two keywords, lengths, percentages, and
    calc expressions, then follow the procedure outlined in <a href="#from-single-keyword">§5.6.1 Determining x or y from a single value</a> with <var>value</var> given by the first part of the provided value and a horizontal <var>bias</var>, then follow the
    procedure again with <var>value</var> given by the second part of the provided value and a vertical <var>bias</var>.</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>Otherwise:</p>
     <ol>
      <li data-md="">
       <p>if the provided value starts with a keyword followed by a length, percentage, or calc expression, then follow
    the procedure outlined in <a href="#from-keyword-and-length">§5.6.2 Determining x or y from a keyword and a length</a> with <var>keyword</var> set to the
    keyword, <var>length</var> set to the length, percentage, or calc expression, and auto <var>bias</var>.</p>
      <li data-md="">
       <p>otherwise, follow the procedure outlined in <a href="#from-single-keyword">§5.6.1 Determining x or y from a single value</a> with <var>value</var> set to the first component of the provided value and an auto <var>bias</var>.</p>
      <li data-md="">
       <p>if <var>bias</var> is horizontal, set it to vertical. Otherwise, set it to horizontal.</p>
      <li data-md="">
       <p>if the remainder of the provided value is a single keyword, length, percentage or calc expression, follow
    the procedure outlined in <a href="#from-single-keyword">§5.6.1 Determining x or y from a single value</a> with <var>value</var> set to the keyword and the existing <var>bias</var>.</p>
      <li data-md="">
       <p>otherwise, if the remainder of the provided value consists of a keyword followed by a length, percentage or
    calc expression, follow the procedure outlined in <a href="#from-keyword-and-length">§5.6.2 Determining x or y from a keyword and a length</a> with <var>keyword</var> set to the keyword, <var>length</var> set to the length, percentage, or calc expression, and
    the existing <var>bias</var>.</p>
      <li data-md="">
       <p>Otherwise, the process fails.</p>
     </ol>
   </ol>
   <h4 class="heading settled" data-level="5.6.1" id="from-single-keyword"><span class="secno">5.6.1. </span><span class="content">Determining <var>x</var> or <var>y</var> from a single value</span><a class="self-link" href="#from-single-keyword"></a></h4>
   <p>The following process sets a value for either <var>x</var> or <var>y</var>, depending on an input <var>value</var> and <var>bias</var>. The process also updates <var>bias</var> based on the <var>value</var>.</p>
   <ol>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>If <var>value</var> is the keyword "left" and <var>bias</var> is not vertical, then set <var>x</var> to a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-63">CSSNumericValue</a></code> value representing 0% and <var>bias</var> to horizontal and exit this process.</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>If <var>value</var> is the keyword "right" and <var>bias</var> is not vertical, then set <var>x</var> to a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-64">CSSNumericValue</a></code> value representing 100% and <var>bias</var> to horizontal and exit this process.</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>If <var>value</var> is the keyword "top" and <var>bias</var> is not horizontal, then set <var>y</var> to a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-65">CSSNumericValue</a></code> value representing 0% and <var>bias</var> to vertical and exit this process.</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>If <var>value</var> is the keyword "bottom" and <var>bias</var> is not horizontal, then set <var>y</var> to a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-66">CSSNumericValue</a></code> value representing 100% and <var>bias</var> to vertical and exit this process.</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>If <var>value</var> matches the <a class="production css" data-link-type="type" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#typedef-length-percentage">&lt;length-percentage></a> production, then set <var>norm</var> to the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#normalize-a-numeric-value" id="ref-for-normalize-a-numeric-value-8">normalizing |value| as a numeric value</a>. If <var>bias</var> is vertical,
    set <var>y</var> to <var>norm</var>, otherwise set <var>x</var> to <var>norm</var> and <var>bias</var> to
    horizontal. Exit this process.</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>If <var>value</var> is not the keyword "center", then this process fails.</p>
   </ol>
   <h4 class="heading settled" data-level="5.6.2" id="from-keyword-and-length"><span class="secno">5.6.2. </span><span class="content">Determining <var>x</var> or <var>y</var> from a keyword and a length</span><a class="self-link" href="#from-keyword-and-length"></a></h4>
   <p>The following process sets a value for either <var>x</var> or<var>y</var>, depending on an input <var>keyword</var>, <var>length</var>, and <var>bias</var>. The process also updates <var>bias</var> based on the <var>keyword</var> and <var>length</var>.</p>
   <ol>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>follow the procedure outlined in <a href="#from-single-keyword">§5.6.1 Determining x or y from a single value</a> with <var>value</var> given by <var>keyword</var>, using the provided <var>bias</var></p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>let <var>adjustment</var> be the result of <a data-link-type="dfn" href="#normalize-a-numeric-value" id="ref-for-normalize-a-numeric-value-9">normalizing |length| as a numeric value</a>.</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>If the keyword is "right" or "bottom", let <var>adjustment</var> be the result of subtracting <var>adjustment</var> from a zero length.</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>amend <var>x</var> (if <var>bias</var> is horizontal) or <var>y</var> (if <var>bias</var> is vertical) by
    adding <var>adjustment</var> to it.</p>
   </ol>
   <h3 class="heading settled" data-level="5.7" id="resourcevalue-normalization"><span class="secno">5.7. </span><span class="content"><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssresourcevalue" id="ref-for-cssresourcevalue-8">CSSResourceValue</a></code> normalization</span><a class="self-link" href="#resourcevalue-normalization"></a></h3>
   <p>Resource references are normalized by determining whether the reference is invalid
(in which case <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssresourcevalue-state" id="ref-for-dom-cssresourcevalue-state-4">state</a></code> is set to <span class="css">error</span>) or
requires network data (in which case <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssresourcevalue-state" id="ref-for-dom-cssresourcevalue-state-5">state</a></code> is set to <span class="css">loading</span>). If data is not required and the reference is valid then <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssresourcevalue-state" id="ref-for-dom-cssresourcevalue-state-6">state</a></code> is set to <span class="css">loaded</span>.</p>
   <p>If <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssresourcevalue-state" id="ref-for-dom-cssresourcevalue-state-7">state</a></code> is set to <span class="css">loading</span> then the image
reference is reevaluated once the pending data becomes available, according to the
same rules referenced above.</p>
   <p>Normalization does not fail for <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssresourcevalue" id="ref-for-cssresourcevalue-9">CSSResourceValue</a></code> objects.</p>
   <div class="example" id="example-be708839"><a class="self-link" href="#example-be708839"></a> The string 'url(<span class="css">bike.png</span>)' is converted into a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssurlimagevalue" id="ref-for-cssurlimagevalue-2">CSSURLImageValue</a></code> with <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssresourcevalue-state" id="ref-for-dom-cssresourcevalue-state-8">state</a></code> set to <span class="css">unloaded</span> and the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssurlimagevalue-url" id="ref-for-dom-cssurlimagevalue-url-2">url</a></code> set to <span class="css">bike.png</span>. The <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssimagevalue-intrinsicwidth" id="ref-for-dom-cssimagevalue-intrinsicwidth-2">intrinsicWidth</a></code>, <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssimagevalue-intrinsicheight" id="ref-for-dom-cssimagevalue-intrinsicheight-2">intrinsicHeight</a></code> and <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssimagevalue-intrinsicratio" id="ref-for-dom-cssimagevalue-intrinsicratio-2">intrinsicRatio</a></code> are all set to null. </div>
   <h2 class="heading settled" data-level="6" id="stylevalue-serialization"><span class="secno">6. </span><span class="content"><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-34">CSSStyleValue</a></code> Serialization</span><a class="self-link" href="#stylevalue-serialization"></a></h2>
   <p>The way that a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-35">CSSStyleValue</a></code> serializes is dependent on how the value was constructed.</p>
   <dl>
    <dt data-md="">if the value was constructed from a DOMString
    <dd data-md="">
     <p>the serialization is the DOMString from which the value was constructed.</p>
    <dt data-md="">otherwise, if the value was constructed using an IDL constructor
    <dd data-md="">
     <p>the serialization is specified in the sections below.</p>
    <dt data-md="">otherwise, if the value was extracted from the CSSOM
    <dd data-md="">
     <p>the serialization matches the CSSOM serialization of the corresponding value.</p>
   </dl>
   <div class="example" id="example-6493830e">
    <a class="self-link" href="#example-6493830e"></a> 
    <p>For example:</p>
<pre class="lang-javascript highlight"><span class="kd">var</span> length1 <span class="o">=</span> CSSNumericValue<span class="p">.</span>from<span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">"42.0px"</span><span class="p">);</span>
length1<span class="p">.</span>toString<span class="p">();</span> <span class="c1">// "42.0px"</span>
<span class="c1"></span>
<span class="kd">var</span> length2 <span class="o">=</span> CSSNumericValue<span class="p">.</span>from<span class="p">(</span><span class="mf">42.0</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s2">"px"</span><span class="p">);</span>
length2<span class="p">.</span>toString<span class="p">();</span> <span class="c1">// "42px";</span>
<span class="c1"></span>
element<span class="p">.</span>style<span class="p">.</span>width <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s2">"42.0px"</span><span class="p">;</span>
<span class="kd">var</span> length3 <span class="o">=</span> element<span class="p">.</span>styleMap<span class="p">.</span>get<span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">'width'</span><span class="p">);</span>
length3<span class="p">.</span>toString<span class="p">();</span> <span class="c1">// "42px";</span>
</pre>
   </div>
   <h3 class="heading settled" data-level="6.1" id="unparsedvalue-serialization"><span class="secno">6.1. </span><span class="content"><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunparsedvalue" id="ref-for-cssunparsedvalue-11">CSSUnparsedValue</a></code> Serialization</span><a class="self-link" href="#unparsedvalue-serialization"></a></h3>
   <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunparsedvalue" id="ref-for-cssunparsedvalue-12">CSSUnparsedValue</a></code> objects are serialized by first serializing each <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssvariablereferencevalue" id="ref-for-cssvariablereferencevalue-11">CSSVariableReferenceValue</a></code>, then concatenating the contained DOMStrings and <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssvariablereferencevalue" id="ref-for-cssvariablereferencevalue-12">CSSVariableReferenceValue</a></code> serializations in order.</p>
   <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssvariablereferencevalue" id="ref-for-cssvariablereferencevalue-13">CSSVariableReferenceValue</a></code> objects are serialized by the following process:</p>
   <ol>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>the fallback <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunparsedvalue" id="ref-for-cssunparsedvalue-13">CSSUnparsedValue</a></code> is serialized</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>if the fallback serialization is the empty string, then the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssvariablereferencevalue" id="ref-for-cssvariablereferencevalue-14">CSSVariableReferenceValue</a></code> serializes as "var(" + variable + ")"</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>otherwise, the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssvariablereferencevalue" id="ref-for-cssvariablereferencevalue-15">CSSVariableReferenceValue</a></code> serializes as
"var(" + variable + "," + fallback serialization + ")"</p>
   </ol>
   <h3 class="heading settled" data-level="6.2" id="keywordvalue-serialization"><span class="secno">6.2. </span><span class="content"><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csskeywordvalue" id="ref-for-csskeywordvalue-12">CSSKeywordValue</a></code> Serialization</span><a class="self-link" href="#keywordvalue-serialization"></a></h3>
   <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csskeywordvalue" id="ref-for-csskeywordvalue-13">CSSKeywordValue</a></code> objects are serialized to their contained <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csskeywordvalue-value" id="ref-for-dom-csskeywordvalue-value-5">value</a></code> attribute.</p>
   <h3 class="heading settled" data-level="6.3" id="numericvalue-serialization"><span class="secno">6.3. </span><span class="content"><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-65">CSSUnitValue</a></code> Serialization</span><a class="self-link" href="#numericvalue-serialization"></a></h3>
   <p>If their <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-unit" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-unit-24">unit</a></code> is "number", <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-66">CSSUnitValue</a></code> objects are serialized
to the string representation of their <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-value-19">value</a></code>.</p>
   <p>Otherwise, if their <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-unit" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-unit-25">unit</a></code> is "percent", <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-67">CSSUnitValue</a></code> objects are serialized
to the string representation of their <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-value-20">value</a></code> followed by the character U+0025 PERCENTAGE SIGN (%).</p>
   <p>Otherwise, <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-68">CSSUnitValue</a></code> objects are serialized
to the string representation of their <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-value" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-value-21">value</a></code> followed by their <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssunitvalue-unit" id="ref-for-dom-cssunitvalue-unit-26">unit</a></code>.</p>
   <h3 class="heading settled" data-level="6.4" id="calc-serialization"><span class="secno">6.4. </span><span class="content"><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathvalue" id="ref-for-cssmathvalue-12">CSSMathValue</a></code> Serialization</span><a class="self-link" href="#calc-serialization"></a></h3>
   <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathvalue" id="ref-for-cssmathvalue-13">CSSMathValue</a></code> objects are serialized into a <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://drafts.csswg.org/css-values-4/#funcdef-calc">calc()</a> expression</p>
   <p class="issue" id="issue-b7b1e314"><a class="self-link" href="#issue-b7b1e314"></a> TODO</p>
   <h3 class="heading settled" data-level="6.5" id="transformvalue-serialization"><span class="secno">6.5. </span><span class="content"><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csstransformvalue" id="ref-for-csstransformvalue-9">CSSTransformValue</a></code> Serialization</span><a class="self-link" href="#transformvalue-serialization"></a></h3>
   <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csstransformvalue" id="ref-for-csstransformvalue-10">CSSTransformValue</a></code> objects are serialized by generating a space-separated list
of serializations of the contained <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csstransformcomponent" id="ref-for-csstransformcomponent-12">CSSTransformComponent</a></code> objects.</p>
   <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csstransformcomponent" id="ref-for-csstransformcomponent-13">CSSTransformComponent</a></code> objects are serialized according to the following rules:</p>
   <ul>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>For all objects except <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmatrixcomponent" id="ref-for-cssmatrixcomponent-3">CSSMatrixComponent</a></code> objects, the serialization
is defined by the object constructors.</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>When there are multiple constructors for a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmatrixcomponent" id="ref-for-cssmatrixcomponent-4">CSSMatrixComponent</a></code> object, then
if the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d" id="ref-for-dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d-20">is2D</a></code> attribute is set to true,
then the relevant constructor is the constructor with fewer arguments; otherwise
the relevant constructor is the constructor with more arguments.</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>Each serialization is represented by a function</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>The function’s name is a lowercase version of the component object type,
without the CSS prefix</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>The function’s arguments are a comma-separated list that matches the
arguments to the relevant constructor. The values of the arguments are given
by the attributes contained in the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csstransformcomponent" id="ref-for-csstransformcomponent-14">CSSTransformComponent</a></code>.</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-67">CSSNumericValue</a></code> attributes serialize using the rules above.
Doubles serialize to their string representation.</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmatrixcomponent" id="ref-for-cssmatrixcomponent-5">CSSMatrixComponent</a></code> objects serialize to a list of 6 components if <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d" id="ref-for-dom-csstransformcomponent-is2d-21">is2D</a></code> is set, or 12 components otherwise.
Component order and format is given by <a data-link-type="biblio" href="#biblio-css-transforms-1">[CSS-TRANSFORMS-1]</a>.</p>
   </ul>
   <h3 class="heading settled" data-level="6.6" id="positionvalue-serialization"><span class="secno">6.6. </span><span class="content"><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csspositionvalue" id="ref-for-csspositionvalue-8">CSSPositionValue</a></code> Serialization</span><a class="self-link" href="#positionvalue-serialization"></a></h3>
   <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csspositionvalue" id="ref-for-csspositionvalue-9">CSSPositionValue</a></code> objects are serialized by:</p>
   <ul>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>serializing the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csspositionvalue-x" id="ref-for-dom-csspositionvalue-x-6">x</a></code> attribute according to
the rules for <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-68">CSSNumericValue</a></code> objects above.</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>serializing the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csspositionvalue-y" id="ref-for-dom-csspositionvalue-y-6">y</a></code> attribute according to
the rules for <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-69">CSSNumericValue</a></code> objects above.</p>
    <li data-md="">
     <p>returning the concatenation of the two serializations (x before y), separated
by a space.</p>
   </ul>
   <h3 class="heading settled" data-level="6.7" id="urlimagevalue-serialization"><span class="secno">6.7. </span><span class="content"><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssurlimagevalue" id="ref-for-cssurlimagevalue-3">CSSURLImageValue</a></code> Serialization</span><a class="self-link" href="#urlimagevalue-serialization"></a></h3>
   <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssurlimagevalue" id="ref-for-cssurlimagevalue-4">CSSURLImageValue</a></code> objects are serialized to the string given by
"url(" + <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssurlimagevalue-url" id="ref-for-dom-cssurlimagevalue-url-3">url</a></code> + ")".</p>
   <h3 class="heading settled" data-level="6.8" id="fontfacevalue-serialization"><span class="secno">6.8. </span><span class="content"><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssfontfacevalue" id="ref-for-cssfontfacevalue-4">CSSFontFaceValue</a></code> Serialization</span><a class="self-link" href="#fontfacevalue-serialization"></a></h3>
   <p><code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssfontfacevalue" id="ref-for-cssfontfacevalue-5">CSSFontFaceValue</a></code> objects are serialized to the value of their contained <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-cssfontfacevalue-fontfamilyname" id="ref-for-dom-cssfontfacevalue-fontfamilyname-1">fontFamilyName</a></code>.</p>
   <h2 class="heading settled" data-level="7" id="security-considerations"><span class="secno">7. </span><span class="content">Security Considerations</span><a class="self-link" href="#security-considerations"></a></h2>
   <p>There are no known security issues introduced by these features.</p>
   <h2 class="heading settled" data-level="8" id="privacy-considerations"><span class="secno">8. </span><span class="content">Privacy Considerations</span><a class="self-link" href="#privacy-considerations"></a></h2>
   <p>There are no known privacy issues introduced by these features.</p>
   <h2 class="heading settled" id="computed-stylevalue-objects"><span class="content">Appendix A: Computed <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-36">CSSStyleValue</a></code> objects</span><a class="self-link" href="#computed-stylevalue-objects"></a></h2>
   <p>This appendix describes the restrictions on <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-37">CSSStyleValue</a></code> objects that
appear as computed values (i.e. as a value stored on computed <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#stylepropertymapreadonly" id="ref-for-stylepropertymapreadonly-5">StylePropertyMapReadOnly</a></code> objects).</p>
   <h3 class="heading settled" id="computed-unparsedvalue-objects"><span class="content">Computed <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunparsedvalue" id="ref-for-cssunparsedvalue-14">CSSUnparsedValue</a></code> objects</span><a class="self-link" href="#computed-unparsedvalue-objects"></a></h3>
   <p>A property with a declared <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunparsedvalue" id="ref-for-cssunparsedvalue-15">CSSUnparsedValue</a></code> value will not
compute to a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunparsedvalue" id="ref-for-cssunparsedvalue-16">CSSUnparsedValue</a></code>. Instead, after custom property references
are resolved, the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-38">CSSStyleValue</a></code> subclass appropriate to the property will be
used.</p>
   <div class="example" id="example-dadcf498">
    <a class="self-link" href="#example-dadcf498"></a> For example, a style rule containing: 
<pre class="style">width: calc(var(--foo) + 10%);
</pre>
    <p>Will represent a declared width as an <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunparsedvalue" id="ref-for-cssunparsedvalue-17">CSSUnparsedValue</a></code>, but if this value
is the winning value during computation for a given element then that element’s
computed width will be represented by a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-70">CSSNumericValue</a></code> object (assuming
that --foo resolves to a valid substitution).</p>
   </div>
   <p>Often there will be no <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-39">CSSStyleValue</a></code> subclass appropriate - for example when a custom property
contains a reference to another custom property. In these cases, a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-40">CSSStyleValue</a></code> is used directly to represent a value of unknown type.</p>
   <div class="example" id="example-c4465609">
    <a class="self-link" href="#example-c4465609"></a> 
    <p>For example, a style rule containing:</p>
<pre class="style">--foo: var(--bar) black;
</pre>
    <p>Will represent a declared value for --foo as a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunparsedvalue" id="ref-for-cssunparsedvalue-18">CSSUnparsedValue</a></code>, and if
this value is the winning declaration for --foo during computation for a given
element, then that element’s will have a computed value for --foo that is
represented by a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssstylevalue" id="ref-for-cssstylevalue-41">CSSStyleValue</a></code>.</p>
   </div>
   <h3 class="heading settled" id="computed-keywordvalue-objects"><span class="content">Computed <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csskeywordvalue" id="ref-for-csskeywordvalue-14">CSSKeywordValue</a></code> objects</span><a class="self-link" href="#computed-keywordvalue-objects"></a></h3>
   <p>During computation, <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csskeywordvalue" id="ref-for-csskeywordvalue-15">CSSKeywordValue</a></code> objects are either as specified (e.g. <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-positioning/#valdef-top-auto">auto</a> values for lengths that participate in layout) or resolved to a relevant value
and renormalized (e.g. the color <a class="css" data-link-type="maybe" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-color-4/#valdef-color-red">red</a>).</p>
   <h3 class="heading settled" id="computed-numericvalue-objects"><span class="content">Computed <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-69">CSSUnitValue</a></code> objects</span><a class="self-link" href="#computed-numericvalue-objects"></a></h3>
   <p>During computation, <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssunitvalue" id="ref-for-cssunitvalue-70">CSSUnitValue</a></code> objects
are range-restricted or rounded as appropriate to the relevant property,
but otherwise as specified.</p>
   <h3 class="heading settled" id="computed-calc-objects"><span class="content">Computed <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathvalue" id="ref-for-cssmathvalue-14">CSSMathValue</a></code> objects</span><a class="self-link" href="#computed-calc-objects"></a></h3>
   <p>During computation, <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssmathvalue" id="ref-for-cssmathvalue-15">CSSMathValue</a></code> objects are reduced accordingly:</p>
   <p class="issue" id="issue-b7b1e3140"><a class="self-link" href="#issue-b7b1e3140"></a> TODO</p>
   <h3 class="heading settled" id="computed-transformvalue-objects"><span class="content">Computed <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csstransformvalue" id="ref-for-csstransformvalue-11">CSSTransformValue</a></code> objects</span><a class="self-link" href="#computed-transformvalue-objects"></a></h3>
   <p>During computation, any <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssnumericvalue" id="ref-for-cssnumericvalue-71">CSSNumericValue</a></code> objects referenced by a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csstransformcomponent" id="ref-for-csstransformcomponent-15">CSSTransformComponent</a></code> (e.g. the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csstranslation-x" id="ref-for-dom-csstranslation-x-3">x</a></code> attribute of a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csstranslation" id="ref-for-csstranslation-4">CSSTranslation</a></code>) are
computed according to <a href="#computed-numericvalue-objects">Computed CSSUnitValue objects</a>, but the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csstransformvalue" id="ref-for-csstransformvalue-12">CSSTransformValue</a></code> object is otherwise as specified.</p>
   <h3 class="heading settled" id="computed-positionvalue-objects"><span class="content">Computed <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csspositionvalue" id="ref-for-csspositionvalue-10">CSSPositionValue</a></code> objects</span><a class="self-link" href="#computed-positionvalue-objects"></a></h3>
   <p>During computation, both the <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csspositionvalue-x" id="ref-for-dom-csspositionvalue-x-7">x</a></code> and <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#dom-csspositionvalue-y" id="ref-for-dom-csspositionvalue-y-7">y</a></code> components of a <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#csspositionvalue" id="ref-for-csspositionvalue-11">CSSPositionValue</a></code> are
computed according to <a href="#computed-numericvalue-objects">Computed CSSUnitValue objects</a>.</p>
   <h3 class="heading settled" id="computed-imagevalue-objects"><span class="content">Computed <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssimagevalue" id="ref-for-cssimagevalue-7">CSSImageValue</a></code> objects</span><a class="self-link" href="#computed-imagevalue-objects"></a></h3>
   <p>Computed <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssimagevalue" id="ref-for-cssimagevalue-8">CSSImageValue</a></code> objects are as specified.</p>
   <h3 class="heading settled" id="computed-fontfacevalue-objects"><span class="content">Computed <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssfontfacevalue" id="ref-for-cssfontfacevalue-6">CSSFontFaceValue</a></code> objects</span><a class="self-link" href="#computed-fontfacevalue-objects"></a></h3>
   <p>Computed <code class="idl"><a data-link-type="idl" href="#cssfontfacevalue" id="ref-for-cssfontfacevalue-7">CSSFontFaceValue</a></code> objects are as specified.</p>
  </main>
  <h2 class="no-ref no-num heading settled" id="conformance"><span class="content"> Conformance</span><a class="self-link" href="#conformance"></a></h2>
  <h3 class="no-ref heading settled" id="conventions"><span class="content"> Document conventions</span><a class="self-link" href="#conventions"></a></h3>
  <p>Conformance requirements are expressed with a combination of
    descriptive assertions and RFC 2119 terminology. The key words “MUST”,
    “MUST NOT”, “REQUIRED”, “SHALL”, “SHALL NOT”, “SHOULD”, “SHOULD NOT”,
    “RECOMMENDED”, “MAY”, and “OPTIONAL” in the normative parts of this
    document are to be interpreted as described in RFC 2119.
    However, for readability, these words do not appear in all uppercase
    letters in this specification. </p>
  <p>All of the text of this specification is normative except sections
    explicitly marked as non-normative, examples, and notes. <a data-link-type="biblio" href="#biblio-rfc2119">[RFC2119]</a></p>
  <p>Examples in this specification are introduced with the words “for example”
    or are set apart from the normative text with <code>class="example"</code>,
    like this: </p>
  <div class="example" id="example-f839f6c8">
   <a class="self-link" href="#example-f839f6c8"></a> 
   <p>This is an example of an informative example.</p>
  </div>
  <p>Informative notes begin with the word “Note” and are set apart from the
    normative text with <code>class="note"</code>, like this: </p>
  <p class="note" role="note">Note, this is an informative note.</p>
  <p>Advisements are normative sections styled to evoke special attention and are
    set apart from other normative text with <code>&lt;strong class="advisement"></code>, like
    this: <strong class="advisement"> UAs MUST provide an accessible alternative. </strong> </p>
  <h3 class="no-ref heading settled" id="conformance-classes"><span class="content"> Conformance classes</span><a class="self-link" href="#conformance-classes"></a></h3>
  <p>Conformance to this specification
    is defined for three conformance classes: </p>
  <dl>
   <dt>style sheet 
   <dd>A <a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/CSS21/conform.html#style-sheet">CSS
            style sheet</a>. 
   <dt>renderer 
   <dd>A <a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/CSS21/conform.html#user-agent">UA</a> that interprets the semantics of a style sheet and renders
            documents that use them. 
   <dt>authoring tool 
   <dd>A <a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/CSS21/conform.html#user-agent">UA</a> that writes a style sheet. 
  </dl>
  <p>A style sheet is conformant to this specification
    if all of its statements that use syntax defined in this module are valid
    according to the generic CSS grammar and the individual grammars of each
    feature defined in this module. </p>
  <p>A renderer is conformant to this specification
    if, in addition to interpreting the style sheet as defined by the
    appropriate specifications, it supports all the features defined
    by this specification by parsing them correctly
    and rendering the document accordingly. However, the inability of a
    UA to correctly render a document due to limitations of the device
    does not make the UA non-conformant. (For example, a UA is not
    required to render color on a monochrome monitor.) </p>
  <p>An authoring tool is conformant to this specification
    if it writes style sheets that are syntactically correct according to the
    generic CSS grammar and the individual grammars of each feature in
    this module, and meet all other conformance requirements of style sheets
    as described in this module. </p>
  <h3 class="no-ref heading settled" id="partial"><span class="content"> Partial implementations</span><a class="self-link" href="#partial"></a></h3>
  <p>So that authors can exploit the forward-compatible parsing rules to
    assign fallback values, CSS renderers <strong>must</strong> treat as invalid (and <a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/CSS21/conform.html#ignore">ignore
    as appropriate</a>) any at-rules, properties, property values, keywords,
    and other syntactic constructs for which they have no usable level of
    support. In particular, user agents <strong>must not</strong> selectively
    ignore unsupported component values and honor supported values in a single
    multi-value property declaration: if any value is considered invalid
    (as unsupported values must be), CSS requires that the entire declaration
    be ignored.</p>
  <h4 class="heading settled" id="conform-future-proofing"><span class="content"> Implementations of Unstable and Proprietary Features</span><a class="self-link" href="#conform-future-proofing"></a></h4>
  <p>To avoid clashes with future stable CSS features,
        the CSSWG recommends <a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/CSS/#future-proofing">following best practices</a> for the implementation of <a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/CSS/#unstable">unstable</a> features and <a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/CSS/#proprietary-extension">proprietary extensions</a> to CSS. </p>
  <h3 class="no-ref heading settled" id="testing"><span class="content"> Non-experimental implementations</span><a class="self-link" href="#testing"></a></h3>
  <p>Once a specification reaches the Candidate Recommendation stage,
    non-experimental implementations are possible, and implementors should
    release an unprefixed implementation of any CR-level feature they
    can demonstrate to be correctly implemented according to spec. </p>
  <p>To establish and maintain the interoperability of CSS across
    implementations, the CSS Working Group requests that non-experimental
    CSS renderers submit an implementation report (and, if necessary, the
    testcases used for that implementation report) to the W3C before
    releasing an unprefixed implementation of any CSS features. Testcases
    submitted to W3C are subject to review and correction by the CSS
    Working Group. </p>
  <p>
   Further information on submitting testcases and implementation reports
    can be found from on the CSS Working Group’s website at <a href="https://www.w3.org/Style/CSS/Test/">https://www.w3.org/Style/CSS/Test/</a>.
    Questions should be directed to the <a href="https://lists.w3.org/Archives/Public/public-css-testsuite">public-css-testsuite@w3.org</a> mailing list. 
<script src="https://www.w3.org/scripts/TR/2016/fixup.js"></script>
  </p>

  <aside class="dfn-panel" data-for="normalize-a-transform-function">
   <b><a href="#normalize-a-transform-function">#normalize-a-transform-function</a></b><b>Referenced in:</b>
   <ul>
    <li><a href="#ref-for-normalize-a-transform-function-1">5.5. &lt;transform-list> and &lt;transform-function> values</a>

<script>/* script-dfn-panel */

        document.body.addEventListener("click", function(e) {
            var queryAll = function(sel) { return [].slice.call(document.querySelectorAll(sel)); }
            // Find the dfn element or panel, if any, that was clicked on.
            var el = e.target;
            var target;
            var hitALink = false;
            while(el.parentElement) {
                if(el.tagName == "A") {
                    // Clicking on a link in a <dfn> shouldn't summon the panel
                    hitALink = true;
                }
                if(el.classList.contains("dfn-paneled")) {
                    target = "dfn";
                    break;
                }
                if(el.classList.contains("dfn-panel")) {
                    target = "dfn-panel";
                    break;
                }
                el = el.parentElement;
            }
            if(target != "dfn-panel") {
                // Turn off any currently "on" or "activated" panels.
                queryAll(".dfn-panel.on, .dfn-panel.activated").forEach(function(el){
                    el.classList.remove("on");
                    el.classList.remove("activated");
                });
            }
            if(target == "dfn" && !hitALink) {
                // open the panel
                var dfnPanel = document.querySelector(".dfn-panel[data-for='" + el.id + "']");
                if(dfnPanel) {
                    console.log(dfnPanel);
                    dfnPanel.classList.add("on");
                    var rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();
                    dfnPanel.style.left = window.scrollX + rect.right + 5 + "px";
                    dfnPanel.style.top = window.scrollY + rect.top + "px";
                    var panelRect = dfnPanel.getBoundingClientRect();
                    var panelWidth = panelRect.right - panelRect.left;
                    if(panelRect.right > document.body.scrollWidth && (rect.left - (panelWidth + 5)) > 0) {
                        // Reposition, because the panel is overflowing
                        dfnPanel.style.left = window.scrollX + rect.left - (panelWidth + 5) + "px";
                    }
                } else {
                    console.log("Couldn't find .dfn-panel[data-for='" + el.id + "']");
                }
            } else if(target == "dfn-panel") {
                // Switch it to "activated" state, which pins it.
                el.classList.add("activated");
                el.style.left = null;
                el.style.top = null;
            }

        });
        </script>
